Abhidharmasamuccaya chos mngon pa kun las btus pa bzhugs so /
namo buddhāya /
[atha mūlavastuni tridharmaparicchedaḥ prathamaḥ /
tridharmaḥ saṃgrahaḥ saṃprayogo 'nvayaśca lakṣaṇe /
viniścaye satyadharmau prāptiḥ sāṃkathyameva ca /
kati kasmādupādānaṃ vyavasthānaṃ ca lakṣaṇam 		/
rgya gar skad du /
aa bhi dha rma sa mu tstsha ya /
bod skad du /
chos mngon pa kun las btus pa /
bam po dang po /
'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo /
sdom ni /
du dang ci phyir nyer len dang /
mtshan nyid de yi rnam gzhag dang; /
go rims don dang dpe dbye dang /
bsdus la sogs pa rnam pa bzhi /
bsdus dang mtshungs ldan ldan pa dang /
rnam par nges pa bzhir dbye ste /
bden dang chos 'thob 'brel gtam ni /
rnam par nges pa'i dbye ba ste /
anukamārthadṛṣṭāntabhedā jñeyāḥ samuccaye kun las btus pa'i spyi sdom yin /
phung po rnams ni du /
skandhā dhātava āyatanāni ca kati khams rnams ni du /
skye mched rnams ni du zhe na /
skandhāḥ pañca phung po rnams ni lnga ste /
rūpaskandho vedanāskandhaḥ saṃjñāskandhaḥ saṃskāraskandho vijñānaskandhaśca gzugs kyi phung po dang tshor ba'i phung po dang 'du shes kyi phung po dang 'du byed kyi phung po dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po'o /
dhātavo 'ṣṭādaśa /
cakṣurdhātū rūpadhātuścakṣurvijñānadhātuḥ śrotradhātuḥ śabdadhātuḥ śrotravijñānadhāturghrāṇadhāturgandhadhāturghrāṇavijñānadhāturjivhādhātū rasadhāturjivhāvijñānadhātuḥ kāyadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyadhātuḥ kāyavijñānadhāturmanodhāturdharmadhāturmanovijñānadhātuśca 		khams rnams ni bcva brgyad de /
mig gi khams dang gzugs kyi khams dang mig gi rnams par shes pa'i khams dang rna ba'i khams dang sgra'i khams dang rna ba'i rnams par shes pa'i khams dang sna'i khams dang dri'i khams dang sna'i rnam par shes pa'i khams dang lce'i khams dang ro'i khams dang lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams dang lus kyi khams dang reg bya'i khams dang lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang yid kyi khams dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
āyatanāni dvadaśa /
cakṣurāyatanaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ śrotrāyatanaṃ śabdāyatanaṃ ghrāṇāyatanaṃ gandhāyatanaṃ jivhāyatanaṃ rasāyatanaṃ kāyāyatanaṃ spraṣṭavyāyatanaṃ manaāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanaṃ ca /
kimupādāya skandhāḥ pañcaiva 		skye mched rnams ni bcu gnyis te /
mig gi skye mched dang gzugs kyi skye mched dang rna ba'i skye mched dang sgra'i skye mched dang sna'i skye mched dang dri'i skye mched dang lce'i skye mched dang ro'i skye mched dang lus kyi skye mched dang reg bya'i skye mched dang yid kyi skye mched dang chos kyi skye mched do /
ci'i phyir phung po rnams lnga kho na zhe na /
paṃcākārātmavastūdbhāvanatāmupādāya bdag gi gzhi rnam pa lnga brjod pa'i phyir te /
saparigrahadehātmavastu upabhogātmavastu abhilāpātmavastu sarvadharmādharmābhisaṃskārātmavastu tadāśrayātmasvastu copādāya /
kimupādāya dhātovo 'ṣṭādaśaiva 		bdag gi gzhi lus yongs su gzung ba dang bcas pa brjod pa dang bdag gi gzhi longs spyod brjod pa dang bdag gi gzhi tha snyad brjod pa dang bdag gi gzhi chos dang chos ma yin pa mngon par 'du byed pa brjod pa dang bdag gi gzhi de dag gi gnas brjod pa'i phyir ro /
ci'i phyir khams rnams bcva brgyad kho na zhe na /
dvābhyāṃ dehaparigrahābhyāmatītavarttamānaṣaḍākāropabhogadhāraṇatāmupādāya /
kimupādāyāyatanāni dvādaśaiva 		lus dang yongs su gzung ba gnyis kyis /
'das pa dang da ltar gyi nye bar spyod pa rnam pa drug 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
ci'i phyir skye mched rnams bcu gnyis kho na zhe na /
dvābhyāṃ dehaparigrahābhyāmanāgataṣaḍākāropabhogāyadvāratāmupādāya lus dang yongs su gzung ba gnyis nyid /
ma 'ongs pa'i nye bar spyod pa rnam pa drug skye ba'i sgo'i phyir ro /
kasmāt skandhā upādānamityucyante ci'i phyir nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams zhes bya zhe na /
upādānena sahitatvāt skandhā upādānami tyucyante nye bar len pa dang ldan pas de'i phyir nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams zhes bya'o /
upādānaṃ katamat nye bar len pa gang zhe na /
skandheṣu cchando rāgaśca 'dir 'dun pa dang 'dod chags gang yin pa'o /
kasmāt /
ḥcchando rāgaścopādānamityucyate 		ci'i phyir 'dun pa dang 'dod chags nyid nye bar len pa zhes bya zhe na /
anāgatavarttamānaskandhānāmabhinirvarttanato 'parihārataśca /
anāgate 'bhilāṣād varttamāne 'dhāvasānācca cchando rāgaścopādānamityucyate 		ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi phung po mngon par 'grub pa dang yongs su mi gtong ba'i phyir te /
ma 'ongs pa la 'dod pa dang da ltar la lhag par chags pa'i phyir ro /
kasmād dhātava āyatanāni ca sopādānadharmā ityucyante /
tatra skandhavannirddeśaḥ 		ci'i phyir khams rnams dang skye mched rnams nye bar len pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams zhes bya zhe na /
de la phung po bzhin du bshad do /
kiṃlakṣaṇaṃ rūpam /
rūpaṇa lakṣaṇaṃ rūpam /
tad dvividham 		gzugs kyi phung po'i mtshan nyid ci zhe na /
gzugs su yod pa rnam pa gnyis kyis gzugs su yod pa'i mtshan nyid de /
sparśena rūpaṇaṃ pradeśena rūpaṇaṃ ca reg pas gzugs su yod pa dang yul dpyad pas gzugs su yod pa'o /
sparśena rūpaṇaṃ katamat reg pas gzugs su yod pa gang zhe na /
karacaraṇapāṣāṇaśasradaṇḍaśītoṣṇakṣutpipāsāmaśakadaṃśasarpavṛścikādīnāṃ sparśena vyābādhanam /
pradeśena rūpaṇaṃ katamat /
deśena rūpaṇa midaṃ cedaṃ ca rūpamevaṃ caivaṃ ca rūpamiti praṇihitāpraṇihitacetovitarkeṇa pratibimbacitrīkāratā 		lag pa'i 'dus te reg pas reg na gzugs su rung ba dang bong ba'i 'dus te reg pa dang dbyig pa'i 'dus re reg pa dang mtshon cha'i 'dus re reg pa dang grang ba dang tsha ba dang bkres pa dang skom pa dang sprang bu dang sha sprang dang rlung dang nyi ma dang sdig sprul gyi 'dus te reg pas reg na gzugs su rung ba'o /
yul dpyad pas gzugs su yod pa gang zhe na /
gang yul la gzugs 'di dang 'di'o /
gzugs 'di lta bu dang 'di lta bu'o zhes mnyam par gzhag pa'am /
mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i yid rtog pa dang mtshungs par ldan pas bkra bar 'dzin pa'o /
kiṃlakṣaṇā vedanā tshor ba'i mtshan nyid ci zhe na /
anubhavalakṣaṇā vedanā myong ba'i mtshan nyid de /
nānāvidhānāṃ śubhaśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalavipākaṃ pratyanubhavantyanenetyanubhavaḥ myongs ba'i ngo bo gang gis dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa so sor myong ba'o /
kiṃlakṣaṇā saṃjñā 'du shes kyi mtshan nyid ci zhe na /
saṃjānanālakṣaṇā saṃjñā 'dus te shes par byed pa'i mtshan nyid de /
saṃjñā nānādharmapratibimbodgrahaṇa svabhāvā yayā draṣṭaśrutamatavijñātānarthān vyavaharati mtshan mar 'dzin pa dang bkra bar 'dzin pa'i ngo bo gang gis ji ltar mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i don rnams la tha snyad 'dogs pa'o /
kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ 'du byed rnams kyi mtshan nyid ci zhe na /
abhisaṃskāralakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ mngon par 'du byed pa'i mtshan nyid de /
saṃskārabhisaṃskāra svabhāvo yena kuśalākuśalāvyakṛteṣu pakṣeṣu cittaṃ prerayati sems kyi mngon par 'du byed pa'i ngo bo gang gis dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang gnas skabs sna tshogs rnams su sems 'jug par byed pa'o /
kiṃlakṣaṇaṃ vijñānam rnam par shes pa'i mtshan nyid ci zhe na /
vijānanālakṣaṇaṃ vijñānam rnam par shes par byed pa'i mtshan nyid de /
vijñānaṃ yena rūpaśabdagandharasasparśadharmān nānā viṣayān vijānāti /
cakṣurdhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ 		rnam par shes par byed pa'i ngo bo gang gis /
gzugs rnams kyang rnam par shes pa dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos rnams kyang rnam par shes pa'o /
mig gi khams kyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
yena cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭavān paśyati yacca tasya bījamupacitamālayavijñānaṃ taccakṣuḥ /
yathā cakṣurdhātulakṣaṇaṃ tathā śrotraghrāṇajihyakāyamanodhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni 		mig gang gis gzugs rnams mthong bar gyur pa dang lta ba dang de'i sa bon bsags pa dang rnam par smin pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gang yin pa de mig gi khams kyi mtshan nyid do /
mig gi khams kyi mtshan nyid ci lta ba bzhin du /
rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi khams kyi mtshan nyid kyang de bzhin no /
rūpadhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ /
rūpaṃ yaccakṣuṣā dṛṣṭaṃ dṛśyate ca yacca tatra cakṣurdhātorādhipatyaṃ tadrūpadhātu lakṣaṇam /
yathā rūpadhātu lakṣaṇaṃ tathā śabdagandharasasparśadharmadhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni 		gzugs kyi khams kyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
mig gang gis gzugs gang dag mthong bar gyur pa dang mthong ba rnams dang de la mig gi khams dbang byed pa nyid gang yin pa de gzugs kyi khams kyi mtshan nyid do /
gzugs kyi khams kyi mtshan nyid ji lta ba bzhin du /
sgra dang ro dang reg bya dang chos kyi khams kyi mtshan nyid kyang de bzhin no /
cakṣūrvijñānadhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
cakṣurāśrayā rūpālambanā rūpaprativijñaptiḥ yacca tasya bījamupacitaṃ /
vipākālayavijñānaṃ taccakṣurvijñānadhātulakṣaṇam 		rten mig dang dmigs pa gzugs kyis /
gzugs su snang ba'i rnam par rig pa gang yin pa dang de'i sa bon bsags pa dang rnam par smin pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gang yin pa de /
mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid do /
yathā cakṣurvijñānadhātulakṣaṇaṃ tathā śrotraghrāṇajivhākāyamanovijñānadhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid ji lta ba bzhin du /
rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid kyang de bzhin no /
āyatanaṃ kiṃlakṣaṇam skye mched kyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
dhātuvad yathāyogaṃ veditavyam /
rūpaskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat /
yatkiṃcidrūpaṃ sarvaṃ taccatvāri mahābhūtāni catvāri ca mahābhūtānyupādāya 		de ni khams bzhin du blta ste /
de yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
gzugs kyi phung po'i rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na /
gzugs gang yin pa ci yang rung ste /
de thams cad 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag dang 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa'o /
katamāni catvāri mahābhūtāni 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag gang zhe na /
pṛthivīdhātuḥ abdhātuḥ tejodhātuḥ vāyudhātuśca sa'i khams dang chu'i khams dang me'i khams dang rlung gi khams so /
pṛthivīdhātuḥ katamaḥ sa'i khams gang zhe na /
kaṭhinatā sra ba nyid do /
abdhātuḥ katamaḥ niṣyandatā chu'i khams gang zhe na /
gsher ba nyid do /
tejodhātuḥ katamaḥ me'i khams gang zhe na /
uṣṇatā /
vāyudhātuḥ katamaḥ 		tsha ba nyid do /
rlung gi khams gang zhe na /
kampanatā /
upādāya rūpaṃ katamat /
cakṣurindriyaṃ śrotrendriyaṃ ghrāṇendriyaṃ jivhendriyaṃ kāyendriyaṃ rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyānāmekadeśo dharmāyatanasaṃgṛhītaṃ ca rūpam 		yang zhing g yo ba nyid do /
rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gang zhe na /
mig gi dbang po dang rna ba'i dbang po dang sna'i dbang po dang lce'i dbang po dang lus kyi dbang po dang gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya'i phyogs gcig dang chos kyi skye mched pa'i gzugs so /
cakṣurindriyaṃ katamat mig gi dbang po gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya cakṣuvijñānā śrayo rūpaprasādaḥ /
śrotrendriyaṃ katamat 		'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
mig gi rnam par shes pa'i rten gzugs dang ba'o /
rna ba'i dbang po gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya śrotravijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rten gzugs dang pa'o /
ghrāṇendriyaṃ katamat sna'i dbang po gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya ghrāṇavijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
sna'i rnam par shes pa'i rten gzugs dang pa'o /
jivhendriyaṃ katamat lce'i dbang po gang zhe na /
catvāri mahabhūtānyupādāya jivhāvijñānaśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ /
kāyendriyaṃ katamat 		'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
lce'i rnam par shes pa'i rten gzugs dang pa'o /
lus kyi dbang po gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya kāyavijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i rten gzugs dang pa'o /
rūpaṃ katamat gzugs gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya cakṣurindriyagocaro 'rthaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
mig gi dbang po'i spyod yul gyi don gang yin pa ste /
yathā nīlaṃ pītaṃ lohitamavadātaṃ dīrghaṃ hrasvaṃ vṛttaṃ parimaṇḍalaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmamunnatamavanataṃ sātaṃ visātamātapaḥ chāyā āloko 'dhakāramabhraṃ dhūmo rajo mahikā ca /
abhyavakāśarūpaṃ vijñaptirūpaṃ nabha ekavarṇaṃ rūpam 		'di lta sta; sngon po dang ser po dang dmar po dang dkar po dang ring po dang thung du dang lham pa dang zlum po dang rdul phra mo dang rags pa dang phyal le ba dang phyal le ba ma yin pa dang mthon po dang dma' ba dang grib ma dang nyi ma dang snang ba dang mun pa dang sprin dang du ba dang rdul dang khug rna dang mngon par skabs yod pa dang rnam par rig byed dang nam mkha' kha dog gcig pa'o /
tat punastridhā /
śobhanamaśobhanamubhayaviparītaṃ ca /
śabdaḥ katamaḥ 		de yang kha dog bzang po dang kha dog ngan pa dang; de gnyi ga'i bar mar gnas pa dang kha dog dang 'dra ba'o /
sgra gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya śrotrendriyabrāhyo 'rthaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
rna ba'i dbang po'i gzung ba'i don gang yin pa ste /
manojño vā amanojño vā ubhayaviparīto vā /
upāttamahābhūtahetuko vā anupāttamahābhūtahetuko vā tadubhayo bālokaprasiddho vā siddhopanīto vā parikalpito vā āryairdeśito vā tīrthaidaśito vā 		yid du 'ong ba dang yid du mi 'ong ba dang gnyi ga ma yin pa dang zin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba dang zin pa ma yin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba dang de gnyi ga dang 'jig rten gyi grags pa dang grub pas bstan pa dang kun brtags pa dang 'phags pas tha snyad btags pa dang 'phags pa ma yin pas tha snyad btags pa'o /
gandhaḥ katamaḥ dri gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya ghrāṇendriyagrāhyo 'rthaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
sna'i dbang po'i gzung ba'i don gang yin pa ste /
yathā surabhirasurabhiḥ samagandhaḥ sahajagandhaḥ sāṃyogikagandhaḥ pāriṇāmikagandhaśca /
rasaḥ katama 		dri zhim pa dang dring ba dang dri mnyam pa dang lhan cig skyes pa dang sbyar ba las byung ba dang gyur pa las byung ba'o /
ro gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtāmyupādāya jivhendriyabrāhyo 'rthaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
lce'i dbang po'i gzung ba'i don gang yin pa ste /
tikto 'mlo madhuraḥ kaṭuko lavaṇaḥ kaṣāyaśca /
manojño vā amanojño vā ubhayaviparīto vā sahajo vā sāṃyogiko vā pāriṇāmiko vā 		de yang kha ba dang sgyur ba dang tsha ba dang bska ba dang lan tshva dang mngar ba dang yid du 'ong ba dang yid du ma 'ong ba dang de gnyi ga ma yin pa dang lhan cig skyes pa dang sbyar ba las byung ba dang gyur ba las 'byung ba'o /
spraṣṭavyaikadeśaḥ katamaḥ reg bya'i phyogs gcig gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya kāyendriya grāhyo 'rthaḥ 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa /
lus kyi dbang pos gzung ba'i don gang yin pa ste /
ślakṣṇatvaṃ karkaśatvaṃ laghutvaṃ gurūtvaṃ picchilatvaṃ mandatvamamandatvaṃ śītatvamuṣṇatvaṃ jighatsā pipāsā tṛptirbalaṃ daurbalayaṃ mūrcchā kaṇḍūtiḥ pūtirvyādhirjarāmaraṇaṃ klāntirviśrāma ūrjā ca 'jam pa nyid dang rtsub pa nyid dang yang ba nyid dang lci ba nyid dang mnyen pa nyid dang lhod pa nyid dang lhod pa ma yin pa dang grang ba dang bkres pa dang skom pa dang tshim pa dang nyam yod pa dang nyam chung ba dang brgyal ba dang g ya' ba dang 'gred pa dang na ba dang rga ba dang 'chi ba dang ngal ba dang ngal sos pa dang spungs che ba'o /
dharmāyatanasaṃgṛhītaṃ rūpaṃ katamat chos kyi skye mched pa'i gzugs gang zhe na /
pañcavidham /
ābhisaṃkṣepikamābhyavakāśiṃkaṃ sāmādānikaṃ parikalpitaṃ vaibhutvikaṃ ca 		de ni rnam pa lngar blta ste /
bsdus pa las gyur pa dang mngon par skabs yod pa dang yang dag par blangs pa las byung ba dang kun brtags pa dang dbang 'byor pa'o /
vedanāskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat /
ṣaḍvedanākāyāḥ /
cakṣuḥsaṃsparśajā vedanā śrotraghrāṇajivhākāyamanaḥ saṃsparśajā vedanā /
evaṃ ṣaḍvedanā kāyāḥ sukhā vā duḥkhā aduḥkhāsukhā vā /
punaḥ sukhā kāyikī vedanā duḥkhā kāyikī vedanā aduḥkhāsukhā kāyikīvedanā sukhā caitasikī vedanā duḥkhā caitasikī vedanā aduḥkhāsukhā caitasikī vedanā sukhā sāmiṣavedanā duḥkhā sāmiṣavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā sāmiṣavedanā sukhā nirāmiṣavedanā duḥkhā nirāmiṣavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā nirāmiṣavedanā punaḥ sukhā gredhāśritavedanā duḥkhā gredhāśritavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā gredhāśritavedanā sukhā naiṣkramyāśritavedanā duḥkhā naiṣkramyāśritavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā naiṣkramyānnitavedanā ca /
kāyikī vedanā katamā 		tshor ba'i phung po'i rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na /
tshor ba'i tshogs drug ste /
mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba bde ba yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa yang rung ba dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba bde ba yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde pa yang ma yin pa yang rung ba ste /
bde ba lus kyi yang rung /
sdug bsngal lus kyi yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa lus kyi yang rung /
bde ba sems kyi yang rung /
sdug bsngal sems kyi yang rung /
sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa sems kyi yang rung /
bde ba zang zing dang bcas pa yang rung /
sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa zang zing dang bcas pa yang rung /
bde ba zang zing med pa yang rung /
sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa zang zing med pa yang rung /
bde bzhin pa rten pa yang rung /
sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa zhen pa rten pa yang rung /
bde ba mngon par 'byung ba rten pa yang rung /
sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa mngon par 'byung ba rten pa yang rung ba'o /
lus kyi gang zhe na /
paṃcavijñānasaṃprayuktā vedanā /
caitasikī vedanā katamā /

sāmiṣavedanā katamā /
ātmabhāvatṛṣṇāsaṃprayuktā vedanā /

sems kyi gang zhe na /

zang zing dang bcas pa gang zhe na /

zang zing med pa gang zhe na /

saṃjñāskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat 		de dang mi ldan pa'o /

ṣaṭ saṃjñākāyāḥ /
cakṣuḥsaṃsparśajā saṃjñā /
śrotraghrāṇa /
jivhākāyamanaḥsaṃsparśajā saṃjñā yathā sanimittama pi saṃjānāti animittamapi parīttamapi mahadgata mapyapramāṇamapi nāsti kiṃcidityākiṃcanyāyatanamapi saṃjānāti 		'du shes kyi tshogs drug ste; mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i 'du shes dang rna ba dang sna dang lus dang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i 'du shes te /
gang gis mtshan ma dang bcas pa yang dag par shes shing /
mtshan ma med pa dang chung du dang rgya chen por gyur pa dang tshad med pa dang ci yang med do snyam nas /
ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyang yang dag par shes pa'o /
sanimittasaṃjñā katamā mtshan ma dang bcas pa'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
avyavahārakuśalasyānimittadhātusamā pannasya bhavāgrasamāpannasya ca saṃjñāṃ sthāpayitvā yāvadanyā saṃjñā /
animittasaṃjñā katamā /
yā sthāpitā saṃjñā 		tha snyad la mi mkhas pa dang mtshan ma med pa'i dbyings la snyoms par zhugs pa dang; srid pa'i rtse mo la snyoms par zhugs pa'i 'du shes ma gtogs pa gang de las gzhan pa'i 'du shes so /
mtshan ma med pa'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
'du shes gang ma gtogs pa'o /
parīttā saṃjñā katamā chung ngu'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
yayā kāmadhātuṃ saṃjānāti gang gis 'dod pa'i khams shes pa'o /
mahagdatā saṃjñā katamā rgya chen por gyur pa'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
yayā rūpadhātuṃ saṃjānāti gang gis gzugs kyi khams shes pa'o /
apramāṇasaṃjñā katamā tshad med pa'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
yayā ākāśāna ntyāyatanaṃ vijñānānantyāyatanaṃ saṃjānāti gang gis nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched shes pa'o /
akiñcana saṃjñā katamā ci yang med pa'i 'du shes gang zhe na /
yayā ākiñcanyāyatanaṃ saṃjānāti gang gis ci yang med pa'i skye mched shes pa'o /
saṃskāraskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat 'du byed kyi phung po'i rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na /
ṣaṭ cetanākāyāḥ /
cakṣuḥsaṃsparśajā cetanā śrotraghrāṇajvihākāyamanaḥsaṃsparśajā cetanā yayā kuśalatvāya cetayate saṃkleśāya cetayate avasthābhedāya cetayate itīyaṃ cetanā vedanāṃ saṃjñācca sthāpayitvā tadanye caitasikā dharmāścittaviprayuktāśca saṃskārāḥ saṃskāraskandha ityucyate 		sems pa'i tshogs drug ste /
mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i sems pa dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i sems pa ste /
gang gis dge ba'i phyir yang sems par byed /
kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyir yang sems par byed /
gnas skabs kyi bye brag la yang sems par byed pa ste /
de ltar na sems pa 'di dang tshor ba dang 'du shes ma gtogs pa de las gzhan pa'i sems las byung ba'i chos rnams dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams ni 'du byed kyi phung po zhes bya'o /
te punaḥ katame de dag kyang gang zhe na /
manaskāraḥ sparśaḥ cchando 'dhimokṣaḥ smṛtiḥ samādhiḥ prajñāśraddhā hīrapatrāpyamālobho 'dveṣo 'mohoḥ vīryaṃ praśrabdhirapramāda upekṣā apristhitā rāgaḥ pratigho māno 'vidyā vicikitsā satkāyadṛṣṭirantaragrāhadṛṣṭirdṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavṛtaparāmarśaḥ mithyādṛṣṭi krodha upanāhaḥ mrakṣaḥ pradāśaḥ īrṣyāḥ mātsaryaṃ śāṭhyaṃ mado vihinsā āhrikyamanapatrāpyaṃ styānamauddhatyaṃ āśraddhyaṃ kausīdyaṃ pramādo muṣitasmṛtitāsaṃprajanyaṃ vikṣepo middhaṃ kaukṛtyaṃ vitarko vicāraśca /
cetanā katamā /

akuśale pravṛttikarmikā kuśalecāpravṛttikarmikā vā 		dge ba'i rtsa ba gcod pa'i las can dang mi dge ba'i rtsa ba dam du 'dzin pa'i rten byed pa'i las can dang mi dge ba la 'jug pa'i las can dang dge ba la mi 'jug pa'i las can no /
yā etāḥ pañca dṛṣṭayaḥ āsāṃ kati samāropadṛṣṭayaḥ katyapavāddṛṣṭayaḥ lta ba lnga po 'di dag las sgro 'dogs pa'i lta ba ni du /
skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba ni du zhe na /
catasraḥ samāropadṛṣṭayaḥ jñeye svabhāvaviśeṣasamāropatāmupādāya dṛṣṭau cāgraśuddhisamāropatāmupādāya /
ekā yadbhūyasā apavādadṛṣṭiḥ 		bzhi ni sgro 'dogs pa'i lta ba ste /
shes bya la ngo bo nyid dang khyad par du sgro 'dogs pa dang lta ba la mchog dang 'dag par sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
gcig ni phal cher la skur pa 'degs pa'i lta ba'o /
yāśca purvāntakalpikā dṛṣṭayaḥ yāścaparāntakalpikā dṛṣṭayaḥ tāḥ katibhyo dṛṣṭibhyo veditavyāḥ sngon gyi mthar rtog pa'i lta ba gang yin pa dang phyi ma'i mthar rtog pa'i lta ba gang yin pa de dag lta ba du zhig las byung bar rig par bya zhe na /
dvābhyāṃ sarvābhyo vā gnyis sam /
thams cad las so /
yā avyākṛtacastuṣu dṛṣṭayastāḥ katibhyo dṛṣṭibhyo veditavyāḥ lung du ma bstan pa'i dngos po rnams la lta ba gang yin pa de dag lta ba du zhig las byung bar rig par bya zhe na /
dvābhyāṃ sarvābhyo vā /
kaṃ doṣaṃ paśyatā bhagavatā skandhadhātvāyatanegu pañcamiḥ kāraṇairātmā pratikṣiptaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭiparigṛhītān pañca doṣān paśyatā vilakṣaṇatādoṣaṃ anityatādoṣaṃ asvāsthya doṣaṃ nirdehatādoṣaṃ ayatnato mokṣadoṣaṃ ca /
yā pañcasūpādānaskadheṣu viṃśatikoṭikā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ rūpa[mā]tmeti samanupaśyati rūpavantamātmānamātmīyaṃ rūpaṃ rūpe ātmānaṃ vedanāṃ saṃjñāṃ saṃskārān vijñānamātmeti samanupaśyati vijñānavantamātmānamātmīyaṃ vijñānaṃ vijñāne ātmānaṃ tatra katyātmadṛṣṭayaḥ katyātmīyadṛṣṭayaḥ pañcātmadṛṣṭayaḥ pañcadaśātmīyadṛṣṭayaḥ 		gnyis sam /
thams cad las so /
bcom ldan 'das kyis nyes pa gang gzigs nas /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la rnam pa lngas bdag bsal ba mdzad ce na /
'jig tshogs la lta bas yongs su zin pa'i nyes pa lnga gzigs nas te /
mtshan nyid dang mi mthun pa'i nyes pa dang mi rtag pa nyid kyi nyes pa dang rang dbang med pa'i nyes pa dang lus med pa'i nyes pa dang bsgrim mi dgos par thar par 'gyur ba'i nyes pa'o /
gang nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag la 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i mtha' nyi shu po /
gzugs bdag yin par lta ba dang; bdag gzugs dang ldan pa dang gzugs bdag gi yin pa dang gzugs la bdag gnas pa dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa bdag yin par lta ba dang bdag rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa dang rnam par shes pa bdag gi yin pa dang rnam par shes pa la bdag gnas so zhes bya ba de la /
bdag tu lta ba ni du /
bdag gir lta ba ni du zhe na /
kena kāraṇena pañca [daśā]tmīyadṛṣṭayaḥ /
sambandhātmīyatāmupādāya vaśavarttanātmīyatāmupādāya avinirbhogavṛttyātmīyatāṃ copādāya 		lnga ni bdag tu lta ba'o /
bcom ldan ni bdag gir lta ba'o /
ci'i phyir bcom lnga bdag gir lta ba zhes bya zhe na /
'brel bas bdag gir 'gyur ba dang dbang sgyur bas bdag gir 'gyur ba dang tha dad du mi 'jug pas bdag gir 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
satkāyadṛṣṭirnirūpitavastukā vaktavyā anirupitavastukā vaktavyā 'jig tshogs la lta ba dpyad pa'i gzhi can zhes bya'am /
ma dpyad pa'i gzhi can zhes bya zhe na /
anirūpitavastukā vaktavyā rajjvāṃ sarpabuddhivat ma dpyad pa'i gzhi can zhes brjod par bya ste /
thag pa la sprul gyi blo bzhin no /
krodhaḥ katamaḥ khro ba gang zhe na /
pratyupasthite apakāranimitte prati[ghāṃ] śikaścetasa āghātaḥ /
śastrādānaṃ daṇḍādānādisaṃrambhasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ 		gnod par byed pa'i rgyu nye bar gnas na /
khong khor ba'i char gtogs pa'i sems kyi kun nas mnar sems pa ste /
mtshon cha len pa dang chad pas gcod pa la sogs pa dang gnod pa shom pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
upanohaḥ katamaḥ tata ūrdhvaṃ pratighāṃśika eva vairāśayasyānutsargaḥ khon du 'dzin pa gang zhe na /
de'i 'og tu khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa nyid kyis /
shar gnyer ba'i bsam pa mi gtong ba ste /
akṣāntisanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ mi bzod pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
makṣaḥ katamaḥ 'chab pa gang zhe na /
samyak coditasya mohāṃśikā avadyapracchādanā /
kaukṛtyāsparśa vihārasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ 		legs par bskul ba la gti mug gi char gtogs pas kha na ma tho ba 'khyud pa ste /
'gyod pa dang reg par mi gnas pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
madāśaḥ katamaḥ 'tshig pa gang zhe na /
pratighāṃśikaḥ krodhopanāhapūrvaṅgamaścetasa āghātaḥ khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa khro ba dang khon du 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba'i sems kyis kun nas mnar sems pa ste /
uccapragāḍhapāruṣyavacanasanniśrayadāna karmakaḥ apuṇyaprasavakarmakaḥ asparśavihārakarmakaśca /
īrṣyā katamā 		tshig rtsub po blang zhing drag po'i rten byed pa'i las can dang bsod nams ma yin pa 'phel ba'i las can dang reg par mi gnas pa'i las can no /
phrag dog gang zhe na /
lābhasatkārā dhyavasitasya parasaṃpattiviśeṣe dveṣāṃśikaḥ a[marṣa] kṛtaścetaso vyāropaḥ rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par chags nas gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa'i khyad par la mi bzod par gyur ba sems khong nas 'khrug pa zhe sdang gi char gtogs pa ste /
daurmanasyāsparśavihārakarmakaḥ /
mātsaryaṃ katamat 		yid mi bde ba dang reg par mi gnas pa'i las can no /
ser sna gang zhe na /

asaṃlekhasanniśrayadānakarmakam /

śāṭhyaṃ ka[tamat] g yo gang zhe na /

'dod chags dang gti mug gi char gtogs pas nyes pa yang dag par skyong ba ste /
samyagavavādalābhaparipanthakaram yang dag pa'i gdams ngag rnyed pa'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no /
madaḥ katamaḥ rgyags pa gang zhe na /
ārogyaṃ vā āgamya yauvanaṃ vā dīrghāyuṣkalakṣaṇaṃ vopalabhyanyatamānyatamāṃ vā sāsravāṃ saṃpattiṃ rāgāṃśikannandīsaumanasyam /
sarvvakleśopakleśasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ 		nad med pa dang lang tshol bab pa la brten cing tshe ring ba'i mtshan ma dang zag pa dang bcas pa'i phun sum tshogs pa gang yang rung ba mthong nas /
'dod chags kyi char gtogs pa'i dga' ba dang yid bde ba ste /
nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi rten byed pa'i las can no /
vihinsā katamā rnam par 'tshe ba gang zhe na /
prati[ghāṃśi]kā nirvṛṇatā niṣkaraṇatā nirdayatā /
viheṭhanakarmikā 		khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa /
snying brtse ba med pa dang; snying rje ba med pa dang brtse ba med pa ste /
rnam par tho 'tsham pa'i las can no /
āhrīkyaṃ katamat ngo tsha med pa gang zhe na /
rāgadveṣamohāṃśikā svayamavadyenālajjanā /
sarvvakleśopakleśasāhāyyakarmakam /

khrel med pa gang zhe na /

sarvvakleśopakleśasāhāyyakarmakam /

rmugs pa gang zhe na /

sarvakleśopakleśasāhāyyakarmakam /
auddhatya katamat 		nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi grogs byed pa'i las can no /
rgod pa gang zhe na /
śubhanimittamanusarato rāgāṃśikaścetaso 'vyupaśamaḥ sdug pa'i mtshan ma'i rjes su 'jug pa'i 'dod chags kyi char gtogs pa'i sems rnam par ma zhi ba ste /
śamathaparipanthakarmakam zhi gnas kyi bar du gcod pa'i las can no /
āśradudhvaṃ katamat ma dad pa gang zhe na /

kausīdyasanniśrayadānakarmakam /

nidrāpārśvaśayana sukhallikāmāgamya mohāṃśikaścetaso 'nabhyutsāhaḥ nyal ba dang snyes pa dang 'phres pa'i bde ba la brten nas /
gti mug gi char gtogs pa'i sems mi spro ba ste /

pramodaḥ katamaḥ bag med pa gang zhe na /
sakausīdyān rāgadveṣamohānniśritya kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāmabhāvanā sāsravebhyaśca dharmebhyaścetaso 'nārakṣā /
akuśalavṛddhikuśalaparihāṇisanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ 		chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug le lo dang bcas pa la gnas nas /

mi dge ba 'phel ba dang dge ba 'grib pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
muṣitasmṛtitā katamā brjod nges pa gang zhe na /

vikṣepasanniśrayadānakarmikā g yeng ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
asaṃprajanyaṃ katamat shes bzhin ma yin pa gang zhe na /

āpattisanniśrayadānakarmakam 		nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i shes rab ste /

ltung ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
vikṣepaḥ katamaḥ rnam par g yeng ba gang zhe na /
rāgadveṣamohāṃśikaścetaso visāraḥ /
sa punaḥ svabhāvavikṣepaḥ bahirdhāvikṣepaḥ adhyātmavikṣepaḥ nimitta vikṣepaḥ dauṣṭhulyavikṣepaḥ manasikāravikṣepaśca 		'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi char gtogs pa'i sems kyi rnam par 'phro ba ste /
de yang ngo bo nyid kyis g yeng ba dang phyi rol tu g yeng ba dang nang gi g yeng ba dang mtshan ma'i g yeng ba dang gnas ngan len gyi g yeng ba dang yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba'o /
svabhāvavikṣipaḥ katamaḥ ngo bo nyid kyis g yeng ba gang zhe na /
pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga'o /
bahirdhā vikṣepa katamaḥ phyi rol tu g yeng ba gang zhe na /

adhyātmavikṣepaḥ katamaḥ /
kuśalaprayuktasya layauddhatyāsvādanā 		nang gi g yeng ba gang zhe na /
dge ba la zhugs pa bying ba dang rgod pa dang ro myang bar byed pa'o /
nimittavikṣepa katamaḥ mtshan ma'i g yeng ba gang zhe na /
parasaṃbhāvanāṃ puraskṛtya kuśalaprayogaḥ gzhan yid ches par bya ba sngon du btang ste dge ba la sbyor ba'o /
hauṣṭhulyavikṣepaḥ katamaḥ gnas ngan len gyi g yeng ba gang zhe na /
ahaṃkāramamakārāsmimānapakṣyaṃ dauṣṭhulyamāganya kuśalaprayuktasyotpannotpanneṣu vediteṣvahamiti vā mameti vā asmīti vā udgraho vyavakiraṇā nimittīkāraḥ ngar 'dzin pa dang nga yir 'dzin pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal gyi phyogs kyi gnas ngan len la brten nas /
dge ba la zhugs pa'i tshor ba byung ba 'byung ba rnams lang zhe'am /
nga yi zhe'am /
nga'o snyam du 'dzin pa dang 'dres pa dang mtshan mar 'dzin pa'o /
manasikāravikṣepaḥ katamaḥ yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba gang zhe na /
samapattyantaraṃ vā yānāntaraṃ vā samāpadyamānasya saṃśrayato vā yo visāraḥ snyoms par 'jug pa gzhan nam /
theg pa gzhan la snyoms par 'jug pa dang gnas pa'i rnam par 'phro ba gang yin pa ste /
vairāgyapari panthakarmakaḥ middhaṃ katamat 'dod chags dang 'brel ba'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no /
gnyid gang zhe na /
middhanimittamāgamya mohāṃśikaścetaso 'bhisaṃkṣepaḥ kuśalaḥ akuśalaḥ avyākṛtaḥ kāle vā akāle vā yukto vā ayukto vā /
kṛtyāvipattisanniśrayadānakarmakam 		gnyid kyi rgyu la brten nas dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang dus dang dus ma yin pa dang rigs pa dang mi rigs pa la sems sdud pa gti mug gi char gtogs pa ste /
bya ba shor ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
kaukṛtyaṃ katamat /
yadabhipretānabhipretaṃ kāraṇākāraṇāmāgamya mohāṃśikaścetaso vipratisāraḥ 		'gyod pa gang zhe na /

kuśalamakuśalamavyākṛtaṃ kāle akāle yuktamayuktañca /
cittasthitiparipanthakarmakaḥ /
vitarkaḥ katamaḥ /
cetanāṃ vā niśritya prajñāṃ vā paryeṣako manojalpaḥ 		dge ba dang mi dge ba dang; lung du ma bstan pa dang dus dang dus ma yin pa dang rigs pa dang mi rigs pa la sems kyis yid la gcags pa gti mug gi char gtogs pa ste /
sems gnas pa'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no /
rtog pa gang zhe na /
sems pa'am /
shes rab la brten nas /
kun tu tshol ba'i yid kyis brjod pa ste /
sā ca cittasyaudārikatā de ni sems rtsing ba'o /
vicāraḥ katamaḥ /
cetanāṃ vā niśritya prajñāṃ vā pratyavekṣako manojalpaḥ 		dpyod pa gang zhe na /
sems pa'am /
shes rab la brten nas /
so sor rtog pa'i yid kyis brjod pa ste /
sa ca cittasya sūkṣmatā de ni sems zhib pa'o /
sparśāsparśavihārasaṃniśrayadānakarmakau /
api khalu kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ svavipakṣaprahāṇaṃ karma /
kleśopakleśānāṃ svapratipakṣaparipanthanaṃ karma /
citta viprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ katame 		reg par gnas pa dang reg par mi gnas pa'i rten byed pa'i las can dag go /
yang chos dge ba rnams kyi las ni rang gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs spangs pa'o /
nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi las ni rang gi gnyen po'i bar du gcod pa'o /
sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams gang zhe na /
prāptirasaṃjñisamāpattinirodhasamāpattirāsaṃjñikaṃ jīvitendriyaṃ nikāyasabhāgatā jātirjarā sthitiranityatā nāmakāyāḥ padakāyāḥ vyañjanakāyāḥ pṛthagjanatvaṃ pravṛttiḥ pratiniyamo yogaḥ javo 'nukramaḥ kālo deśaḥ saṃkhyā sāmagrī ca /
prāptiḥ katamā /
kuśalakuśalāṃnāṃ dharmāṇāmācayāpacaye prāptiḥ pratilagbhaḥ samanvāgama iti prajñaptiḥ /
asaṃjñisamāpattiḥ katamā 		'thob pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa pa dang srog gi dbang po dang ris mthun pa dang skye ba dang rga ba dang gnas pa dang mi rtag pa nyid dang ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs dang so so'i skye bo nyid dang 'jug pa dang so sor nges pa dang 'byor 'brel pa dang mgyogs pa dang go rims dang dus dang yul dang grangs dang tshogs pa'o /
'thob pa gang zhe na /
dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos rnams kyi 'phel ba dang 'grib pa la 'thob pa dang rnyed pa dang ldan pa zhes gdags so /
'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa gang zhe na /
śubhakṛtsnavītarāgasyoparyavītarāgasya niḥsaraṇasaṃjñāpūrvakeṇa manasikāreṇāsthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ nirodhe asaṃjñisamāpattiriti prajñaptiḥ /
nirodhasamāpattiḥ katamā 		dge rgyas kyi 'dod chags dang bral la /
steng ma'i 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pas sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brtan pa ma yin pa rnams 'gog pa la 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa zhes gdags so /
'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa gang zhe na /
ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral la /
ākiṃcanyāyatanavītarāgasya bhavāgrāduccalitasya śāntavihārasaṃjñāpūrvakeṇa manasikāreṇāsthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ nirodhe nirodhasamāpattiriti prajñaptiḥ srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa'i zhi bar gnas pa'i 'dus shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pas /
sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brten pa ma yin pa rnams dang brtan pa de dag las kyang kha cig 'gog pa la /
'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa zhes gdags so /
āsaṃjñikaṃ katamat /
asaṃjñisattveṣudeveṣūpapannasyāsthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ nirodhe āsaṃjñikapriti prajñaptiḥ 		'du shes med pa pa gang zhe na /
sems can 'du shes med pa'i lha rnams kyi nang du skyes pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brten pa ma yin pa rnams 'gog pa la 'du shes med pa pa zhes gdags so /
jīvitendriyaṃ katamat srog gi dbang gi po gang zhe na /
nikāyasabhāge pūrvakarmāviddhe sthitikālaniyame āyuriti prajñaptiḥ ris mthun par sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs pa'i gnas pa'i 'dus nges pa la /
tshe zhes gdags so /
nikāyasabhāgaḥ katamaḥ /
teṣāṃ teṣāṃ sattvānāṃ tasmiṃ stasmin sattvanikāye ātmabhāvasadṛśatāyāṃ nikāyasabhāga iti prajñaptiḥ 		ris mthun pa gang zhe na /
sems can gyi rigs de dang der sems can de dang de dag gi lus 'dra ba la ris mthun pa zhes gdags so /
jātiḥ katamā skye ba gang zhe na /
nikāyasabhāge saṃskārāṇāmabhūtvābhāve jātiriti prajñaptiḥ /
jarā katamā /
nikāyasabhāme saṃskārāṇāṃ prabandhānyathātve jareti prajñaptiḥ 		ris mthun par 'du byad rnams ma byung ba las byung ba la skye ba zhes gdags so /
rga ba gang zhe na /
ris mthun par 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun gzhan du 'gyur ba la rga ba zhes gdags so /
sthitiḥ katamā gnas pa gang zhe na /
nikāyasabhāge prabandhāvipraṇāśe sthitiriti prajñaptiḥ /
anityatā katamā /
nikāyasabhāge saṃskārāṇāṃ prabandhavināśe anityateti prajñaptiḥ 		ris mthun par 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun mi 'jig pa la gnas pa zhes gdags so /
mi rtag pa nyid gang zhe na /
ris mthun par 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun 'jig pa la mi rtag pa nyid ces gdags so /
nāmakāyāḥ katame /
dharmāṇāṃ svabhāvādhivacane nāmakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ 		ming gi tshogs gang zhe na /
chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid kyi tshig bla dags la ming gi tshogs zhes gdags so /
padakāyāḥ katame /
dharmāṇāṃ viśeṣādhivacane padakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ 		tshig gi tshogs gang zhe na /
chos rnams kyi khyad par gyi tshig bla dags la tshig gi tshogs zhes gdags so /
vyañjanakāyāḥ katameḥ tadubhayāśrayeṣvakṣareṣu vyañjanakāyā iti prajñaptiḥ /
tadubhayābhivyañjanatāmupādāya 		yi ge'i tshogs gang zhe na /
de gnyid ga'i gnas yi ge rnams la yi ge'i tshogs zhes gdags te /
de gnyi ga gsal bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
varṇo 'pi saḥ rjod pa yang de yin te /
arthasaṃvarṇanatāmupādāya don yang dag par brjod pa'i phyir ro /
akṣare punaḥ paryāyākṣaraṇatāmupādāya yi ge ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
pṛthagjanatvaṃ katamat /
āryadharmāṇāmapratilābhe pṛthagjanatvamiti prajñaptiḥ /
pravṛttiḥ katamā /
hetuphala prabandhānupacchede pravṛttiriti prajñaptiḥ 		so so'i skye bo nyid gang zhe na /
'phags pa'i chos rnams ma tho ba la so so'i skye bo zhes gdags so /
'jug pa gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyun mi 'chad pa la 'jug pa zhes gdags so /
pratiniyamaḥ katamaḥ /
hetuphalanānātve pratiniyama iti prajñaptiḥ 		so sor nges pa gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu tha dad pa la so sor nges pa zhes gdags so /
yogaḥ katamaḥ /
hetuphalānurūpye yoga iti prajñaptiḥ 		'byor 'brel pa gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu rjes su mthun pa la 'byor pa zhes gdags so /
javaḥ katamaḥ /
hetuphalāśupravṛttau java iti prajñaptiḥ /
anukramaḥ katamaḥ /
hetuphalaikatye pravṛttau anukrama iti prajñaptiḥ 		mgyogs pa gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu myur bar byung ba la mgyogs pa zhes gdags so /
go rims gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu re re nas 'byung ba la go rims zhes gdags so /
kālaḥ katamaḥ /
hetuphalaprabandhapravṛttau kāla iti prajñaptiḥ /
deśaḥ katamaḥ /
pūrvadakṣiṇapaścimottarā dharordhvāsu sarvato daśasu dikṣu hetuphala eva deśa iti prajñaptiḥ /
saṃkhyā katamā /
saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyekaśo bhede saṃkhyeti prajñaptiḥ 		dus gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyun tu 'byung ba la dus zhes gdags so /
yul gang zhe na /
shar dang lho dang nub dang byang dang 'og dang steng dang phyogs bcu thams cad na rgyu dang 'bras bu yod pa nyid la yul zhes gdags so /
grangs gang zhe na /
'du byed rnams kyi so so tha dad pa la grangs zhes gdags so /
sāmagrī katamā /
hetuphalapratyayasamavadhāne sāmagrīti prajñaptiḥ 		tshogs pa gang zhe na /
rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rkyen 'dus pa la tshogs pa zhes gdags so /
vijñānaskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat /
yaccittaṃ manovijñānamapi 		rnam par shes pa'i phung po'i rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na /
sems dang yid gang yin pa rnam par shes pa yang de yin no /
tatra cittaṃ katamat /
skandhadhātvāyatanavāsanāparibhāvitaṃ sarvavījakamālayavijñānaṃ vipākavijñānamādānavijñānamapi tat /
tadvāsanācitatāmupādāya /
manaḥ katamat 		sems gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyi bag chags kyis yongs su bsgoms pas bon thams cad pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa dang len pa'i rnam par shes pa yang de yin te /
de dag gi bag chags bsags pa'i phyir ro /
yid gang zhe na /
yannityakālammanyanātmākamālayavijñānaṃ caturbhiḥ kleśaiḥ saṃprayuktamātmadṛṣṭyātmasnehenāsmimānenāvidyayā ca /
tacca sarvatragaṃ kuśale 'pyakuśale 'pyavyākṛte 'pi sthāpayitvā mārgasabhmukhībhāvaṃ nirodhasamāpattimaśaikṣa bhūmiṃ ca yacca ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ samanantaraniruddhaṃ vijñānam 		gang dus rtag tu rlom sems pa'i bdag nyid dang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dmigs pa dang nyon mongs pa bzhi po bdag tu lta ba dang bdag la chags pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang ma rig pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ste /
de yang lam mngon du gyur pa dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang mi slob pa'i sa ma gtogs par dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa thams cad du 'gro ba dang gang yang rnam par shes pa drug po dag 'gags ma thag pa'i rnam par shes pa'o /
vijñānaṃ katamat rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
ṣaḍ vijñānakāyāḥ /
cakṣurvijñānaṃ śrotraghrāṇajivhākāyamanovijñānam /
cakṣurvijñānaṃ katamat /
cakṣurāśrayā rūpālambanā prati vijñaptiḥ 		rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug ste /
mig gi rnam par shes pa dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o /
mig gi rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
mig la brten cing gzugs la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
śrotravijñānaṃ katamat /
śrotrāśrayā śabdālambanā prativijñaptiḥ 		rna ba'i rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
rna ba la brten cing sgra la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
ghrāṇavijñānaṃ katamat sna'i rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
ghrāṇāśrayā gandhālambanā pratibijñaptiḥ sna la brten cing dri la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
jilhāvijñānaṃ katamat lce'i rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
jivhāśrayā rasālambanā prativijñaptiḥ /
kāyavijñānaṃ katamat 		lce la brten cing ro la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
lus kyi rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
kāyāśrayā spraṣṭavyālambanā prativijñaptiḥ /
manovijñānaṃ katamat 		lus la brten cing re bya la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
yid kyi rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
manaāśrayā dharmālambanā prativijñaptiḥ /
dhātuvyavasthānaṃ katamat 		yid la brten cing chos la dmigs nas so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
khams kyi rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na /
rūpaskandhā eva daśa dhātavaḥ gzugs kyi phung po gang yin pa de ni khams bcu ste /
cakṣurdhātuḥ rūpadhātuḥ śrotradhātuḥ śabdadhātuḥ ghrāṇadhātuḥ gandhadhātuḥ jivhādhātuḥ rasadhātuḥ kāyadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyadhātuḥ mano dhātvekadeśaśca mig gi khams dang gzugs kyi khams dang rna ba'i khams dang; sgra'i khams dang sna'i khams dang dri'i khams dang lce'i khams dang ro'i khams dang lus kyi khams dang reg bya'i khams dang chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig kyang yin no /
vedanāskandhaḥ saṃjñāskandhaḥ saṃskāraskandhaśca dharmadhātvekadeśaḥ tshor ba'i phung po dang 'du shes kyi phung po dang 'du byed kyi phung po gang yin pa de ni chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig go /
vijñānaskandha eca sapta vijñānaghātavaḥ rnam par shes pa'i phung po gang yin pa de ni rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun te /
cakṣurādayaḥ ṣaḍ vijñānadhātavo manodhātuśca /
dharmadhātau skandhairasaṃgṛhītaṃ katamat 		mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang yid kyi khams so /
khams rnams kyi nang nas phung po rnams kyis ci zhig ma bsdus she na /
dharmadhātāvasaṃskṛtā dharmāḥ chos kyi khams la yod pa'i 'dus ma byas so /
te 'saṃskṛtādharmāḥ punaraṣṭadhā /
kuśaladharmatathatā akuśaladharmatathatā avyākṛtadharmatathatā ākāśam apratisaṃkhyā nirodhaḥ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ āniṃjyaṃ saṃjñāvedayitanirodhaśca /
kuśaladharmatathatā katamā 		de yang 'dus ma byas kyi dngos po brgyad de /
chos dge ba rnams kyi de bzhin nyid dang de bzhin du chos mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams kyi de bzhin nyid dang nam mkha' dang so sor brtags pa ma yin pas 'gog pa dang so sor brtags pas 'gog pa dang mi g yo ba dang 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa'o /
chos dge ba rnams kyi de bzhin nyid gang zhe na /
nairātmyam /
sā punarucyate śūnyatā animittaṃ bhūtakoṭiḥ paramārtho dharmādhātuśca 		bdag med pa rnam pa gnyis dang stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma med pa dang yang dag pa'i mtha' dang don dam pa ste /
kimupādāya tathatā tathatocyate chos kyi dbyings kyang de yin no /
ananyayābhāvatāmupādāya /
kimupādāya tathatā nairātmyamucyate /
dvividhātmaviprayuktatāmupādāya 		ci'i phyir de bzhin nyid la de bzhin nyid ces bya zhe na /
gzhan du mi 'gyur ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
kimupādāya tathatā śūnyatocyate /
sarvasaṃkleśāpracāratāmupādāya 		ci'i phyir stong pa nyid ces bya zhe na; kun nas nyon mongs pa mi rgyu ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya tathatā animittamucyate /
sarvanimittopaśamatāmupādāya 		ci'i phyir mtshan ma med pa zhes bya zhe na /
mtshan ma nye bar zhi ba'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya tathatā bhūtakāṭirucyate /
aviparyāsālambanatāmupādāya /
kimupādāya tathatā paramārtha ucyate 		ci'i phyir yang dag pa'i mtha' zhes bya zhe na /
phyin ci log med pa'i dmigs pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
ci'i phyir don dam pa zhes bya zhe na /
paramārthajñānagocarasthānatāmupādāya 'phags pa'i ye shes dam pa'i spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya tathatā dharmadhāturucyate /
sarveṣāṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ ca buddha dharmanimittāśrayatāmupādāya /
yathā kuśalaladharmatathatā tathā akuśaladharmatathatā avyākṛta dharmatathatā ca jñeyā 		ci'i phyir chos kyi dbyings zhes bya zhe na /
nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
chos dge ba rnams kyi de bzhin nyid ji lta ba bzhin du chos mi dge ba rnams dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams kyi de bzhin nyid kyang de bzhin du blta bar bya'o /
ākāśaṃ katamat /
rūpābhāvaḥ sarvakṛtyāvakāśatāmupādāya 		nam mkha' gang zhe na /
gzugs med cing byed pa thams cad kyi go 'byed pa'i phyir ro /
apratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ katamaḥ so sor brtags pa ma yin pas 'gog pa gang zhe na /
yo nirodho na visaṃyogaḥ gang 'gog pa la bral ba ma yin pa'o /
pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ katamaḥ so sor brtags pas 'gog pa gang zhe na /
yo nirodho visaṃyogaḥ gang 'gog la de ni bral ba'o /
ānijyaṃ katamat mi g yo ba gang zhe na /
śubhakṛtsnavītarāgasyoparyavītarāgasya sukhanirodhaḥ dge rgyas kyi 'dod chags dang bral la gong ma'i 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i bde ba dang sdug bsngal 'gog pa'o /
saṃjñāvedayitanirodhaḥ katamaḥ /
ākiṃcanyāyatanavītarāgasya bhāvāgrāduccalitasya śāntavihārasaṃjñāmanasikārapūrvakeṇa asthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ tadekatyānāṃ ca sthāvarāṇāṃ nirodhaḥ 		'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa gang zhe na /
ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral la /
srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa zhi bar gnas pa'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pas /
sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brten pa ma yin pa dang brtan pa de dag las kyang kha cig 'gog pa'o /
paṃcarūpāṇi vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāraskandhāḥ te 'ṣṭau asaṃskṛtā dharmāścaivaṃ te ṣoḍaśa dharmadhātava ucyante gzugs rnam pa lnga gang yin pa dang; tshor ba'i phung po dang 'du shes kyi phung po dang 'du byed kyi phung po gang yin pa dang 'dus ma byas kyi dngos po brgyad gang dag yin pa de dag gcig tu bsdus te /
āyatanavyavasthānaṃ katamat rnam pa bcu drug gi bdag nyid ni chos kyi khams so /
daśa rūpadhātava eva daśa rūpāyatanāni /
sapta vijñānadhātava eva manaāyatunam /
dharmadhāturdharmāyatanam /
anene nayena skandhadhātvāyatanāni triṣu dharmeṣu saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti 		skye mched kyi rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na; gzugs can gyi khams bcu po gang yin pa de dag nyid skye mched bcu'o /
rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun gang dag yin pa de dag yid kyi skye mched do /
chos kyi khams gang yin pa de chos kyi skye mched do /
de nyid kyi phyir phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams ni chos gsum du 'gyur te /
rūpaskandho dharmadhāturmanaāyatanaṃ ca /
yaduktaṃ cakṣuśca cakṣurdhātuśceti /
kiṃ syāccakṣuśca cakṣurdhātuśca /
āhosvit syāccakṣurdhātuśca cakṣuśca /
syāccakṣurna cakṣurdhātuḥ 		gzugs kyi phung po dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi skye mched do /
mig ces kyang bya /
mig gi khams zhes kyang bya na /
mig gang yin pa mig gi khams kyang de yin na /
mig gi khams gang yin pa mig kyang de yin nam zhe na /
mig yin la mig gi khams ma yin pa yang yod de /
yathā arhataścaramaṃ cakṣuḥ dgra bcom pa tha ma'i mig go /
syāccakṣardhātu rna cakṣuḥ mig gi khams yin la mig ma yin pa yang yod de /
yathā aṇḍe vā kalale vā arvude vā peśyāṃ vā mātuḥkukṣau vālabdhaṃ cakṣurlabdhaṃ vā naṣṭam /
ārūpyeṣūpapannasya pṛthagjanasya vā yaścakṣurhetuḥ /
syāccakṣuścakṣurdhātuśca 		sgo nga'i nang na 'dug pa dang nur nur por gyur pa dang mer mer por gyur pa dang nar nar por gyur pa dang ma'i mngal na gnas pa mig ma dod pa dang mig zhar ba dang gzugs med par skyes pa'i so so'i skye bo'i mig gi rgyu'o /
mig kyang yin la mig gi khams kyang yin pa'ang yod de /
śiṣṭāsvavasthāṣu /
na syāccakṣurna cakṣurdhātuśca 		de ma yin pa'i gnas skabs gzhan rnams so /
mig kyang ma yin la mig gi khams kyang ma yin pa'ang yod de /
nirupādhiśeṣanirvāṇadhātusamāpannasya ārūpyeṣūpapannasyāryasya vā /
yathā cakṣuśya cakṣurdhātuśca tathā śrotraghrāṇajivhākāya dhātavo yathāyogyaṃ veditavyāḥ 		phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa dang gzugs med par skyes pa'i 'phags pa'i'o /
mig dang mig gi khams ji lta ba bzhin du /
rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang lus kyi khams kyang de bzhin te /
de yang ci rigs su sbyar ro /
kiṃ syānmano 'pi manodhāturapi ahosvit syānmanodhāturapi mano 'pi yid gang yin pa yid kyi khams kyang de yin nam /
yid kyi khams gang yin pa yid kyang de yin nam zhe na /
syānmano na manodhātuḥ yid yin la yid kyi khams ma yin pa yang yod de /
yathā arhataścaramaṃ manaḥ dgra bcom pa tha ma'i yid do /
syānmanodhāturna manaḥ /
yathā nirodhasamāpannasya yo manohetuḥ /
syānmano 'pi manodhāturapi 		yid kyi khams yin la yid ma yin pa'ang yod de /
'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa'i yid kyi khams so /
yid kyang yin la yid kyi khams kyang yin pa'ang yod de /
śiṣṭāsvavasthāsu /
na syānmano 'pi manodhāturapi 		de ma yin pa'i gnas skabs gzhan rnams so /
yid kyang ma yin la yid kyi khams kyang ma yin pa'ang yod de /
yathā nirūpādhiśeṣanirvāṇadhātusamāpannasya /
tadbhūmāvutpannaḥ kiṃ tadbhūmikena cakṣuṣā tadbhūmikāni rūpāṇi paśyati 		phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i'o /
gang du byung zhing skyes par gyur pa de'i sa pa nyid kyi mig gis de'i sa pa'i gzugs rnams mthong ngam zhe na /
tadbhūmikena cakṣuṣā tadbhūmikāni rūpāṇi paśyati, anyabhūmikenāpi de'i sa pa'i mig gis de'i sa pa'i gzugs rnams mthong ba'ang yod /
gzhan gyi sa pas mthong ba'ang yod de /
kāmadhātāvapapannaḥ māvacareṇa cakṣuṣā kāmāvacarāṇi rūpāṇi paśyati /
rūpāvacareṇordhvabhūmikeana cakṣuṣā adharabhūmikānyapi rūpāṇi paśyati 		'dod pa'i khams su byung zhing skyes par gyur pa 'dod pa na spyod pa'i mig gis 'dod pa na spyod pa'i gzugs rnams mthong ba dang gzugs na spyod pa sa gong ma pas sa 'og ma pa rnams mthong ba'o /
mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ba ji lta ba bzhin du /
yathā cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi pratigṛṇhāti tatha śrotreṇa śabdaṃ pratigṛṇhāti /
yathā kāmadhātāvutpannastathā rūpadhātāvutpannaḥ kāmāvacareṇa ghrāṇena jivhayā kāyena cā kāmāvacarān gandhān jighrati rasānāsvādane sparśān budhyati ca 		rna bas sgra yang de bzhin no /
'dod pa'i khams su byung zhing skyes par gyur pa ji lta ba bzhin du /
gzugs kyi khams su skyes par gyur pa'ang de bzhin no /
'dod pa'i khams su skyes pa 'dod pa na spyod pa'i sna dang lce dang lus kyis 'dod pa na spyod pa nyid kyi dri rnams snom mo /
ro rnams myang ngo /
reg bya rnams reg go /
rūpadhātāvutpanno rūpāvacareṇa kāyena svabhūmikān sparśān budhyati /
tasmin dhātau svabhāvato na gandharasau 		gzugs kyi khams su skyes par gyur pa gzugs na spyod pa'i lus kyis /
rang gi sa pa nyid kyi reg bya rnams la reg go /
de na dri dang ro ni rang bzhin gyis med de /
vijñaptyāhārarāgavirahāt kham gyi zas kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
anena nayena na ghrāṇajivhayo rvijñānam de'i phyir sna'i rnam par shes pa dang lce'i rnam par shes pa yang med do /
kāmadhātāvutpannaḥ kāmāvacareṇa manasā traidhātukānanāsravāṃśca dharmāna vijānāti 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur pa 'dod pa na spyod pa'i yid kyis /
khams gsum pa na spyod pa rnams dang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyang shes so /
yadhā kāmadhātāvutpannastathā rūpadhātāvutpannaḥ /
ārūpyadhātāvutpanna ārūpyāvacareṇa manasā ārūpyāvacarān svabhūmikānanāsravāṃśca dharmān vijānāti 		'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur pa ji ltar bzhin du /
gzugs kyi khams su skyes par gyur pa yang bzhin no /
gzugs med pa'i khams su byung zhing skyes par gyur pa ni /
gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i yid kyis /
gzugs med pa na spyod pa rang gi sa pa rnams dang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyang shes so /
anāsraveṇa manasā traidhātukānanāsravāṃśca dharmān vijānāti zag pa med pa'i yid kyis ni /
khams gsum pa na spyod pa rnams dang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyang shes so /
kimupādāya skandhānāṃ tathānukramaḥ /
vijñānādhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya /
catvāri vijñānādhiṣṭhānāni vijñānāni ca pūrvāparāśritāni 		ci'i phyir phung po rnams go rims su blags she na /
rnam par shes pa'i gnas nyid kyi phyir te /
rnam par shes pa'i gnas bzhi dang gnas bzhin dang rnam par shes pa'o /
yathā rūpaṃ tathā bhavaḥ /
yathā vedayate tathā saṃjānīte /
yathā saṃjānīte tathā cetayate /
yathā cetayate tathā vijñānaṃ tatra tatropagaṃ bhavati 		yang sna ma ni phyin ma'i rten yin pa'i phyir te; gzugs ji lta ba de bzhin du myong ngo /
ji ltar tshor bar byed pa de bzhin du 'du shes su byed do /
ji ltar 'du shes su byed pa de bzhin du sems par byed do /
ji ltar sems par byed pa de bzhin du rnam par shes par byed de /
de dang der nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur ro /
saṃkleśavyavadānataḥ /
yatra saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ca /
vedanānimittagrahaṇābhisaṃskāreṇa saṃkleśavyavadānābhyāṃ ca saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ca 		yang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba nyid kyi phyir te /
gang du kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang myong ba dang mtshan mar 'dzin pa dang mngon par 'du byed pa gang gis kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang gang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba ste /
anena nayena skandhānāmukramo nirdiśyate phung po rnams kyi go rims bstan pa ni de lta'o /
kathaṃ dhātūnāṃ tathānukramaḥ ci'i phyir khams rnams go rims su blags she na /
laukika vastu vikalpapravṛttitā mupādāya 'jig rten gyi tha snyad dang mthun pa'i phyir ro /
katamā laukikī vastuvikalpapravṛttiḥ 'jig rten gyi tha snyad dang mthun pa gang zhe na /
loke prathamaṃ paśyati de la thog ma kho nar phan tshun du blta'o /
dṛṣṭvā vyatisārayati blta ba la brten nas kun tu smra'o /
vyatisārya snāpitaṃ gandhaṃ mālyaṃ ca paricarati de'i 'og tu khrus dang byung ba dang phreng ba longs spyod du byed do /
tato nānāvidhaṃ praṇītaṃ bhojanaṃ paricarati de'i 'og tu bzang ba dang btung ba yongs su spyod do /
tato 'nekaśayyāsanadāsīparikān paricarati de'i 'og tu mal dang gding ba dang bud med la yongs su spyod do /
aparato manodhātorapi teṣu teṣu vikalpaḥ thams cad du rnam par rtog pa can yid kyi khams so /
evaṃ ca adhyātmadhātoranukrameṇa bahirdhādhātorvyavasthānam nang gi khams rnams rgyur byas nas phyi'i khams rnams go rims su blags so /
tadanukrameṇa vijñānadhātorvyavasthānam de'i 'og tu rnam par shes pa'i khams rnams so /
yathā dhātūnāmanukrama āyatanānāmapi tadvat /
skandhārthaḥ katamaḥ /
yat kiṃcidrūpam /
atītamanāgataṃ pratyutpannamadhyātmaṃ vā bahirdhā vā audārikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yadvā dūre yadvāntike tatsarvamabhisaṃkṣipyocyate rūpaskandhaḥ rāśyarthamupādaya 		khams rnams kyi go rims ji ltar ba bzhin du skye mched rnams kyi 'ang de bzhin no /
phung po'i don gang zhe na /
gzugs gang yin pa ci yang rung ste /
'das pa'am /
ma 'ongs pa'am /
da ltar byung ba'am /
nang gi'am /
phyi'i'am /
rags pa'am /
phra ba'am /
ngan pa'am /
gya nom pa'am /
rgyang ring ba gang yin pa'am /
thag nye ba gang yin pa de thams cad gcig tu bsdus te spungs pa'i phyir gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya'o; /
yathā vittarāśiḥ /
evaṃ yāvat vijñānaskandham 		rnam par shes pa'i phung po'i bar du'ang de bzhin te /
nor gyi phung po bzhin no /
āpica duḥkhavaipulya lakṣaṇatāmupādāya skandha ucyate yang sdug bsngal shin tu rgyas pa'i mtshan nyid kho na'i phyir te /
yathāmahāvṛkṣaskandhaḥ /
yaduktaṃ sūtre 		ji skad du sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'di 'ba' zhig 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
yathā aikāntikamahāduḥkhasamudayataḥ /
api ca saṃkleśato bhāravahanatāmupādāya skandha ucyate 		zhes gsungs pa lta bu ste; shing gi phung po bzhin no /
yang kun nas nyon mongs pa'i khur khyer ba nyid kyi phyir te /
yathā skandhena bhāramudvahati phrag khur khyer ba bzhin no /
dhātvarthaḥ katamaḥ khams kyi don gang zhe na /
sarvadharmavījārthaḥ chos thams cad kyi sa bon gyi don to /
svalakṣaṇadhāraṇārthaḥ yang rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i don to /
kāryakāraṇa bhāvadhāraṇārthaḥ yang 'bras bu dang rgyu'i dngos po 'dzin pa'i don to /
sarvaprakāradharmasaṃgra hadhāraṇārthañca /
āyatanārthaḥ katamaḥ 		yang chos kyi rnam pa thams cad bsdus nas 'dzin pa'i don to /
skye mched kyi don gang zhe na /
vijñānāyadvārārtha āyatanārthaḥ /
yathā buddhena bhāṣitam rūpaṃ budbudopamaṃ vedanā phenopamā saṃjñā marīcikopamā saṃskārāḥ parṇo pamā vijñānaṃ māyopamamiti /
kimarthaṃ rūpaṃ budbudopamaṃ yāvad vijñānaṃ māyopamamiti 		rnam par shes pa'i skye ba'i sgo'i don to /
gzugs ni dbu ba rdos pa lta bu'o /
tshor ba ni chu'i chu bur lta bu'o /
'du shes ni smig rgyu lta bu'o /
'du byed rnams ni chu shing gi phung po lta bu'o /
rnam par shes pa ni sgyu ma lta bu'o zhes gang gsungs pa de la /
ci'i phyir gzugs dbu ba rngos pa lta bu'o zhes bya ba nas /
rnam par shes pa sgyu ma lta bu'o zhes bya ba'i bar du zhe na /
anātmato 'śucito hīnarasato 'dṛḍhato 'sārataśca /
athamūlavastuni tridharmaparicchede prathame dvitīyo bhāgaḥ 		bdag med pa nyid dang gtsang ba med pa nyid dang ro bro ba chung ba nyid dang mi brtan zhing snying po med pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
punaḥ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ vikalpāḥ katame phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
tathācodānam sdom du na /
dravyamanto jñeyarūpāṇyāsravotpannakādi ca rdzas yod shes bya ba gzugs can sogs /
zag bcas byung la sogs pa dang /
atītāḥ pratyayāścaiva kathaṃ kati kimarthibhiḥ 'das dang rkyen la sogs pa rnams /
ji ltar du zhig ci yi phyir /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣu kathaṃ dravyamat kati dvayamanti kimarthaṃ dravyamatparīkṣā /
abhilāpanirapekṣastadanyanirapekṣaścendriyagocaro dravyamat 		phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams /
ji ltar na rdzas su yod pa yin /
rdzas su yod pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir rdzas su yod par brtag ce na /
dbang po'i spyod yul brjod pa dang de las gzhan pa la mi ltos pa ni rdzas su yod pa'o /
sarvaṃ dravyamat thams cad kyang rdzas su yod pa'o /
ātmadravyā bhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ prajñaptimat 		bdag la rdzas su mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir rdzas su yod par brtag go /
ji ltar na btags pa'i yod pa yin /
kati prajñaptimanti kimarthaṃ prajñaptimatparīkṣā /
abhilāpasāpekṣastadanyasāpekṣaścendriyagocaraḥ prajñaptimat 		btags pa'i yod pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir btags pa'i yod par brtag ce na /
dbang po'i spyod yul brjod pa dang de las gzhan pa la ltos pa dang bcas pa ni btags pa'i yod pa'o /
sarvaṃ prajñaptimat thams cad kyang btags pa'i yod pa'o /
prajñaptimadātmā bhiniveśatyājanārtham bdag la btags par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir btags pa'i yod par brtag go /
kathaṃ saṃvṛtimat ji ltar na kun rdzob tu yod pa yin /
kati saṃvṛtimanti kun rdzob tu yod pa rnams ni du zhig /
kimarthaṃ saṃvṛtimatparīkṣā ci'i phyir kun rdzob tu yod par brtag ce na /
saṃkleśālambanaṃ saṃvṛtimat /
sarvaṃ saṃvṛtimat /
saṃkleśanimittātmābhiniveśatyajanārtham /
kathaṃ paramārthasat 		kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba'i dmigs pa ni kun rdzob tu yod pa'o /
thams cad kyang kun rdzob tu yod pa'o /
bdag la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rgyur mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na don dam par yod pa yin /
kati paramārthasanti don dam par yod pa rnams ni du zhig /
kimarthaṃ paramārthasatparīkṣā ci'i phyir don dam par yod par brtag ce na /
vyavadānālambanaṃ paramārthasat rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i dmigs pa ni don dam par yod pa'o /
sarvaṃ paramārthasat thams cad kyang don dam par yod pa'o /
vyavadānanimittātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham bdag la rnam par dag pa'i rgyur mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ jñeyaṃ kati jñeyāni kimarthaṃ jñeyaparīkṣā ji ltar na shes par bya ba yin /
shes par bya ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir shes par bya bar brtag ce na /
jñeyāni paṃca /
rūpaṃ cittaṃ caitasikā dharmāścittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārā asaṃskṛtaṃ ca /
yatra saṃkleśo vyavadānaṃ vayat saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate vā yaśca saṃkleśayati vyavadāyayati vā yā ca tatrāvasthā yā ca vyavadānatā tadāśrayeṇa sarvaṃ jñeyam /
tatra rūpaṃ rūpaskandho daśarūpadhātavo daśa rūpāyatanāni dharmadhātvāyatanasaṃgṛhītāni ca rūpāṇi 		shes par bya ba ni rnam pa lnga ste /
gzugs dang sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams dang 'dus ma byas rnams te /
gang du kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang gang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang gang gis kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang de'i gnas skabs gang yin pa dang rnam par byang ba gang yin pa de'i dbang du byas nas /
thams cad kyang shes par bya ba dag go /
de la gzugs ni gzugs kyi phung po ste /
gzugs can gyi khams bcu dang skye mched bcu dang chos kyi khams dang skye mched pa'i gzugs so /
cittaṃ vijñānaskandhaḥ saptavijñānadhātavo manaāyatanaṃ ca sems ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po ste /
rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun dang yid kyi skye mched do /
caitasikā dharmā vedanāskandhaḥ saṃjñāskandhaḥ saṃskāraskandho dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaśca sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ni /
tshor ba'i phung po dang 'du shes kyi phung po dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i 'du byed kyi phung po dang chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig kyang yin no /
cittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ citta viprayuktaḥ saṃskāraskandho dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaśca ldan pa ma yin pa ni ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi phung po dang chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig kyang yin no /
asaṃskṛtaṃ dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaḥ 'dus ma byas ni chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go /
api khalu jñeyā dharmāḥ adhimuktijñānagocarato 'pi yuktijñānagocarato 'pi avisārajñānagocarato 'pi pratyātmajñānagocarato 'pi parātmajñānagocarato 'pi adharajñānagocarato 'pi ūrdhvajñānagocarato 'pi vidūṣaṇajñānagocarato 'pi asamutthānajñānagocarato 'pi anutpādajñānagocarato 'pi jñānajñānagocarato 'pi niṣṭhājñānagocarato 'pi mahārthajñānagocarato 'pi yang shes bya'i chos rnams ni /
mos pa'i shes pa'i spyod yul dang rigs pa'i shes pa'i spyod yul dang rnam par 'phro ba med pa'i shes pa'i spyod yul dang so so rang gis shes pa'i spyod yul dang gzhan gyi bdag nyid shes pa'i spyod yul dang 'og ma shes pa'i spyod yul dang gong ma shes pa'i spyod yul dang rnam par sun 'byin pa'i shes pa'i spyod yul dang kun nas mi ldang ba shes pa'i spyod yul dang mi skye ba shes pa'i spyod yul dang shes pa shes pa'i spyod yul dang mthar thug pa shes pa'i spyod yul dang don chen po shes pa'i spyod yul gyi phyir yang ngo /
jānakapaśyakātmābhiniveśatmājanārtham bdag la shes pa po dang mthong ba por mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ vijñeyaṃ kati vijñeyāni kimarthaṃ vijñeyaparīkṣā ji ltar na rnam par shes par bya ba yin /
rnam par shes par bya ba rnams ni du zhig /
avikalpanato 'pi vikalpanato 'pi hetuto 'pi pravṛttito 'pi nimittato 'pi naimittakato 'pi vipakṣapratipakṣato 'pi sūkṣmaprabhedato 'pi vijñeyaṃ draṣṭavyam ci'i phyir rnam par shes par bya bar brtag ce na /
rnam par mi rtog pa dang rnam par rtog pa dang rgyu dang 'jug pa dang rgyu mtshan dang rgyu mtshan las byung ba dang mi mthun pa dang gnyen po dang phra ba'i rab tu dbye bas kyang rnam par shes par bya bar blta'o /
sarvāṇi vijñeyāni /
draṣṭā dyātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		thams cad kyang rnam par shes par bya ba dag go /
bdag la mthong ba po la sogs par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathamabhijñeyaṃ katyabhijñeyāni kimarthamabhijñeyaparīkṣā /
saṃkrāntito 'pi anuśravato 'pi caritapraveśato 'pi āgatito 'pi gatito 'pi niḥsaraṇato 'pi 		ji ltar na mngon par shes par bya ba yin /
mngon par shes pa bya ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir mngon par shes par bya bar brtag ce na /
kun tu 'gro ba dang rjes su thos pa dang spyod pa la 'jug pa dang 'ong bas dang 'gro ba dang nges par 'byung ba'i phyir yang ngo /
sarvāṇyabhijñeyāni /
sānubhāvātmābhiniveśatyājanartham 		thams cad kyang mngon par shes par bya ba dag go /
bdag la mthu dang bcas par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ rūpi kati rūpīṇi kimarthaṃ rūpiparīkṣā ji ltar na gzugs can yin /
gzugs can rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gzugs can du brtag ce na /
rūpi tadātmato 'pi bhūtāśrayato 'pi nandīsamudayato 'pi pradeśato 'pi deśavyāptito 'pi deśopadeśato 'pi deśagocarato 'pi dvayasamaya gocarato 'pi sambandhato 'pya nuvandhato 'pi prarūpaṇato 'pi vyābādhanato 'pi saṃprāpaṇato 'pi saṃcayavyavasthānato 'pi vahirmukhato 'pi antarmukhato 'pi āyatato 'pi parichinnato 'pi tatkālato 'pi nidarśanato 'pi rūpi draṣṭavyam gzugs de'i bdag nyid dang 'byung ba rten du gyur pa dang dga' ba'i kun 'byung ba dang phyogs dang bcas pa dang yul la khyab pa dang yul nye bar bstan du rung ba dang yul spyod yul du 'gyur ba dang gnyis spyod yul du mtshungs pa dang 'brel pa dang rjes su 'brel ba dang rab tu rtog pa dang gnod par bya ba yin pa dang go bar byed pa dag /
bsags pa rnam par gzhag pa dang phyi rol du bltas pa dang nang du bltas pa dang rgyun ring ba dang dus yongs su chad pa dang de'i dus dang nges par bstan pa'i phyir yang gzugs can du blta'o /
thams cad kyang gzugs can dag go /
sarvāṇi rūpīṇi yathāyogaṃ vā yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
rūpyātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham bdag la gzugs can du mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathamarūpi katyarūpīṇi kimarthamarūpiparīkṣā /
rūpiviparyayeṇāpyaṃ rūpi /
sarvāṇyarūpīṇi yathāyogaṃ vā /
arūpyātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ sanidarśanaṃ kati sanidarśanāni kimarthaṃ sanidarśanaparīkṣā 		ji ltar na gzugs can ma yin /
gzugs can ma yin pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gzugs can ma yin par brtag ce na /
gzugs can las bzlog pa ni gzugs can ma yin pa dag go /
thams cad kyang gzugs can ma yin pa dag go /
yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
bdag la gzugs can ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na bstan du yod pa yin /
bstan du yod pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir bstan du yod par brtag ce na /
cakṣurgocaraḥ sanidarśanam mig gi yul ni bstan du yod pa'o /
śiṣṭasya rūpivat prabhedaḥ lhag ma'i rab tu dbye ba ni gzugs can bzhin no /
sarvāṇi sanidarśanāni yathāyogaṃ vā /
cākṣuṣātmābhiniveśatyājanā rtham /
kathamanirdarśanaṃ katyanidarśanāni kimarthamanidarśanaparīkṣā 		thams cad kyang bstan du yod pa dag go /
yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
bdag mig gi yul du mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na bstan du med pa yin /
bstan du med pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir bstan du med par brtag ce na /
sanidarśanaviparyayeṇānidarśanaṃ draṣṭavyam bstan du yod pa las bzlog pa ni bstan du med par blta'o /
sarvāṇyanidarśanāni yathāyogaṃ vā thams cad kyang bstan du med pa dag go /
yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
acākṣuṣā tmābhiniveśatyājanārtham bdag mig gi yul ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ sapratighaṃ kati sapratighāni kimarthaṃ sapratigha parīkṣā ji ltar na thogs pa dang bcas pa yin /
thogs pa dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir thogs pa dang bcas par brtag ce na /
yat sanidarśanaṃ saprati ghamapi tat bstan du yod pa gang yi pa de thogs pa dang bcas pa yang de yin no /
api khalu tribhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sapratighaṃ draṣṭavyam yang rnam pa gsum gyis thogs pa dang bcas par blta ste /
jātito 'pi upacayato 'pi aparikarmakṛtato 'pi tatra jātitaḥ yadyadanyo 'nyamāvṛṇotyavriyate ca rigs dang nye bar bsags pa dang yongs su sbyang ba ma byas pas kyang ngo /
de la rigs ni gang phan tshun du sgrib par byed pa dang bsgrib par bya ba'o /
tatropacayataḥ paramaṇorūrddham de la nye bar bsags pa ni rdul phra rab las gong bur gyur pa'o /
tatrāparikarmakṛtataḥ yanna samādhivaśavarttirūpam de la yongs su sbyang ba ma byas pa ni gang ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang gis ma bsgyur ba'i gzugs so /
api khalu prakopapadasthānataḥ - sapratigham yang rab tu 'khrug pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pas thogs pa dang bcas pa'o /
sarvāṇi sapratighāni yathāyogaṃ vā thams cad kyang thogs pa dang bcas pa dag go /
yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
asarvagatātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathamapratighaṃ katyapratighāni kimarthamapratighaparīkṣā 		bdag la thams cad du song ba ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na thogs pa med pa yin /
thogs pa med pa rnams ni du zhig /
sapratighaviparyeṇāpratigham /
sarvāṇyapratighāni yathāyogaṃ vā /
sarvagatātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ sāsravaṃ kati sāsravāṇi kimarthaṃ sāsravaparīkṣā /
āsravatadātmato 'pi āsravasaṃbandhato 'pi āsravānuvandhato 'pi āsravānukūlyato 'pi āsravānvayato 'pi sāsravaṃ draṣṭavyam 		ci'i phyir thogs pa med par brtag ce na /
thogs pa dang bcas pa las bzlog pa ni thogs pa med pa'o /
thams cad kyang thogs pa med pa dag go /
yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro /
bdag la thams cad du song bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zag pa dang bcas pa yin /
zag pa dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zag pa dang bcas par brtag ce na /
zag pa de'i bdag nyid dang zag pa dang 'brel ba dang zag pas bcings pa dang zag pa'i rjes su 'brel pa dang zag pa'i rjes su mthun pa dang zag pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir zag pa dang bcas par blta'o /
pañcopādānaskandhāḥ sāsravāḥ pañcadaśa dhātavo daśāyatanāni trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ /
āsravayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams dang khams bcva lnga dang skye mched bcu dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs ni zag pa dang bcas pa rnams so /
bdag zag pa dang bcas par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zag pa med pa yin /
kathamanāsravaṃ katyanāsravāṇi kimarthamanāsravaparīkṣā zag pa med pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zag pa med par brtag ce na /
sāsravaviparyayeṇānāsravam zag pa dang bcas pa las bzlog pa ni zag pa med par blta'o /
pañcānupādanaskandhāḥ trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ /
āsravaviyuktātmātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		nye bar len pa med pa'i phung po lnga rnams dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs so /
bdag zag pa dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ saraṇaṃ kati saraṇāni kimarthaṃ saraṇaparīkṣā /
yadrūpān rāgadveṣamohānāgamya śastrādānadaṇḍādānakalahabhaṇḍanavigrahavivādāḥ saṃbhavanti tadātmato 'pi tatsambandhato 'pi tadbandhato 'pi tadanubandhato 'pi tadānukūlyato 'pi tadanvayato 'pi saraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam 		ji ltar na 'thab pa dang bcas pa yin /
'thab pa dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'thab pa dang bcas par brtag ce na /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi ngo bo gang la brten nas /
mtshon cha len pa dang chad pas gcod pa dang 'thab rtsod dang mtshang 'bru ba dang rtsod pa dang 'gyed pa rnams 'byung ba de'i bdag nyid dang de dang 'brel pa dang des bcings pa dang de'i rjes su 'brel pa dang de'i rjes su mthun pa dang de'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir 'thab pa dang bcas par blta'o /
yāvanti sāsravāṇi tāvanti saraṇāni /
raṇayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		zag pa dang bcas pa ji snyed pa 'thab pa dang bcas pa'ang de snyed do /
bdag 'thab pa dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathamaraṇaṃ katyaraṇāni kimarthamaraṇaparīkṣā ji ltar na 'thab pa med pa yin /
'thab pa med pa rnams ni du zhig /
saraṇaviparyayeṇāraṇam /
yāvantyanāsravāṇi tāvantyaraṇāni /
raṇaviprayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ sāmiṣaṃ kati sāmiṣāṇi kimarthaṃ sāmiṣaparīkṣā /
yadrūpān rāgadveṣamohānāgamya paunarbhavikamātmabhāvamadhyavasyati tadātmato 'pi tatsambandhato 'pi tadbandhato 'pi tadanubandhato 'pi tadānukūlyato 'pi tadanvayato 'pi sāmiṣaṃ draṣṭavyam 		ci'i phyir 'thab pa med par brtag ce na /
'thab pa dang bcas pa las bzlog pa ni 'thab pa med pa'o /
zag pa med pa ji snyed par 'thab pa med pa'ang de snyed do /
bdag 'thab pa dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zang zing dang bcas pa yin /
zang zing dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zang zing dang bcas par brtag ce na /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi ngo bo gang la brten nas /
yang srid pa'i lus la lhag par chags pa de'i bdag nyid dang de dang 'brel pa dang des bcings pa dang; de'i rjes su 'brel pa dang de'i rjes su mthun pa dang de'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir zang zing dang bcas par blta'o /
yāvanti saraṇāni tāvanti sāmiṣāṇi /
āmiṣayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ nirāmiṣaṃ kati nirāmiṣāṇi kimarthaṃ nirāmiṣaparīkṣā 		'thab pa dang bcas pa ji snyed par zang zing dang bcas pa yang de snyed do /
bdag zang zing dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zang zing med pa yin /
zang zing med pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zang zing med par brtag ce na /
sāmiṣaviparyayeṇa nirāmiṣam zang zing dang bcas pa las bzlog pa ni zang zing med pa'o /
yāvantyaraṇāni tāvanti nirāmiṣāṇi 'thab pa med pa ji snyed par zang zing med pa yang de snyed do /
āmiṣaviyuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ gredhāśritaṃ kati gredhā śritāni kimarthaṃ gredhāśritaparīkṣā 		bdag zang zing dang bral bar mngon par zhin pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zhen pa rten pa yin /
zhen pa rten pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zhen pa rten par brtag ce na /
yadrūpān rāgadveṣamohānāgamya pañcakāmaguṇānadhyavasyati tadātmato 'pi tatsambandhato 'pi tabdandhato 'pi tadanubandhato 'pi tadānukulyato 'pi tadanvayato 'pi gredhāśritaṃ draṣṭavyam 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi ngo bo gang la brten nas /
'dod pa'i yon tan ldan rnams la lhag par chags pa de'i bdag nyid dang de dang 'brel pa dang des bcings pa dang de'i rjes su 'brel pa dang de'i rjes su mthun pa dang de'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir zhen pa brten par blta'o /
yāvanti sāmiṣāṇi tāvantigredhāśritāni /
gredhayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ naiṣkramyāśritaṃ kati naiṣkramyāśritāni kimarthaṃ naiṣkramyāśritaparīkṣā 		zang zing dang bcas pa ji snyed par zhen pa rten pa'ang de snyed do /
bdag zhen pa dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na mngon par 'byung ba rten pa yin /
mngon par 'byung ba rten pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir mngon par 'byung ba rten par brtag ce na /
gredhāśritaviparyayeṇa naiṣkramyāśritam zhen pa rten pa las bzlog pa ni mngon par 'byung ba rten pa'o /
yāvantinirāmiṣāṇi tāvantinaiṣkramyāśritāni /
gredhaviyuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ kati saṃskṛtāni kimarthaṃ saṃskṛtaparīkṣā yasyotpā do 'pi prajñāyate vyayo 'pi sthityanyathātvamapi tatsarvaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ draṣṭavyam 		zang zing med pa ji snyed par mngon par 'byung ba rten pa'ang de snyed do /
bdag zhen pa dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na 'dus byas yin /
'dus byas rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'dus byas su brtag ce na /
gang la skye ba dang 'jig pa dang gnas pa dang gzhan du 'gyur ba yang snang ba de 'dus byas su blta'o /
sarvāṇi saṃskṛtāni sthāpayitvā dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśam /
anityātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig ma gtogs pa thams cad kyang 'dus byas dag go /
bdag mi rtag par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathamasaṃskṛtaṃ katyasaṃskṛtāni kimarthamasaṃskṛtaparīkṣā ji ltar na 'dus ma byas yin /
'dus ma byas rnams ni du zhig /
saṃskṛtaviparyayeṇāsaṃskṛtam /
dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaḥ /
nityātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		ci'i phyir 'dus ma byas su brtag ce na /
'dus byas las bzlog pa ni 'dus ma byas so /
chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag rtag par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
anupādāna skandhāḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vaktavyamasaṃskṛtaṃ vaktavyam ? nye bar len pa'i phung po ma yin pa rnams 'dus byas zhes bya'am /
'dus ma byas zhes bya zhe na /
na saṃskṛtaṃ nāsaṃskṛtaṃ vaktavyam 'dus byas kyang ma yin 'dus ma byas kyang ma yin zhes bya'o /
tatkasya hetoḥ de ci'i phyir zhe na /
karmakleśānabhisaṃskṛtatāmupādāya na saṃskṛtam las dang nyon mongs pas mngon par 'dus ma byas pa nyid kyi phyir 'dus byas ma yin no /
kāmakārasaṃmukhī vimukhībhāvatāmupādāya nāsaṃskṛtam /
yaduktaṃ bhagavatā dvayamidaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ cāsaṃskṛtaṃ ceti [?] /
tatkathaṃ yenārthena saṃskṛtaṃ na tenārthenāsaṃskṛtam 		'dod pa bzhin du byed pas mngon du phyogs pa dang rgyab kyis lta ba'i dngos po nyid kyi phyir 'dus ma byas kyang ma yin no /
bcom ldan 'das kyis 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas zhes bya ba 'di ni gnyis so zhes gang gsungs pa ji lta bu zhe na /
don gang gis 'dus byas su gyur pa'i don des 'dus ma byas ma yin no /
yenāsaṃskṛtaṃ na tenārthena saṃskṛtamityatra nayo draṣṭavyaḥ /
kathaṃ laukikaṃ kati laukikāni kimarthaṃ laukikaparīkṣā /
traidhātukaparyāpannaṃ laukikaṃ lokottara pṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ ca tatpratibhāsam 		don gang gis 'dus ma byas su gyur pa'i don de nyid kyis 'dus byas ma yin te /
tshul 'di ni 'di ltar blta bar bya'o /
bam po gnyis pa /
ji ltar na 'jig rten pa yin /
'jig rten pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'jig rten par brtag ce na /
khams gsum par gtogs pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes la thob pa de ltar snang ba yang 'jig rten pa'o /
skandhānāmekadeśaḥ pañcadaśa dhātavaḥ daśāyatanāni trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ phung po rnams kyi phyogs gcig dang khams bco lnga dang skye mched bcu dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs so /
ātmani lokābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ lokottaraṃ kati lokottarāṇi kimarthaṃ lokottaraparīkṣā /
traidhātukapratipakṣo ' viparyāsaniṣprapañcanirvikalpatayā ca nirvikalpaṃ lokottaram 		bdag la 'jig rten du mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na 'jig rten las 'das pa yin /
'jig rten las 'das pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das par brtag ce na /
khams gsum pa'i gnyen po rnam par mi rtog pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ste /
phyin ci log dang spros pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
api khalu paryāyeṇa loko ttarapṛṣṭalabdhaṃ lokottaram yang rnam grangs su na /
'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes la thob pa yang yin te /
alaukikā śritatāmupādāya 'jig rten las 'das pa la rten pa'i phyir ro /
skandhānāmekadeśaḥtrayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayoḥ /
kevalātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		phung po rnams dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'ba' zhig tu mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na byung ba yin /
kathamutpannaṃ katyutpannāni kimarthamutpannaparīkṣā byung ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir byung bar brtag ce na /
atīta pratyutpannamutpakṣam 'das pa dang da ltar byung ba ni byung ba'o /
sarvepāmekadeśaḥ aśāśvatātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag ther zug ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
api khalu caturviśatividhamutpannam yang byung ba ni rnam pa nyi shu rtsa bzhi ste /
ādyutpannaṃ prabandhotpannam upacayotpannam āśrayotpannaṃ vikārotpannaṃ paripākotpannaṃ hānyutpannaṃ viśeṣotpannaṃ prabhāsvarotpannam aprabhāsvarotpannaṃ saṃkrāntyutpannaṃ savījotpannam avījotpannaṃ pratibimbavibhutvanidarśanotpannaṃ paraṃparotpannaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgotpannaṃ saṃyogaviyogotpannam avasthāntarotpannaṃ cyutopapādotpannaṃ saṃvarttavivarttotpannaṃ pūrvakālotpannaṃ maraṇakālo tpannam antarotpannaṃ pratisandhikālotpannaṃ ca dang po byung ba dang rgyun gyis byung ba dang rgyas pa las byung ba dang rten byung ba dang 'gyur bar byung ba dang yongs su smin pa byung ba dang nyams par byung ba dang khyad par du byung ba dang 'od gsal bar byung ba dang 'od gsal ba ma yin par byung ba dang kun tu 'gro bas byung ba dang sa bon dang bcas par byung ba dang sa bon ma yin par byung ba dang gzugs brnyan dang dbang 'byor ba dang nges par bstan pa'i phyir byung ba dang gcig nas gcig tu byung ba dang skad cig zhig nas byung ba dang phrad pa dang bral bas byung ba dang gnas skabs gzhan du byung ba dang 'chi 'pho ba dang skye bas byung ba dang 'jig pa dang 'chags pas byung ba dang sngon gyi dus na byung ba dang 'chi ba'i dus na byung ba dang bar du byung ba dang nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i dus na byung ba'o /
ji ltar na ma byung ba yin /
kathamanutpannaṃ katyanutpannāni kimarthamanutpannaparīkṣā /
anāgatamasaṃskṛtaṃ cānutpannam 		ma byung ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir ma byung bar brtag ce na /
ma 'ongs pa dang 'dus ma byas ni ma byung ba'o /
sarvepāmekadeśaḥ /
śāśvatātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag ther zug tu mngon par zhen pa spang pa'i phyir ro /
api khalūtpannaviparyayeṇānutpannam yang byung ba las bzlog pa ni ma byung ba'o /
ji ltar na 'dzin pa yin /
kathaṃ grāhakaṃ kati grāhakāṇi kimarthaṃ grāhakaparīkṣā /
rūpīndriyaṃ cittacaitasikāśca dharmā grāhakaṃ draṣṭavyam /
trayaḥ skandhā rūpasaṃskāraskandhaikadeśaḥ dvādaśa dhātavaḥ ṣaḍāyatanāni dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaśca /
bhoktātmā bhiniveśalājanārtham 		'dzin pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'dzin par brtag ce na /
dbang po gzugs can dang sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ni 'dzin par blta ste /
phung po gsum dang gzugs dang 'du byed kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang khams bcu gnyis dang skye mched drug dang; chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag za ba por mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
api khalu aprāptagrāhakaṃ prāptagrāhakaṃ svalakṣaṇavarttamānapratyeka grāhakaṃ svasāmānyalakṣaṇasarvakālaṃ sarvaviṣayagrāhakaṃ ca grāhakaṃ draṣṭavyam yang ma phrad pa dang phrad nas 'dzin pa dang da ltar gyi rang gi mtshan nyid so sor 'dzin pa dang rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dus thams cad pa'i yul thams cad 'dzin pa yang 'dzin par blta'o /
sāmagrīvijñāna samutpattitāmupādāya /
prajñaptikaśca grāhakavādo draṣṭavyaḥ 		tshogs na rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i phyir btags pa can yang 'dzin par smra'o zhes blta bar bya'o /
ji ltar na gzung ba yin /
kathaṃ grāhyaṃ kati grāhyāni kimarthaṃ grāhyaparīkṣā /
yattāvad grāhakaṃ grāhyamapi tat 		gzung ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gzung bar brtag ce na /
'dzin pa gang yin pa gzung ba yang de yin no /
syādgrāhyaṃ na grāhakaṃ grāhakagocara evārthaḥ gzung ba yin la 'dzin pa ma yin pa yang yod de /
'dzin pa'i spyod yul nyid kyi don to /
sarvāṇi grāhyāṇi viṣayātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ vahirmukhaṃ kati bahirmukhāni kimarthaṃ bahirmukha parīkṣā 		thams cad do /
bdag la yul du mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na phyi rol tu bltas pa yin /
phyi rol tu bltas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir phyi rol tu bltas par brtag ce na /
