kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ bahirmukhaṃ sthāpayitvā buddhaśāsane śrutamayacintāmayatadanudharmaparigṛhītāṃ ścittacaitasikān dharmān sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba dang de'i rjes su mthun pa'i chos bsgrubs pas yongs su bsdus pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ma gtogs par 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa ni phyi rol tu bltas pa'o /
ca tvāro dhātavaḥ dve cāyatane tadanyeṣāṃ caikadeśaḥ khams bzhi dang skye mched gnyis dang de las gzhan pa dag gi phyogs gcig go /
avītarāgātmābhiniveśatyājanartham /
kathamantarmukhaṃ katyantarmukhāni kimarthamantamukhaparīkṣā 		bdag 'dod chags dang bral ba ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na nang du bltas pa yin /
nang du bltas pa rnams ni du zhig /
bahirmukhaviparyayeṇāntarmukham /
catuto dhātūn sthāpayitvā dve cāyatane tadanyeṣāmekadeśaḥ /
vītarāgātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		ci'i phyir nang du bltas par brtag ce na /
phyi rol tu bltas pa las bzlog pa ni nang du bltas pa'o /
khams bzhi dang skye mched gnyis ma gtogs pa de las gzhan pa dag gi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'dod chags dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ kliṣṭaṃ kati kliṣṭāni kimarthaṃ kliṣṭaparīkṣā ji ltar na nyon mongs pa can yin /
nyon mongs pa can rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir nyon mongs pa can du brtag ce na /
akuśalaṃ nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ ca kliṣṭam mi dge ba dang bsgribs la lung du ma bstan pa ni nyon mongs pa can no /
nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ punaḥ sarvatragamanaḥ saṃprayuktaḥ kleśo rūpārūpya pratisaṃyuktaśca /
skandhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātunāṃ caturṇṇāmāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ /
kleśayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathamakliṣṭaṃ katyakliṣṭāni kimarthamakliṣṭaparīkṣā 		bsgribs la lung du ma bstan pa ni kun tu 'gro ba'i yid dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i lhan cig skyes pa'i 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi'i phyogs gcig go /
bdag nyon mongs pa dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na nyon mongs pa can ma yin /
nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa rnams ni du zhig /
kuśalamanivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ vākliṣṭam /
aṣṭau dhātavaḥ aṣṭāyatanāni skandhānāṃ śeṣāṇāṃ ca dhātvāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ /
kleśaviyuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathamatītaṃ katyatītāni kimarthamatītaparikṣā 		ci'i phyir nyon mongs pa can ma yin par brtag ce na /
dge ba dang ma bsgribs la lung du ma bstan pa ni nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'o /
khams brgyad dang skye mched brgyad dang phung po dang khams dang skye mched lhag ma rnams kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag nyon mongs pa dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na 'das pa yin /
'das pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'das par brtag ce na /
utpannaniruddha lakṣaṇato 'pi hetuphalopayo gato 'pi saṃkleśavyavadānakāritra samatikrāntito 'pi hetuparigrahavināśato 'pi phalasvalakṣaṇabhāvābhāvatāpi smarasaṃkalpanimittatohapi apekṣāsaṃkleśanimittato 'pi upekṣāvyavadānanimittato 'pi atitaṃ draṣṭavyam sarveṣāmekedaśaḥ /
pravarttakātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		byung la 'gags pa'i mtshan nyid dang rgyu dang 'bras bu spyad zin pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar byed pa las yang dag par shin tu 'das pa dang rgyu yongs su bzung nas zhig pa dang 'bras bu dang rang gi mtshan nyid yod pa dang med pa dang dran pa dang dran pa'i kun tu rtog pa'i mtshan ma dang ltos pas kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan ma dang btang snyoms kyis rnam par byang ba'i mtshan ma yin pas kyang 'das par blta'o /
thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'jug par byed par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na ma 'ongs pa yin /
kathamanāgataṃ katyanāgatāni kimarthamanāgataparīkṣā ma 'ongs pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir ma 'ongs par brtag ce na /
hetau satya nutpannato 'pi alabdhasva lakṣaṇato 'pi hetuphalānupayogato 'pi saṃkleśavyavadānabhāvā pratyupasthānato 'pi hetusvabhā vābhāvato 'pi abhinandanāsaṃkleśa nimittato 'pi abhinandanāvyavadānanimittato 'pyanāgataṃ draṣṭavyam rgyu yod kyang ma byung ba dang rang gi mtshan nyid ma thob pa dang rgyu dang 'bras bu ma spyad pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i dngos po nye bar mi gnas pa dang rgyu dang rang gi mtshan nyid yod pa dang med pa dang mngon par dga' bas kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan ma dang mngon par dga' ba med pas rnam par byang ba'i mtshan ma yin pas kyang ma 'ongs par blta'o /
sarveṣāmekadeśaḥ /
pravarttakātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ pratyutpannaṃ kati pratyutpannāni kimarthaṃ pratyutpannaparīkṣā 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'jug par byed par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na da ltar byung ba yin /
da ltar byung ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir da ltar byung bar brtag ce na /
utpannāniruddha lakṣaṇato 'pi hetuphalopayogānupayogato 'pi saṃkleśa vyavadānapratyupasthānato 'pi atītānāgata bhāva nimittato 'pi kāritrapratyupasthānato 'pi pratyutpannaṃ draṣṭavyam byung lam 'gags pa'i mtshan nyid dang rgyu dang 'bras bu spyad zin pa dang spyad ma zin pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba nye bar gnas pa dang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs par rab tu gzhag pa'i rgyu dang byed pa nye bar gnas pas kyang da ltar byung bar blta'o /
sarveṣāmekadeśaḥ /
pravarttakātmābhiniveśatyājanārthameva 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'jug par byed par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
atītānāgatapratyutpannaṃ punaḥ kathāvastu na nirvāṇam 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba ni gtam gyi gzhi yin no /
mya ngan las 'das pa ni ma yin te /
pratyātmavedanīyatayā nirabhilapyatāmupādāya bhutabhavyavarttamānaparihā rādhiṣṭhānatāṃ copādaya so so rang gis rig par bya ba dang brjod du med pa nyid dang byung ba dang 'byung ba dang da ltar gyi tha snyad kyi gnas ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ kuśalaṃ kati kuśalāni kimarthaṃ kuśalaparīkṣā /
svabhāvato 'pi sambandhato 'pi anubandhato 'pi utthānato 'pi paramārthato 'pi upapattilābhato 'pi prayogato 'pi puraskārato 'pi anugrahato 'pi parigrahato 'pi pratipakṣato 'pyupaśamato 'pi niṣyandato 'pi kuśalaṃ draṣṭavyam 		ji ltar na dge ba yin /
dge ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir dge bar brtag ce na /
ngo bo nyid dang 'brel ba dang rjes su 'brel ba dang slong ba dang don dam pa dang skye bas 'thob pa dang sbyor ba dang mdun du bya ba dang phan 'dogs pa dang yongs su 'dzin pa dang gnyen po dang nye bar zhi ba dang rgyu mthun pas kyang dge bar blta'o /
skandhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātunāṃ caturṇāṃ cāyatānānāṃ pradeśaḥ /
dharmayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi'i phyogs so /
bdag chos dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
svabhāvataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat śraddhādaya ekādaśa caitasikā dharmāḥ ngo bo nyid kyis dge ba gang zhe na /
dad pa la sogs pa sems las byung ba'i chos bcu gcig go /
sambandhataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat /
tatsaṃprayuktā dharmāḥ 		'brel pas dge ba gang zhe na /
de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i chos rnams so /
anubandhataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat rjes su 'brel pas dge ba gang zhe na /
teṣāmeva yā vāsanā /
utthanataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat 		de dag nyid kyi bag chags gang yin pa'o /
slong bas dge ba gang zhe na /
tatsamutthāpitaṃ kāyakarmma vākkarmma des kun nas bslang ba'i lus dang ngag gi las so /
paramārthataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat don dam pas dge ba gang zhe na /
tathatā /
upapattilābhataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat 		de bzhin nyid do /
skye bas 'thob pas dge ba gang zhe na /
eṣāmeva kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ pūrvābhyāsamāgamyaṃ tadrūpā vipākābhinirvṛtiḥ dge ba'i chos 'di dag nyid sngon goms par byas pa la brten nas /
de'i ngo bo'i rnam par smin pa mngon par 'grub pa ste /
yathā teṣveva prakṛtyā apratisaṃkhyāya rūciḥ saṃtiṣṭhate des de dag nyid la rang bzhin gyis so sor ma brtags par 'dod pa kun tu gnas pa'o /
prayogataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat sbyor bas dge ba gang zhe na /
satpuruṣasaṃsevāmāgamya saddharmaśravaṇaṃ yoniśo manaskāraṃ dharmānudharmapratipattiṃ kuśalasya bhāvanā skyes bu dam pa la brten pa dang dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa la brten nas dge ba bsgom pa'o /
mdun du bya bas dge ba gang zhe na /
gang de bzhin gshegs pa'am /
puskārataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat mchod rten nam /
gzugs su byas pa'am /
yattathāgataṃ vā puraskṛtya caitye vā pustagate vā citragate dharmaṃ vā puraskṛtya dharmādhiṣṭhāni pustake pūjākarma /
anugrahataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat 		ri mor bris pa mdun du byas sam /
chos sam chos kyi gzhi glegs bam mdun du byas te mchod pa'i las byed pa'o /
phan 'dogs pas dge ba gang zhe na /
yaccaturbhi saṃgrahavastubhiḥ sattvānanugṛṇhataḥ gang bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi po dag gis sems can la phan 'dogs pa'o /
parigrahataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat /
yaddānamayena puṇyakriyāvastunā vā śīlamayena vā svargopapattiparigraho vā āḍhyo kulopapattiparigraho vā vyavadānānukūlyaparigraho vā pratipakṣataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat /
yo vidūṣaṇāpratipakṣaḥ ādhārapratipakṣa dūrobhāva pratipakṣaḥ viṣkambhaṇāpratipakṣaḥ visaṃyogapratipakṣaḥ kleśāvaraṇapratipakṣaḥ jñeyāvaraṇapratipakṣaḥ 		yongs su 'dzin pas dge ba gang zhe na /
gang sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po'am /
tshul khrims las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos pos mtho ris su skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa'am /
phyug po dang rigs mthon por skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa'am /
rnam par byang ba'i rjes su mthun pa yongs su 'dzin pa'o /
gnyen pos dge ba gang zhe na /
gang rnam par sun 'byin pa gnyen po dang spong ba gnyen po dang gzhi gnyen po dang thag sring ba gnyen po dang rnam par gnon pa gnyen po dang bral ba gnyen po dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po'o /
upaśamataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat nye bar zhi bas dge ba gang zhe na /
yattatparyādāya rāgaprahāṇaṃ paryādāya dveṣaprahāṇaṃ paryādāya mohaprahāṇaṃ paryādāya sarvakleśaprahāṇaṃ saṃjñāvedayitanirodhaḥ sopadhiśeṣo nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhāturapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaṃ ca gang 'dod chags mtha' dag spong ba dang zhe sdang mtha' dag spong ba dang gti mug mtha' dag spong ba dang nyon mongs pa mtha' dag spong ba dang 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa dang phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings dang mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'o /
niṣyandataḥ kuśalaṃ katamat /
upaśamaprāptasya tadādhipatyena vaiśeṣikā guṇā abhijñādayo laukikalokottarāḥ sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇāḥ 		rgyu mthun pas dge ba gang zhe na /
nye bar zhi ba thob pa de'i dbang gis yon tan khyad par can 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i mngon par shes pa la sogs pa thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa rnams so /
kathamakuśalaṃ katyakuśalāni kimarthamakuśalaparīkṣā ji ltar na mi dge ba yin /
mi dge ba rnams ni du zhig /
svabhāvato 'pi saṃbandhato 'pi anubandhato 'pi utthānato 'pi paramārthato 'pi upapattilābhato 'pi prayogato 'pi puraskārato 'pi upaghātato 'pi parigrahato 'pi vipakṣato 'pi paripanthato 'pyakuśalaṃ draṣṭavyam ci'i phyir mi dge bar brtag ce na /
ngo bo nyid dang 'brel pa dang rjes su 'brel pa dang slong ba dang don dam pa dang skye bas 'thob pa dang sbyor ba dang mdun du bya ba dang gnod pa byed pa dang yongs su 'dzin pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang bar du gcod pas kyang mi dge bar blta'o /
skandhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātunāṃ caturṇṇāmāyatanānāṃ pradeśaḥ phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi'i phyogs so /
adharmayuktātmābhini veśatyājanārtham /
svabhāvato 'kuśalaṃ katamat /
manaḥsaṃprayuktaṃ rūpārūpyāvacaraṃ ca kleśaṃ sthāpayitvā tadanyaḥ klaśopakleśo duścaritasamutthāpakaḥ 		bdag chos ma yin pa dang ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ngo bo nyid kyis mi dge ba gang zhe na /
yid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba'o /
sambandhato 'kuśalaṃ katamat 'brel bas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
taireva kleśopakleśaiḥ saṃprayuktā dharmāḥ /
anubandhato 'kuśalaṃ katamat 		nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa de dag nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i chos rnams so /
rjes su 'brel bas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
teṣāmeva vāsanā de dag nyid kyi bag chags so /
utthānato 'kuśalaṃ katamat samutthāpitaṃ kāyavākkarma /
paramārthato 'kuśalaṃ katamat 		slong bas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
des kun nas bslang ba'i lus dang ngag gi las so /
don dam par mi dge ba gang zhe na /
sarvasaṃsāraḥ 'khor ba thams cad do /
upapattilābhato 'kuśalaṃ katamat skye bas 'thob pas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
yathāpi tadakuśalā bhyāsa stūdapo vipāko 'bhinivarttate yenākuśala eva rūciḥ santiṣṭhate mi dge ba goms par byas pas de'i ngo bo'i rnam par smin pa mngon par 'grub pa ste /
des mi dge ba nyid la 'dod pa kun tu gnas pa'o /
prayogato 'kuśalaṃ katamat sbyor bas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
yathāpi tadasatpuruṣasaṃsevāmāgamyasaddharmaśravaṇamayoni śomanaskāraṃ kāyena duścaritaṃ carati vācā manasā duścarītaṃ carati skyes bu dam pa ma yin pa la brten pa dang dam pa'i chos ma yin pa nyan pa dang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa la brten nas /
lus kyis nyes par spyad pa spyod pa dang ngag dang yid kyis nyes par spyad pa spyod pa'o /
puraskārato 'kuśalaṃ katamat /
yathāpi tadanyatamānyatamaṃ devanikāyasanniśrayaṃ puraskṛtya hiṃsāpūrvakaṃ vā kudṛṣṭipūrvakaṃ vā caityaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati tatra vā pūjākarma prayojayati yatra mahān janakāyo 'puṇyena yujyate 		mdun du bya bas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
lha'i ris gang yang rung ba la brten pa mdun du byas nas /
'tshe ba sngon du btang ba'am /
lta ba ngan pa sngon du btang nas lha rten byed pa dang gang du skye bo phal po che bsod nams ma yin pas sbyor ba der mchod pa'i las la sbyor ba'o /
upaghātato 'kuśalaṃ katamat gnod par byed pas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
yathāpi tatsattveṣu kāyena vācā manasā mithyā pratipadyate 'di lta ste /
sems can rnams la lus dang ngag dang yid kyis log par spyod pa'o /
parigrahato 'kuśalaṃ katamat /
yathā tatkāyena duścaritaṃ caritvā vācā manasā duścaritaṃ caritvā durgatau vā sugatau vā aniṣṭaṃ phalaṃ gṛṇhātyakṣepakaṃ vā paripūrakaṃ vā 		yongs su 'dzin pas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
lus kyis nyes par spyod pa spyad pa'am /
ngag dang yid kyis nyes par spyod pa spyod pas ngan 'gro'am bde 'gror 'bras bu mi 'dod pa'i 'phel pa'am /
yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'dzin pa'o /
vipakṣato 'kuśalaṃ katamat mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis mi dge ba gang zhe na /
ye pratipakṣavipakṣā dharmāḥ gnyen po'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi chos gang yin pa dag go /
pari panthato 'kuśalaṃ katamat ye kuśalāntarāyikā dharmāḥ bar du gcod pas mi dge ba gang zhe na /
dge ba'i bar chad byed pa'i chos gang yin pa dag go /
kathamavyākṛtaṃ katyavyākṛtāni kimarthamavyākṛtaparīkṣā ji ltar na lung du ma bstan pa yin /
lung du ma bstan pa rnams ni du zhig /
svābhāvato 'pi sambandhato 'pi anubandhato 'pi utthānato 'pi paramārthato 'pi upapattilābhato 'pi prayogato 'pi puraskārato 'pi anugrahato 'pi upabhogato 'pi parigrahato 'pi pratipakṣato 'pi upaśamato 'pi niṣyandato 'pi avyākṛtaṃ praṣṭhavyam ci'i phyir lung du ma bstan par brtag ce na /
ngo bo nyid dang 'brel pa dang rjes su 'brel pa dang slong ba dang don dam pa dang; skye bas 'thob pa dang sbyor ba dang mdun du bya ba dang phan 'dogs pa dang nye bar spyod pa dang yongs su 'dzin pa dang gnyen po dang nye bar zhi ba dang rgyu mthun pas kyang lung du ma bstan par blta'o /
aṣṭau dhātavaḥ aṣṭāvāyatanāni śeṣāṇāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ /
dharmādharmaviyuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		khams brgyad dang skye mched brgyad dang phung po dang khams dang skye mched lhag ma rnams kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag la chos dang chos ma yin pa dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
svabhāvato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat ngo bo nyid kyis lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
aṣṭau rūpīṇi dhātvāyatanāni sasaṃprayogaṃ manojīvitendriyaṃ nikāyasabhāgo nāma kāyapadakāyavyañjanakāyāśca khams dang skye mched gzugs can brgyad dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'i yid dang srog gi dbang po dang ris mthun pa dang ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs so /
sambandhato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
aduṣṭāprasannacittasya taireva nāmapadavyañjanakāyaiḥ parigṛhītāḥ cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ 		'brel pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
sdang ba yang ma yin /
dang ba yang ma yin pa'i sems su gyur pa'i ming dang tshig dang yi ge de dag nyid kyis yongs su zin pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
anubandhato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat rjes su 'brel pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
teṣāmevābhilāpavāsanā de dag nyid kyis brjod pa'i bag chags so /
utthānato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat slong bas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
tatparigṛhītaiścittacaitasikairdharmairya tsamutthāpitaṃ kāyavākkarma de dag nyid kyis yongs su zin pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams kyis gang kun nas bslang ba'i lus dang ngag gi las so; /
paramārthato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
ākāśamapratisaṃkhyānirodhaśca 		don dam par lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
nam mkha' dang so sor brtags pa ma yin pas 'gog pa'o /
upapattilābhato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
akuśalānāṃ kuśalasāsravāṇāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ vipākaḥ 		skye bas 'thob pa'i lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
mi dge ba'i chos rnams dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'o /
prayogato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat akliṣṭākuśalacetasa airyāpathikaṃ śailpasthānikaṃ ca sbyor bas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
nyon mongs pa can yang ma yin pa dang dge ba yang ma yin pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i spyod lam dang bzo'i gnas so /
puraskārato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
yathāpi tadanyatamānyatamaṃ devanikāyasanniśrayaṃ puraskṛtya hiṃsākudṛṣṭi vivarjitaṃ caityaṃ vā pratiṣṭhāpayati pūjākarma vā prayojayati yatra mahājanakāyo na puṇyaṃ prasavati nāpuṇyam 		mdun du bya bas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
lha'i ris gang yang rung ba la brten pa mdun du byas nas /
'tshe ba'am lta ba ngan pa rnam par spangs te /
lha rten byed pa dang gang du skye bo phal po che bsod nams kyang mi bskyed la bsod nams ma yin pa'ang mi bskyed par lha rten 'dzugs pa'o /
anugrahato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat phan 'dogs pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
yathāpi taddāsabhṛtakakarmakareṣu putradāreṣu vā aduṣṭāprasannacitto dānaṃ dadāti bran dang gla mi dang las byed pa rnams dang bu dang chung ma rnams la sdang ba yang ma yin /
dang ba yang ma yin pa'i sems kyis sbyin pa byin pa'o /
upabhogato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
yathāpi tadapratisaṃkhyākliṣṭacitto bhogānbhuṃkte 		nye bar spyad pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
so sor brtags pa ma yin pa /
nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i sems kyis longs spyod dmas spyad pa'o /
parigrahato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat /
yathāpi tacchilpasthānasyābhyastatvādāyatyāṃ tadrūpaṃ mātmabhāvaparigrahaṃ karoti yena laghu ladhveva teṣu śilpasthāneṣu śikṣāniṣṭhāṃ gacchati 		yongs su 'dzin pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
bzo'i gnas la goms pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa na de'i ngo bo'i lus yongs su 'dzin par byed pa ste /
de la myur bar myur bar bzo'i gnas de dag la bslab pa mthar phyin par 'gyur pa'o /
pratipakṣato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat gnyen pos lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
yathāpi tat pratisaṃkhyāya bhaiṣajyaṃ niṣevate 'di lta ste /
so sor ma brtags pas sman bsten pa'o /
upaśamato 'vyākṛtaṃ katamat nye bar zhi bas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
rūpārūpyavacaraḥ kleśaḥ śamathopagūḍhatāmupādāya gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa ste /
zhi gnas dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
niṣyandato 'vyākṛmataṃ katamat nirvāṇacittasahajam /
api khalu nidarśanataḥ kuśalamapyakuśalamapyavyākṛtamapi draṣṭavyam 		rgyu mthun pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na /
sprul pa'i sems dang lhan cig skyes pa'o /
yang bstan pas kyang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan par blta ste /
tatpunaḥ katamat /
yadbuddhāḥ paramapāramiprāptāśca bodhisattvā nidarśayanti sattvānāmanugrahārthaṃ na tu teṣāṃ tatra tathā kācit pariniṣpattiḥ /
kathaṃ kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ kati kāmapratisaṃyuktāni kimarthaṃ kāmapratisaṃyuktaparīkṣā 		de yang gang zhe na /
gang sangs rgyas rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i pha rol tu son pa rnams kyis sems can la phan gdags pa'i phyir ston pa ste /
de na de dag de bzhin du yongs su grub pa ni gang yang med do /
ji ltar na 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa yin /
'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan par brtag ce na /
avītarāgasya sāsravakuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaṃ kāmaprati saṃyuktaṃ draṣṭavyam 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa ni 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa blta'o /
catvāro dhātavo dve cāyatane tadanyeṣāṃ ca skandhadhātvāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ khams bzhi dang skye mched gnyis dang de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi phyogs gcig go /
kāmāvītarāgātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ rūpapratisaṃyuktāni kimarthaṃ rūpapratisaṃyuktaparīkṣā 		bdag 'dod pa la 'dod chags dang ma bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na gzugs dang rab tu ldan pa yin /
gzugs dang rab tu ldan pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gzugs dang rab tu ldan par brtag ce na /
kāmavītarāgasya rūpāvītarāgasya kuśalāvyakṛtaṃ rūpapratisaṃyuktaṃ draṣṭavyam 'dod pa la 'dod chags dang bral la /
gzugs la 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa ni gzugs dang rab tu ldan par blta'o /
caturo dhātūna dve cāyatane sthāpayitā tadanyeṣāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ /
kāmavītarāgātmabhiniveśatyājanārtham 		khams bzhi dang skye mched gnyis ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag 'dod pa la 'dod chags dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa yin /
kathamārūpapyapratisaṃyuktaṃ katyārūpyapratisaṃyuktāni kimarthamārūpyapratisaṃyuktāparīkṣā gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan par brtag ce na /
rūpavītarāgasyārūpyāvītarāgasya kuśalāvyākṛtaṃ vārūpyapratisaṃyuktaṃ draṣṭavyam gzugs la 'dod chags dang bral la /
gzugs med pa la 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa ni gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa blta'o /
caturṇāṃskandhānāṃ dvayo ścāyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ /
rūpavītarāgātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		phung po bzhi dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs so /
bdag gzugs la 'dod chags dang bral bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
vairāgyaṃ punarekadeśavairāgyaṃ skalavairāgyaṃ prativedhavairāgyamupaghātavairāgyaṃ samudghātavairāgyaṃ ca draṣṭavyam /
api khalu daśa vairāgyāṇi 		'dod chags dang bral ba nyid kyang /
phyogs gcig las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang mtha' dag las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang; rtogs pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang gnod pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang legs par bton pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid du blta'o /
yang 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid bcu ste /
prakṛtivairāgyamupaghātavairāgyamupastambhavairāgyaṃ samutkarṣavairāgyaṃ sammohavairāgyaṃ pratipakṣavairāgyaṃ parijñāvairāgyaṃ prahāṇi vairāgyaṃ sottaravairāgyaṃ niruttaravairāgyam /
prakṛtivairāgyaṃ katamat /
duḥkhāyāṃ vedanāyāṃ duḥkhasthānīyeṣu ca dhamaṣu yā pratikulatā /
upaghātavairāgyaṃ katamat /
maithunaprayuktasya dāhavigame yā pratikūlatā 		rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang gnod pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang nye bar brtan pas 'dod chags bral ba nyid dang phul du byung bas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang rmongs pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid do /
rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang yongs su shes pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang spad bas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang gong ma dang bcas pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid dang gong na med pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid do /
rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba dang; sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba'i gnas kyi chos rnams la gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
gnod pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
'khrig pa la zhugs pa gdung ba dang bral nas gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
upastambhavairāgyaṃ katamat nye bar brtan pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
subhuktavato mṛṣṭe 'pi bhojane yā pratikūlatā 'brangs par bzos pa zas zhim po la yang gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
samutkarṣavairāgyaṃ katamat phul du byung bas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
uccataraṃ sthānaṃ prāptava to nirhīne sthāne yā pratikūlatā thabs shin tu chen po thob pa /
thabs dma' ba la gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
sammohavairāgyaṃ katamat rmongs pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
bālānāṃ nirvāṇe yā pratikūlatā /
pratipakṣa vairāgyaṃ katamat 		byis pa rnams mya ngan las 'das pa la gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
gnyen pos 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
laukikena vā lokottareṇa vā mārgeṇa yatkleśaprahāṇam 'jig rten pa'am 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi nyon mongs pa spong ba gang yin pa'o /
parijñāvairāgyaṃ katamat /
pratilabdhadarśanamārgasya traidhātuke yā pratikūlatā 		yongs su shes pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
mthong ba'i lam thob pa /
khams gsum pa la gang mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa nyid do /
prahāṇivairāgyaṃ katamat spong bas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
bhūmau bhūmau kleśān prajahato yā pratikūlatā sa dang sar nyon mongs pa rab tu spong ba'i mi mthun par 'dzin pa nyid gang yin pa'o /
sottaravairāgyaṃ katamat /
laukikānāṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ ca yadvairāgyam 		gong ma dang bcas pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
'jig rten pa dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang yin pa'o /
niruttaraṃ vairāgyaṃ katamat gong na med pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang zhe na /
yad buddhabodhisattvānāṃ vairāgyaṃ sarvasattvahitasukhādhiṣṭhānatā mupādāya /
kathaṃ śaikṣaṃ kati śaikṣāṇi kimarthaṃ śaikṣaparīkṣā 		sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gang yin pa ste /
sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na slob pa yin /
slob pa rnams ni du zhib /
ci'i phyir slob par brtag ce na /
mokṣaprayuktasya kuśalaṃ śaikṣaṃ draṣṭavyam thar pa la brtson pa'i dge ba ni slob par blta'o /
skandhānā daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ caturṇāṃ cāyatanāmekadeśaḥ /
mokṣaprayuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi'i phyogs so /
bdag thar pa la brtson par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na mi slob pa yin /
kathamaśaikṣaṃ katyaśaikṣāṇi kimarthamaśaikṣaparīkṣā /
śikṣāyāṃ niṣṭhāgatasya kuśalamaśaikṣaṃ draṣṭavyam 		mi slob pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir mi slob par brtag ce na /
bslab pa mthar phyin pa'i dge ba ni mi slob par blta'o /
skandhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ caturṇāṃ cāyatanānāṃ pradeśaḥ /
bhuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ naivaśaikṣānāśaikṣaṃ kati naivaśaikṣānāśaikṣāni kimarthaṃ naivaśaikṣānāśaikṣa parīkṣā /
pṛthagjanasya kuśalākuśalāvyakṛtaṃ śaikṣasya kliṣṭāvyākṛtamaśaikṣasya cāvyākṛtamasaṃskṛtaṃ ca naivaśaikṣānāśaikṣaṃ draṣṭavyam 		phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi'i phyogs so /
bdag grol bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na slob pa yang ma yin mi slob pa yang ma yin /
slob pa yang ma yin mi slob pa yang ma yin pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir slob pa yang ma yin mi slob pa yang ma yin par brtag ce na /
so so'i skye bo'i dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang slob pa'i nyon mongs pa can dang lung du ma bstan pa dang mi slob pa'i lung du ma bstan pa dang 'dus ma byas ni slob pa yang ma yin mi slob pa yang ma yin par blta'o /
aṣṭau dhātavo 'ṣṭā vāyatanāni tadanyeṣāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ pradeśaḥ khams brgyad dang skye mched brgyad dang de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi phyogs gcig go /
amuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ darśanaprahātavyaṃ kati darśanaprahātavyāni kimarthaṃ darśanaprahātavyaparīkṣā /
parikalpitā kliṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ vicikitsādṛṣṭisthānaṃ ye ca dṛṣṭau vipratipannāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ yacca dṛṣṭyā samutthāpitaṃ kāyavā kkarma sarvaṃ cāpāyikaṃ skandhadhātvāyatanaṃ darśanaprahātavyaṃ draṣṭavyam 		bdag grul ba ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na mthong ba bas spang bar bya ba yin /
mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir mthong bas spang bar bya bar brtag ce na /
nyon mongs pa can gyi lta ba kun tu brtags pa rnams dang the tshom dang lta ba'i gnas dang lta ba la log par zhugs pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa gang yin pa dag dang gang yang lta bas kun nas bslang ba'i lus kyi las dang dag gi las dang ngan song ba'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched thams cad ni mthong ba spang bar bya bar blta'o /
sarveṣāmekadeśaḥ /
darśanasaṃpannātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ bhāvanāprahātavyaṃ kati bhāvanāprahātavyāni kimarthaṃ bhāvanāprahātavyaparīkṣā /
labdhadarśanamārgasya tadūrdhvaṃ darśanaprahātavyaviparyayeṇa sāsravā dharmāḥ 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag mthong ba phun sum tshogs par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na bsgom pas spang bar bya ba yin /
bsgom pas spang bar bya ba rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir bsgom pas spang bar bya bar brtag ce na /
mthong ba'i lam thob pa de yan chad kyi mthong bas spang bar bya ba las bzlog pa zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams so; /
sarveṣāmekadeśaḥ /
bhāvanāsaṃpannātmābhiniveśatyajanārtham 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag sgom pa phun sum tshogs par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathamaprahātavyaṃ katyaprahātavyāni kimamarthamaprahātavyaparīkṣā ji ltar na spang bar bya ba ma yin /
spang bar bya ba ma yin pa rnams ni du zhig /
anāsravamaprahātavyaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ sthāpayitvā nirvedhabhāgīyam ci'i phyir spang bar bya ba ma yin par brtag ce na /
zag pa med pa ni spang bar bya ba ma yin par blta'o /
skaṃdhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ caturṇāṃ cāyatanānāṃ pradeśaḥ /
siddhātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		des par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa ma gtogs par phung po rnams dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs so /
bdag grub par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ pratītyasamutpannaṃ kati pratītyasamutpannāni kimarthaṃ pratītyasamutpannaparīkṣā ji ltar na rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yin /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba rnams ni du zhig /
lakṣaṇato 'pyaṅgavibhāgato 'pi aṅgasamāsato 'pyaṅgapratyayatvavyavasthānato 'pi aṅgakarmavyavasthānato 'pi aṅgasaṃkleśasaṃgrahato 'pi arthato 'pi gāmbhīryato 'pi prabhedato 'pyanulomapratiloma to 'pi pratītyasamutpannaṃ draṣṭavyam ci'i phyir rten cing 'brel par 'byung bar brtag ce na /
mtshan nyid dang yan lag rnam par dbye ba dang yan lag mdor bsdu pa dang yan lag rkyen nyid du rnam par gzhag pa dang yan lag gi las rnam par gzhag pa dang yan lag kun nas nyon mongs par bsdu ba dang don dang zab pa dang rab tu dbye ba dang lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pas kyang rten cing 'brel par 'byung bar blta'o /
sarvāṇi dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaṃ sthāpayitvā chos kyi khams dang chos kyi skye mched kyi phyogs gcig ma gtogs pa thams cad do /
ahetuviṣamahetukātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ /
nirīhapratyayotpattitāmupādāya anityapratyayotpattitāmupādāya samarthapratyayotpattitāmupādāya 		bdag dang chos rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa'i rgyu las byung ba mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
mtshan nyid kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
g yo ba med pa'i rkyen las byung ba dang mi rtag pa'i rkyen las byung ba dang nus pa'i rkyen las byung ba'i phyir ro /
kathamaṅgavibhāgataḥ yan lag rnam par dbye bas ji ltar bu zhe na /
dvādaśāṅgāni /
dvādaśāṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ avidyā saṃskārā vijñānaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā tṛṣṇopadānaṃ bhavo jāti rjarāmaraṇaṃ ca 		yan lag bcu gnyis rnams te /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yan lag bcu gnyis ni /
ma rig pa dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa dang ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba dang sred pa dang sred pa dag /
len pa dang srid pa dang skye ba dang rga shi'o /
kathamaṅgasamāsato 'pi /
ākṣepakāṅgamākṣiptāṅgamabhinirvarttakāṅgamabhinirvṛttyaṅgaṃ ca /
ākṣepakāṅgaṃ katamat /
avidyā saṃskārā vijñānaṃ ca 		yan lag mdor bsdu bas ji ltar bu zhe na /
'phen pa'i yan lag dang 'phags pa'i yan lag dang mngon par 'grub par byed pa'i yan lag dang mngon par grub pa'i yan lag go /
'phen pa'i yan lag gang zhe na /
ma rig pa dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa'o /
ākṣiptakāṅgaṃ katamat /
nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca 		'phags pa'i yan lag gang zhe na /
ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba'o /
abhinrivarttakāṅgaṃ katamat /
tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavaśca /
abhinirvṛttyaṅgaṃ katamat /
jāti rjarāmaraṇaṃ ca 		mngon par 'grub par byed pa'i yan lag gang zhe na /
sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa'o /
mngon par grub pa'i yan lag gang zhen /
skye ba dang rga shi'o /
kathamaṅgapratyayatvavyavasthānataḥ /
vāsanāto 'pyāvedhato 'pi manasikārato 'pi sahabhāvato 'pyāṅgānāṃ pratyayatvavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ tacca yathāyogam 		yan lag rkyen nyid du rnam par bzhag pas ji ltar bu zhe na /
bag chags dang shugs dang yid la byed pa dang lhan cig 'byung bas kyang yan lag rnams rkyen nyid du rnam par gzhag par rig par bya ste /
de yang ci rigs su sbyar ro /
kathamaṅgakarmavyavasthānataḥ yan lag gi las rnam par gzhan pas ji ltar bu zhe na /
avidyā kiṃkarmikā /
bhave ca sattvān saṃmohayati pratyayaśca bhavati saṃskārāṇām 		ma rig pa ci'i las can zhe na /
srid pa la sems can rnams rmongs par byed pa dang 'du byed rnams kyi rkyen kyang yin no /
saṃskārāḥ kiṃkarmakāḥ /
gatiṣu ca sattvān vibhajanti pratyayāśca bhavanti vijñānavāsanāyāḥ 		'du byed ci'i las can zhe na /
'gro ba rnams su sems can dag rnam par 'byed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i bag chags kyi rkyen kyang yin no /
vijñānaṃ kiṃ karmakam /
sattvānāṃ karmabandhaṃ ca dhārayati pratyayaśca bhavati nāmarūpasya 		rnam par shes pa ci'i las can zhes na /
sems can rnams kyi las 'ching ba 'dzin pa dang ming dang gzugs kyi rkyen kyang yin no /
nāmarūpaṃ ca kiṃkarmakam /
ātmabhāvaṃ ca sattvān grāhayati pratyayaśca bhavati ṣaḍāyatanasya 		ming dang gzugs ci'i las can zhe na /
sems can rnams lus len du 'jug pa dang skye mched drug gi rkyen kyang yin no /
ṣaḍāyatanaṃ kiṃkarmakam /
ātmabhāvaparipūriṃ ca sattvān grāhayati pratya yaśca bhavati sparśasya 		skye mched drug ci'i las can zhe na /
sems can rnams lus yongs su rdzogs par len du 'jug pa dang reg pa'i rkyen kyang yin no /
sparśaḥ kiṃkarmakaḥ /
viṣayopabhoge ca sattvān pravarttayati pratyayaśca bhavati vedanāyāḥ 		reg pa ci'i las can zhe na /
yul gyi longs spyod la sems can rnams 'dzud pa dang tshor ba'i rkyen kyang yin no /
vedanā kiṃkarmikā /
janmopabhoge ca sattvān pravarttayati pratyayaśca bhavati tṛṣṇāyāḥ 		tshor ba ci'i las can zhe na /
skye ba'i longs spyod la sems can rnams 'dzud pa dang sred pa'i rkyen kyang yin no /
tṛṣṇā kiṃkarmikā /
janmani ca sattvānākarṣayati pratyayaśca bhavati upādānasya 		sred pa ci'i las can zhe na /
sems can rnams kyi skye ba 'dren pa dang len pa'i rkyen kyang yin no /
upādānaṃ kiṃkarmakam /
punarbhavādānārthaṃ sopādānaṃ ca sattvānāṃ vijñānaṃ karoti pratyayaśca bhavati bhavasya 		len pa ci'i las can zhe na /
yang srid pa len pa'i phyir sems can rnams kyi rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa dang bcas par byed pa dang srid pa'i rkyen kyang yin no /
bhavaḥ kiṃkarmakaḥ srid pa ci'i las can zhe na /
punarbhave ca sattvānabhimukhīkaroti pratyayaśca bhavati jāteḥ yang srid par sems can rnams mngon du phyogs par byed pa dang skye ba'i rkyen kyang yin no /
jātiḥ kiṃkarmikā skye ba ci'i las can zhe na /
nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanasparśavedanānupūrvyā ca sattvānabhinirvarttayati pratyayaśca bhavati jarāmaraṇasya /
jarāmaraṇaṃ kiṃkarmakam 		ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang rig pa dang tshor ba'i rim gyis sems can rnams mngon par 'grub par byed pa dang rga shi'i rkyen kyang yin no /
rga shi ci'i las can zhe na /
punaḥ punarvayaḥpariṇāmena jīvitapariṇāmena ca sattvānyojayati yang dang yang na tshod 'gyur ba dang srog 'gyur ba la sems can rnams sbyor ba'o /
kathamaṅgasaṃkle śasaṃgrahataḥ yan lag kun nas nyon mongs par bsdu bas ji lta bu zhe na /
yā cāvidyā yā ca tṛṣṇā yaccopādānamityayaṃ saṃkleśasaṃgrahaḥ /
ye ca saṃskārā yacca vijñānaṃ yaśca bhava ityayaṃ karmasaṃkleśasaṃgrahaḥ 		ma rig pa gang yin pa dang sred pa gang yin pa dang len pa gang yin pa 'di ni nyon mongs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs par bsdu'o /
'du byed gang yin pa dang rnam par shes pa gang yin pa dang srid pa gang yin pa 'di ni las kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa bsdu'o /
śeṣāṇi janmasaṃkleśasaṃgrahaḥ lhag ma rnams ni tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs par bsdu'o /
kathamarthataḥ /
niḥkartṛkārthaḥ pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ /
sahetukārthaḥ niḥsattvārthaḥ parataṃtrārthaḥ nirohakārthaḥ anityārthaḥ kṣaṇikārthaḥ hetuphalaprabandhānupacchedārthaḥ anurūpahetuphalārthaḥ vicitrahetuphalārthaḥ pratiniyatahetuphalārthaśca pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ 		don gyis ji lta bu zhe na /
byed pa po med pa'i don ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don dang rgyu dang bcas pa las byung ba'i don dang sems can med pa'i don dang gzhan gyi dbang gi don dang g yo ba med pa'i don dang mi rtag pa'i don dang skad cig pa'i don dang rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyud rgyun mi 'chad pa'i don dang rgyu dang 'bras bur mthun pa'i don dang rgyu dang 'bras bu sna tshogs kyi don dang rgyu dang 'bras bu so sor nges pa'i don ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don to /
kathaṃ gāmbhīryataḥ zab pas ji lta bu zhe na /
hetu gāmbhīryato 'pi lakṣaṇagāmbhīryato 'pi utpattibhāgāmbhīryato 'pi sthitigāmbhīryato 'pi vṛttigāmbhīryato 'pi gāmbhīryaṃ draṣṭavyam rgyus zab pa dang mtshan nyid kyis zab pa dang skye bas zab pa dang gnas pas zab pa dang 'byung bas zab pas kyang zab par blta'o /
yang rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba skad cig pa yang yin la /
api khalu kṣaṇikaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ sthititaścopalabhyate gnas par yang dmigs /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba g yo ba med pa'i rkyen las 'byung ba'ang yin la /
nirīhakapratyayaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ samarthapratyayaścopalabhyate /
niḥsattvaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ attvataścopalabhyate /
na svato na parato na dvābhyāṃ na svayaṃkārāparakārāhetusamutpannaḥ /
ato 'pi gambhīraḥ 		nus pa'i rkyen las 'byung bar yang dmigs /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba sems can med pa yang yin la sems can du yang dmigs /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba byed pa po yang med la /
las dang 'bras bu chud mi za bar yang dmigs shing bdag las ma yin gzhan las ma yin gnyi ga las ma yin /
rang gi byed pa dang gzhan gyi byed pa dang rgyu med pa las byung ba yang ma yin te /
de'i phyir zab pa'o /
kathaṃ prabhedataḥ /
vijñānotpattiprabhedataḥ cyutyupapattiprabhedataḥ vāhyaśasyotpattiprabhedataḥ saṃvarttavivarttaprabhe dattaḥ āhāropastambhaprabhedataḥ iṣṭāniṣṭagativibhāgaprabhedataḥ viśuddhiprabhedataḥ prabhāvaprabhedataśca prabhedo draṣṭavyaḥ 		rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rab tu dbye ba dang 'chi 'pho dang skye ba'i rab tu dbye ba dang phyi'i lo tog 'byung ba'i rab tu dbye ba dang 'jig pa dang chags pa'i rab tu dbye ba dang zas kyis brtan pa'i rab tu dbye ba dang 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa'i 'gro ba rnam par 'byed pa'i rab tu dbye ba dang rnam par dag pa'i rab tu dbye ba dang mthu stobs kyi rab tu dbye bas kyang rab tu dbye bar blta'o /
kathamanulomapratilomataḥ /
saṃkleśā nulomapratilomato 'pi vyavadānānulomapratilomato 'pi pratītyasamutpādasyānulomapratilomanirddeśo draṣṭavyaḥ 		lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pas ji lta bu zhe na /
kun nas nyon mongs pa'i lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pa dang rnam par byang ba'i lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pas kyang /
atha mūlavastuni tridhamaparicchede prathame tṛtīyo bhāgaḥ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pa bstan par blta'o /
ji ltar na rkyen yin /
kathaṃ pratyayaḥ kati pratyayāḥ kimarthaṃ pratyayaparīkṣā /
hetuto 'pi samanantarato 'pi ālambanato 'pyadhipatito 'pi pratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ 		rkyen rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir rkyen du brtag ce na /
rgyu dang de ma thag pa dang dmigs pa dang bdag pos kyang rkyen du blta'o /
sarvāṇi pratyayaḥ /
ātmahetukadharmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		thams cad kyang rkyen du blta'o /
chos bdag gi rgyu las byung bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
hetupratyayaḥ katamaḥ /
ālayavijñānaṃ kuśalavāsanā ca /
api khalu svabhāvato 'pi prabhedato 'pi sahāyato 'pi saṃpratipattito 'pi paripanthato 'pi parigrahato 'pi hetupratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ 		rgyu'i rkyen gang zhe na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang dge ba'i bag chags so /
yang ngo bo nyid dang rab tu dbye ba dang grogs dang mthun par rtogs pa dang rgyas pa dang bar du gcod pa dang yongs su 'dzin pas kyang rgyu'i rkyen du blta'o /
kathaṃ svabhāvataḥ ngo bo nyid kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
kāraṇaṃ hetusvabhāvataḥ byed rgyu ste rgyu'i ngo bo nyid do /
kathaṃ prabhedataḥ rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na /
utpattikāraṇaṃ tadyathā cakṣuḥ sāmagrī vijñānasya 'byung ba'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na rnam par shes pa'i ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs pa lta bu'o /
sthitikāraṇaṃ tadyathā āhāro bhūtānāṃ sattvānāṃ saṃbhavaiṣiṇāṃ ca gnas pa'i byed rgyu ni dper na sems can byung ba rnams dang 'byung bar 'dod pa rnams kyi zas lta bu'o /
dhṛtikāraṇaṃ tadyathā pṛthivī sattvānām rten pa'i byed rgyu ni dper na sems can rnams kyis lta bu'o /
gsal ba'i byed rgyu ni /
prakāśakāraṇaṃ tadyathā pradīpo rūpāṇām dper na gzugs rnams kyi sgron ma lta bu'o /
vikārakāraṇaṃ tadyathā agnirindhanasya 'gyur ba'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na shing gi me lta bu'o /
viyogakāraṇaṃ tadyathā dātraṃ chedyasya 'bral ba'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na rnga bar byed pa'i zor ba lta bu'o /
pariṇatikāraṇaṃ tadyathā śilpasthānā dikaṃ hiraṇyādīnām bsgyur ba'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na gser la sogs pa'i bzo'i gnas la sogs pa lta bu'o /
saṃpratyayakāraṇaṃ tadyathā dhūmo 'gneḥ yid ches pa'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na me'i du ba lta bu'o /
saṃpratyāyanakāraṇaṃ tadyathā pratijñāhetudṛṣṭāntāḥ sādhyasya yid ches par byed pa'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na bsgrub pa'i dam bca' ba dang gtan tshigs dang dpe rnams lta bu'o /
prāpaṇakāraṇaṃ tadyathā mārgo nirvāṇasya 'thob pa'i byed rgyu ni /
dper na mya ngan las 'das pa'i lam lta bu'o /
vyavahārakāraṇaṃ tadyathā nāma saṃjñā dṛṣṭiśca tha snyad kyi byed rgyu ni /
dper na ming dang mtshan ma dang mthong ba lta bu'o /
apekṣākāraṇaṃ yadapekṣya yatrārthitvamutpadyate ltos pa'i byed rgyu ni /
gang la ltos nas gang don du gnyer ba 'byung ba ste /
tadyathā jighatsāmapekṣya bhojane dper na bkres pa la ltos nas zas lta bu'o /
ākṣepakāraṇaṃ vidūraḥ pratyayaḥ /
tadyathā avidyā jarāmaraṇasya 		'phen pa'i byed rgyu ni /
rgyang ring po'i rkyen te /
dper na rga shi'i ma rig pa lta bu'o /
abhinirvṛttikāraṇamāsannaḥ pratyayaḥ mngon pa 'grub pa'i byed rgyu ni nye ba'i rkyen te /
tadyathā avidyā saṃskārāṇām dper na 'du byed rnams kyi ma rig pa lta bu'o /
parigrahakāraṇaṃ tadanyaḥ pratyayaḥ yongs su 'dzin pa'i byed rgyu ni de las gzhan pa'i rkyen te /
tadyathā kṣetrodakapāsyā ? vāpyādikaṃ sasyodayasya dper na lo tog 'byung ba'i zhing dang chu dang lud la sogs pa lta bu'o /
āvāhakakāraṇamanukūlataḥ pratyayaḥ chud par byed pa'i byed rgyu ni mthun pa'i rkyen te /
tadyathā samyagrājāsevā rājārādhanāyāḥ dper na rgyal po mnyes par byed pa'i phyir rgyal po la legs par brten pa lta bu'o /
prati niyamakāraṇaṃ pratyayavaicitryam so sor nges pa'i byed rgyu ni rkyen sna tshogs pa ste /
tadyathā pañcagatipratyayāḥ pañcānāṃ gatīnām dper na 'gro ba lnga po dag gi 'gro ba lnga'i rkyen lta bu'o /
sahakārikāraṇaṃ pratyayasāmagrī /
tadyathā vijñānasya indriyamaparibhinnaṃ viṣaya ābhāsagataḥ tajjaśca manaskāraḥ pratyupasthitaḥ 		lhan cig byed pa'i byed rgyu ni rkyen rnams tshogs pa ste /
dper na rnam par shes pa'i dbang po ma ma nyams pa dang yul yang snang ba dang de skyed pa'i yid la byed pa yang nye bar gnas pa lta bu'o /
virodhi kāraṇamantarāyaḥ mi mthun pa'i byed rgyu ni bar chad byed pa ste /
tadyathā sasyasyāśaniḥ dper na lo tog la ser ba lta bu'o /
avirodhakāraṇamanantarāyaḥ /
tadyathā tasyaivāntarāyasyābhāvaḥ 		mi mthun pa ma yin pa'i byed rgyu ni bar chad mi byed pa ste /
dper na bar chad byed pa de nyid med pa lta bu'o /
kathaṃ sahāyataḥ grogs kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
ye dharmāḥ sahabhāvenotpadyante nānyatamavaikalyena chos gang dag grogs yod na 'byung gi gang yang rung ba ma tshang na ma yin pa ste /
'di lta ste /
tadyathā bhūtāni bhautikañca 'byung ba rnams dang 'byung ba las gyur pa'o /
kathaṃ saṃpratipattitaḥ mthun par rtogs pas ji lta bu zhe na /
ye dharmāḥ sahabhāvenālambanaṃ saṃpratipadyante nānyatamavaikalyena chos gang dag lhan cig 'byung ba dmigs pa mthun par rtogs kyi /
gang yang rung ba ma tshang na ma yin pa ste /
tadyathā cittaṃ caitasikāśca 'di lta ste /
sems dang sems las byung ba rnams so /
kathaṃ puṣṭitaḥ /
pūrvabhāvitānāṃ kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yā aparānte uttarottarā puṣṭatarā puṣṭatamā pravṛttiḥ 		rgyas pas ji lta bu zhe na /
sngon dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos bsgoms pa rnams phyi ma'i mthar gong nas gong du shin tu rgyas pa dang mchog tu rgyas par 'byung ba gang yin pa'o /
kathaṃ paripanthataḥ bar du gcod pas ji lta bu zhe na /
yā kleśānāmanyatamabhāvanayānyatamaprabandhapuṣṭidṛḍhīkāraḥ /
nirvāṇasantānadūrīkaraṇāya 		gang mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyud thag bsring ba'i phyir nyon mongs pa gang yang rung ba'i rgyun rgyas par brtan par byed pa'o /
kathaṃ parigrahataḥ yongs su 'dzin pas ji lta bu zhe na /
akuśalāḥ kuśalasāsravāśca dharmāḥ /
ātmabhāvaparigrahāya /
kathaṃ samanantarataḥ nairantaryasamanantarato 'pi sabhāgavisabhāgacittacaittotpattisamanantarato 'pi samanantarapratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ 		lus yongs su 'dzin pa'i phyir mi dge ba dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams so /
de ma thag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
rgyun mi 'chad par bar chad med pa dang mthun pa dang mi mthun pa la sems dang sems las byung ba 'byung ba'i de ma thag pas kyang de ma thag pa'i rkyen du blta'o /
kathamālambanataḥ /
paricchinnaviṣayālambanato 'pi aparicchinnaviṣayālambanato 'pi acitrīkāraviṣayālambano 'pi sacitrīkāraviṣayālambanato 'pi savastu śikṣālambanato 'pi avastukaviṣayālambanato 'pi vastvālambanato 'pi parikalpālambanatāpi viparyastālambanato 'pi aviparyastālambatopi savyāghātālambanato 'pi avyāghātālambanato 'pi ālambanapratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ 		dmigs pas ji lta bu zhe na /
yul yongs su chad pa'i dmigs pa dang yul yongs su ma chad pa'i dmigs pa dang yul la bkra bar 'dzin ba med pa'i dmigs pa dang yul la bkra bar 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa dang dngos po dang bcas pa'i yul gyi dmigs pa dang dngos po med pa'i yul gyi dmigs pa dang dngos po'i dmigs pa dang kun brtags pa'i dmigs pa dang phyin ci log gi dmigs pa dang phyin ci ma log pa'i dmigs pa dang thogs pa dang bcas pa'i dmigs pa dang thogs pa med pa'i dmigs pas kyang dmigs pa'i rkyen du blta'o /
kathamadhipatitaḥ /
pratiṣṭhādhipatīto 'pyāvedhādhipatito 'pi sahabhāvādhipa tito 'pi viṣayādhipatito 'pi prasavādhipatito 'pi sthānādhipatito 'pi phalopabhogādhipatito 'pi laukikaviśuddhya dhipatito 'pi lokottaraviśuddhya dhipatito 'pi adhipati pratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ 		bdag pos ji lta bu zhe na /
rten la dbang byed pa dang 'phen pa la dbang byed pa dang lhan cig 'byung ba la dbang byed pa dang yul la dbang byed pa dang skye bar dbang byed pa dang gnas par dbang byed pa dang 'bras bu la nye bar spyod par dbang byed pa dang 'jig rten pa'i rnam par dag pa la dbang byed pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa la dbang byed pas kyang bdag po'i rkyen du blta'o /
kathaṃ sabhāgatatsabhāgaṃ kati sabhāgatatsabhāgāni kimarthaṃ sabhāgatatsabhāgaparīkṣā /
vijñānāvirahitatatsādṛśyendriyaviṣayaprabandhotpattito 'pi vijñānavirahitasvasādṛśyaprabandhotpattito 'pi sabhāgatatsabhāgaṃ draṣṭavyam 		ji ltar na bsten pa mtshungs pa dang de dang mtshungs pa yin /
bsten pa mtshungs pa dang de dang mtshungs pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir bsten pa mtshungs pa dang de dang mtshungs par brtag ce na /
rnam par shes pa dang ma bral zhing de dang 'dra ba'i dbang po yul la rgyun tu 'byung ba dang rnam par shes pa dang bral zhing rang dang 'dra ba rgyun tu 'byung bas kyang bsten pa mtshungs pa dang de dang mtshungs par blta'o /
rūpaskandhaikadeśaḥ pañcarūpīṇi dhātvāyatanāni vijñānayuktāyuktātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang gzugs can gyi khams dang skye mched lnga'o /
bdag rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa dang me ldan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na zin pa yin /
kathamupāttaṃ katyupāttāni kimarthamupāttaparīkṣā /
vedanotpatyāśrayarūpa ta upāttaṃ draṣṭavyam 		zin pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zin par brtag ce na /
tshor ba 'byung ba'i gnas kyi gzugs ni zin par blta'o /
rūpaskandhaikadeśaḥ pañca rūpīṇi dhātvāyatanāni - caturṇāṃ caikadeśaḥ /
dehavaśavarttyā tmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang khams dang skye mched gzugs can lnga dang bzhi'i phyogs gcig go /
bdag lus la dbang bsgyur bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na dbang po yin /
kathamindriyaṃ katīndriyāṇi kimarthabhindriyaparīkṣā dbang po rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir dbang por brtag ce na /
viṣayagrahaṇādhipatito 'pi kuśalaprabandhādhipatito 'pi nikāyasabhāgasthānadhipatito 'pi śubhāśubhakarmaphalabhogādhipatito 'pi laukikavairāgyādhiopatito 'pi lokottaravairāgyādhipatito 'pi indriyaṃ draṣṭavyam yul la 'dzin par dbang byed pa dang rigs kyi rgyud la dbang byed pa dang ris mthun par gnas par dbang byed pa dang dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu la nye bar spyod par dbang byed pa dang 'jig rten gyi 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid la dbang byed pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid la dbang byed pas kyang dbang por blta'o /
vedanāskandho vijñānaskandha rūpasaṃskāraskandhaikadeśaḥ dvādaśa dhātavaḥ ṣaḍāyatanāni dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaśca /
ātmādhipatyabhiniveśatyājanārtham 		tshor ba'i phung po dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po dang gzugs dang 'du byed kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang khams bcu gnyis dang skye mched drug dang chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag dbang byed par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ duḥkhaduḥkhatā kati duḥkhaduḥkhatāni kimarthaṃ duḥkhaduḥkhatāparīkṣā ji ltar na sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid yin /
sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid du brtag ce na /
duḥkhavedanāsvalakṣaṇato 'pi duḥkhavedanīyadharmasvalakṣaṇato 'pi duḥkhaduḥkhatā draṣṭavyā sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba'i rang gi mtshan nyid dang sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi rang gi mtshan nyid kyis kyang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid du blta'o /
sarvepāmekadeśaḥ /
duḥkhitātmābhiniveśatyāja nārtham 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag sdug bsngal bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ viparīṇāmaduḥkhatā kati viparīṇāmaduḥkhatāni kimarthaṃ vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāparīkṣā ji ltar na 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid yin /
'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal rnams ni du zhig /
sukhavedanāvipariṇatisvalakṣaṇato 'pi sukhavedanīyadharmavipariṇatisvalakṣaṇato 'pi tatra cānunayacittavipariṇatito 'pi vipariṇāmaduḥkhatā draṣṭavyā ci'i phyir 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid du brtag ce na /
bde ba'i tshor ba 'gyur ba rang gi mtshan nyid dang bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos 'gyur ba rang gi mtshan nyid dang de la yang rjes su chags pas sems 'gyur bas kyang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid du blta'o /
sarvepāmekadeśaḥ /
sukhitātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ saṃskāraduḥkhatā kati saṃskāraduḥkhatāni kimarthaṃ saṃskāraduḥkhatāparīkṣā 		thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag bde bar mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid yin /
'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid du brtag ce na /
aduḥkhāsukhavedanā svalakṣaṇato 'pi aduḥkhāsukha vedanīyasvadharmalakṣaṇato 'pi tadubhayadauṣṭhulyaparigrahato 'pi dvayāvinirmokṣānityānubandhāyogakṣemato 'pi saṃskāraduḥkhatā draṣṭavyā sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin ba'i tshor ba'i rang gi mtshan nyid dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi rang gi mtshan nyid dang de gnyi ga'i gnas ngan len yongs su 'dzin pa dang de gnyi ga las ma thar ba mi rtag pa nyid kyis rjes su bcings pas grub pa dang bde ba ma yin pas kyang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid du blta'o /
skandhānāṃ trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayorekadeśaṃ sthāpayitvā sarvāṇi phung po rnams dang khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs gcig ma gtogs par thams cad do /
aduḥkhāsukhātmabhiniveśatyājanārtham /
kathaṃ savipākaṃ kati savipākāni kimarthaṃ savipākaparīkṣā /
akuśalaṃ kuśalasāsravaṃ ca savipākaṃ draṣṭavyam 		bdag sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na rnam par smin pa dang bcas pa yin /
rnam par smin pa dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir rnam par smin pa dang bcas par brtag ce na /
mi dge ba dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa ni rnam par smin pa dang bcas par blta'o /
skandhānāṃ daśānāṃ dhātunāṃ caturṇāṃ cāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ /
skandhopanikṣepakapratisaṃghāyakātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		phung po rnams dang khams bcu dang; skye mched bzhi'i phyogs gcig go /
bdag phung po 'jog par byed pa dang nying mtshams sbyor bar byed par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
vipākaḥ punarālayavijñānaṃ sasaṃprayogaṃ draṣṭavyam rnam par smin pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas par blta'o /
tadanyattu vipākajam /
kathamāhāraḥ katyāhārāḥ kimarthaṃ māhāraparīkṣā /
pariṇatito 'pi pāriṇāmikaḥ viṣayato 'pi vaiṣayikaḥ āśayato 'pyāśi ? śayikaḥ upādānato 'pyupādānikaḥ āhāro draṣṭavyaḥ 		de las gzhan pa dag ni rnam par smin pa las byung ba'o /
ji ltar na zas yin /
zas rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir zas su brtag ce na /
'jug pas kyang 'ju bas las gyur pa dang yul gyis kyang yul las gyur pa dang re bas kyang re ba las gyur pa dang len pas kyang len pa las gyur ba nyid ni zas su blta'o /
trayāṇāṃ skandhānāmekādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ pañcānāñcāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ phung po gsum dang khams bcu gcig dang skye mched lnga'i phyogs gcig go /
āhārasthitikātmabhiniveśatyajanārtham bdag zas kyis gnas par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
api khalvāhāro 'śuddhā śrayasthitikaḥ śuddhāśuddhāśrayasthitikaḥ śuddhāśrayasthitikaḥ sthitisāṃdarśinakaśca draṣṭavyaḥ yang zas ni ma dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa dang ma dag pa dang dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa dang dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa dang gnas par kun tu ston par yang blta'o /
ji ltar na gong ma dang bcas pa yin /
kathaṃ sottaraṃ kati sottarāṇi kimarthaṃ sottaraparīkṣā gong ma dang bcas pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gong ma dang bcas par brtag ce na /
saṃskṛtato 'saṃskṛtaikadeśataśca sottaraṃ draṣṭavyam 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi phyogs gcig gis kyang gong ma dang bcas par blta'o /
dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaṃ sthāpayitva sarvāṇi /
ātmadravyahīnābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig ma gtogs par thams cad do /
bdag rdzas ngan par mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ji ltar na gong na med pa yin /
kathamanuttaraṃ katyanuttarāṇi kimarthamanuttara parīkṣā gong na med pa rnams ni du zhig /
ci'i phyir gong na med par brtag ce na /
asaṃskṛtaikadeśato 'nuttaraṃ draṣṭavyam 'dus ma byas kyi phyogs gcig ni gong na med par blta'o /
dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaḥ /
ātmadravyāgrābhiniveśatyājanārtham 		chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go /
bdag rdzas kyi mchog tu mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
ityanena nayenāpramāṇaḥ prabhedanayaḥ de ltar na tshul 'dis rab tu dbye ba'i tshul tshad med do /
api khalu samāsataḥ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ prabhedastrividhaḥ yang mdor bsdu na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi rab tu dbye ba ni rnam pa gsum ste /
parikalpitalakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ vikalpitalakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ dharmatālakṣaṇaprabhedaśca kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba dang rnam par brtags pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba dang chos nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba'o /
tatra parikalpitalakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ de la kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣvātmeti vā sattvo jīvo jantuḥ poṣo pugdalo manujo mānava iti vā yatparikalpyate phung po khams dang skye mched rnams la bdag ce'am /
sems can dang srog dang skye ba po dang gso ba dang gang zag dang shed las skyes dang shed bu zhes gang kun tu rtog pa'o /
vikalpitalakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ rnam par brtags pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rang ru dbye ba gang zhe na /
tānyeva skandhadhātvāyatanāni phung po dang khams dang skye mched de dag nyid do /
dharmatālakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ chos nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
teṣveva skandhadhātvāyataneṣvātmābhāvaḥ sattvajīvajantupoṣapugdalamanujamānavānāmabhāvaḥ nairātmyāstitā /
api khalu caturvidhaḥ prabhedaḥ /
lakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ prakāraprabhevā ākṣayaprabhedaḥ santatiprabhedaśca 		phung po dang khams dang skye mched de dag nyid la bdag med cing /
sems can dang srog dang skye ba po dang gso ba dang gang zag dang shed las skyes dang shed bu med la; bdag med pa ni yod pa nyid do /
yang rab tu dbye ba rnam pa bzhi ste /
mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba dang rnam pas rab tu dbye ba dang lus kyis rab tu dbye ba dang rgyun gyis rab tu dbye ba'o /
lakṣaṇaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
pratyekaṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ svalakṣaṇa bhedaḥ phung po dang khams dang; skye mched rnams so so'i rang gi mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba'o /
prakāraprabhedaḥ /
teṣāmevaskandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ dravyamantaḥ prajñaptimantaḥ saṃvṛtimantaḥ paramārthamantaḥ rūpiṇo 'rūpiṇaḥ sanidarśanā anidarśanā ityevamādi yathānirddiṣṭaḥ 		rnam pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched de dag nyid kyi rdzas su yod pa dang btags pa'i yod pa dag /
kun rdzob tu yod pa dang don dam par yod pa dang gzugs can dang gzugs can ma yin pa dang bstan du yod pa dang bstan du med pa dang de la sogs pa'i ji skad bstan pa rnams so /
āśrayaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ lus kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
yāvantaḥ sattvāśrayā stāvanti skandhadhātvāyatanāni sems can rnams kyi lus ji snyed par phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyang de snyed do /
santatiprabhedaḥ katamaḥ rgyun gyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
pratikṣaṇaṃ skandhadhātvāyatānānāṃ pravṛttiḥ phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi skad cig re re 'byung ba'o /
lakṣaṇaprabhede kuśalaḥ kiṃ parijānāti /
ātmābhiniveśaṃ parijānāti /
prakāraprabhede kuśalaḥ kiṃ parijānāti 		mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas ci zhig yongs su shes she na /
bdag la mngon par zhen pa yongs su shes so /
rnam pas rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas ci zhig yongs su shes she na /
piṇḍasaṃjñāṃ parijānāti ril po'i 'du shes yongs su shes so /
āśrayaprabhede kuśalaḥ kiṃ parijānāti lus kyis rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas ci zhig yongs su shes she na /
akṛtābhyāgamakṛtavipraṇāśasaṃjñāṃ parijānāti ma byas pa dang phrad pa dang byas pa chud za ba'i 'du shes yongs su shes so /
santatiprabhede kuśalaḥ kiṃ parijāti rgyun gyis rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pas ci zhig yongs su shes she na /
sthirasaṃjñāṃ parijānāti /
api khalu ṣaḍvidhaḥ prabhedaḥ eṣāmeva skandhadhātvāyatananām 		brtan pa'i 'du shes yongs su shes so /
yang phung po dang khams dang skye mched 'di dag nyid kyi rab tu dbye ba rnam pa drug ste /
bahirmukhaprabhedaḥ antarmukhaprabhedaḥ āyata kālabhedaḥ paricchinnakālaprabhedaḥ tatkālaprabhedaḥ saṃdarśanaprabhedaśca phyi rol tu bltas pas rab tu dbye ba dang nang du bltas pas rab tu dbye ba dang rgyun ring ba'i dus kyis rab tu dbye ba dang dus yongs su chad pas rab tu dbye ba dang de'i dus kyis rab tu dbye ba dang kun tu ston pas rab tu dbye ba'o /
bahirmukhaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ phyi rol tu bltas pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
yadbhūyasā kāmāvacaraprabhedaḥ phal cher 'dod pa'i khams na spyod pas rab tu dbye ba'o; /
antarmukhaprabhedaḥkatamaḥ nang du bltas pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
sarvāḥ sāmādhibhūmayaḥ mnyam par gzhag pa'i sa pa thams cad do /
āyatakālaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ rgyun ring ba'i dus kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
pṛthagjanānām /
paricchinnakālaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ /
śaikṣāṇāṃ sthāpayitvā caramakṣaṇe skandhadhātvāyatanāni tadanyāni aśaikṣāṇām /
tatkālaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ 		so so'i skye bo rnams kyi'o /
dus yongs su chad pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
slob pa dang mi slob pa rnams kyi tha ma'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams ma gtogs pa'o /
de'i dus kyis rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
aśaikṣāṇāṃ caramakṣaṇe skandhadhātvāyatanāni mi slob pa rnams kyi tha ma'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams so /
saṃdarśanaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ kun tu ston pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
buddhānāṃ pāramiprāptānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ ca sanidarśanāni skandhadhātvāyatanāni /
atha mahāyānābhidharmasamuccayaśāstre mūlavastuni saṃgrahaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ /
saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ 		gang sangs rgyas rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i pha rol tu son pa rnams kyi phung po dang khams dang skye mched dag kun tu ston pa'o /
bsdus pa gang zhe na /
rnam pa bcu gcig tu blta ste /
saṃgraha ekādaśavidho draṣṭavyaḥ /
lakṣaṇasaṃgrahaḥ dhātusaṃgrahaḥ jātisaṃgrahaḥ avasthāsaṃgrahaḥ sahāyasaṃgrahaḥ deśasaṃgrahaḥ kālasaṃgrahaḥ ekadeśasaṃgrahaḥ sakalasaṃgrahaḥ itaretarasaṃgrahaḥ paramārthasaṃgrahaśca 		mtshan nyid kyis bsdus pa dang khams kyis bsdus pa dag /
rigs kyis bsdus pa dang gnas skabs kyis bsdus pa dang; grogs kyis bsdus pa dang phyogs kyis bsdus pa dang dus kyis bsdus pa dang phyogs gcig gis bsdus pa dang mtha' dag gis bsdus pa dang gcig gis gcig bsdus pa dang don dam pas bsdus pa'o /
lakṣaṇasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ mtshan nyid kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ pratyekaṃ svalakṣaṇenaiva tattatsaṃgrahaḥ phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi so so'i rang gi mtshan nyid gang yin pa dag nyid kyis de dag bsdus par blta'o /
dhātusaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ vījabhūtenālayavijñānena tattaddhātusaṃgrahaḥ 		khams kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gang yin pa de /
de dag gi khams bsdus pa'o /
jatisaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ rigs kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ vilakṣaṇānāmapi skandhadhātvāyatanairanyo 'nyasaṃgrahaḥ /
avasthāsaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
sukhāvasthānāṃ skandhadhātvāyatānānāṃ svalakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ 		phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams mtshan nyid tha dad kyang phung po'i don brtsan par byas shing khams dang skye mched kyi don brtsan par byas nas thams cad phan tshun gyis bsdus pa dag go /
gnas skabs kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
bde ba'i gnas skabs kyi phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams ni de dag nyid kyis bsdus pa'o /
duḥkhāvasthānāmaduḥkhāsukhāvasthānāmapi /
avasthāmupādāya /
sahāya saṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ 		de bzhin du sdug bsngal gyi gnas skabs dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i gnas skabs kyang de dag nyid kyis bsdus pa'o /
grogs kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
rūpaskandhaḥ tadanyaiḥskandhairanyo 'yaṃ sahāyataḥ sahāyaiḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ gzugs kyi phung po 'khor dang bcas pa ni de las gzhan pa'i phung po'i grogs su gyur pa rnams kyis grogs kyi bsdu bas bsdus pa'o /
evaṃ tadanye skandhā dhātava āyatanāni ca /
deśasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
pūrvadigāśritānāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ svalakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ /
evaṃ tadanyadiśāmapi skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ veditavyam 		de bzhin du de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la yang rig par bya'o /
phyogs kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
shar phyogs kyi phung po dang khams dang skye mched gang yin pa de rnams de dag nyid kyis bsdus pa'o /
de bzhin du de gzhan pa'i phyogs rnams la yang rig par bya'o /
kālasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ dus kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
atītānāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ svalakṣaṇena saṃgrahaḥ 'das pa'i phung po dang khams dang; skye mched rnams ni de dag nyid kyis bsdus pa'o /
anāgatānāṃ pratyutpannānāmapi skandhadhātvāyatanānām de bzhin du ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba rnams kyang de dag nyid kyis bsdus pa'o /
ekadeśasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
yāvanto dharmāḥ skandhadhātvāyatanaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ teṣāmanyatamasaṃgraha ekadeśa saṃgraho veditavyaḥ /
sakalasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
yāvanto dharmāḥ skandhadhātvāyatanaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ teṣāmaśeṣataḥ saṃgrahaḥ sakalasaṃgraho veditavyaḥ 		phyogs gcig gis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus pa'i chos ji snyed pa de dag gang yang rung bas bsdus pa ni phyogs gcig gis bsdus par rig par bya'o /
mtha' dag gis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus pa'i chos ji snyed pa de dag ma lus par bsdus pa ni mtha' dag gis bsdus par rig par bya'o /
itaretarasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ rūpaskandhasaṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ katyāyatanāni gcig gis gcig bsdus pa gang zhe na /
gzugs kyi phung po khams du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
daśānāmekadeśaḥ /
vedanāskandhasaṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ katyāyatanāni /
ekadeśaḥ /
yathā vedanāskandhastathāsaṃjñāsaṃskāra skandhau /
vijñānaskandhasaṃgrahe kati dhātavaḥ katyāyatanāni /
sapta dhātava ekamāyatanam /
cakṣurdhātusaṃgrahe kati skandhaḥ katyāyatanāni 		khams bcu dang skye mched bcu dang khams dang skye mched gcig gi phyogs gcig gis kyang bsdus so /
tshor ba'i phung po khams du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
khams dang skye mched gcig gi phyogs gcig gis bsdus so /
tshor ba'i phung po ji ltar 'du shes kyi phung po dang 'du byed kyi phung po'ang de bzhin no /
rnam par shes pa'i phung po khams du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
khams bdun dang skye mched gcig gis bsdus so /
mig gi khams phung po du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
rūpaskandhaikadeśa ekamāyatam gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang skye mched gcig gis so /
cakṣurdhātuvat śrotradhrāṇajivhākāya rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyabhrātavaḥ mig gi khams ji lta bar rna ba'i khams dang sna'i khams dang lce'i khams dang lus kyi khams kyang de bzhin no /
manodhātusaṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ katyāyatanāni gzugs kyi khams phung po du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
ekaḥ skandha ekamāyatanam /
dharmadhātusaṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ katyāyatanāni /
trayaḥ skandhā rūpaskandhaikadeśa ekamāyatanam /
cakṣurvijñānadhātusaṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ katyāyatanāni vijñānaskandhāmanaāyatanayorekadeśaḥ /
cakṣurvijñānavat śrotraghrāṃṇajivhākāyamanovijñānadhātavaḥ 		gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang skye mched gcig gis so /
gzugs kyi khams ji ltar bar sgra'i khams dang dri'i khams dang ro'i khams dang reg bya'i khams kyang de bzhin no /
mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams phung po du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
rnam par shes pa'i phung po dang yid kyi skye mched kyi phyogs gcig gis so /
mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams ji lta bar rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang; yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams kyang de bzhin no /
chos kyi khams phung po du dang skye mched du dag gis bsdus she na /
phung po gsum dang gcig gi phyogs gcig dang skye mched gcig gis bsdus so /
cakṣurāyatanasaṃgrahe kati skandhāḥkati dhātavaḥ mig gi skye mched phung po du dang khams du dag gis bsdus she na /
rūpaskandhaikadeśa eko dhātuśca /
yathā cakṣurāyatanaṃ tayā śrotraghrāṇajihvākāyarūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyāyatanāni /
manaāyatanasaṃgrahe kati skandhāḥ kati dhātavaḥ /
ekaḥ skandhaḥ sapta dhātavaḥ /
dharmāyatanasaṃgrahe katiskandhāḥ kati dhātavaḥ 		gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig dang khams gcig gis bsdus so /
mig gi skye mched ji lta bar rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi skye mched rnams dang gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya'i skye mched rnams kyang de bzhin no /
yid kyi skye mched phung po du dang khams du dag gis bsdus she na /
phung po gcig dang khams bdun gyis so /
chos kyi skye mched phung po du dang khams du dag gis bsdus she na /
trayāṇāṃ skandhānā mekadeśa eko dhātuśca phung po gsum dang gcig gi phyogs gcig dang khams gcig gis bsdus so /
tadvat tadanye dharmāḥ skandhadhātvāyatanairnirdṛśyante anye ca na skandhadhātvāyatanairnirddiśyante de bzhin du de las gzhan pa'i chos phung po bstan pa dang khams dang skye mched bstan pa gang yin pa de dag dang gang de bzhin du ma bstan pa 'di lta ste /
yathā dravyamantaḥ prajñāptimantaḥ saṃvṛtimantaḥ paramārthamanto jñeyā vijñeyā abhijñeyā rūpiṇo 'rūpiṇaḥ sanidarśanā anidarśanā ityevamādayaḥ pūrvaṃ nirdṛṣṭāḥ /
teṣāṃ yathāyogaṃ skandhadhātvāyatanairitaretarasaṃgraheveditavyaḥ /
paramārthasaṃgrahaḥ katamaḥ /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ tathatāsaṃgrahakuśalaḥ kamanuśaṃsa labhate 		rdzas su yod pa dang btags pa'i yod pa dang kun rdzob tu yod pa dang don dam par yod pa dang shes par bya ba dang rnam par shes par bya ba dang mngon par shes par bya ba dang gzugs can dang gzugs can ma yin pa dang bstan du yod pa dang bstan du med pa la sogs pa de dag kyang phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus par ji ltar mthun mthun du rig par bya ste /
de ni sngar bstan pa nyid do /
don dam pas bsdus pa gang zhe na /
gang phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi de bzhin nyid do /
ālambane 'bhisaṃkṣepānuśaṃsaṃ pratilabhate de ltar bsdus pa la mkhas pas phan yon ci zhig 'thob ce na /
yathā yathā ālambaneṣu cittābhisaṃkṣepaḥ tathā tathā kuśalamūlābhivṛddhiḥ /
atha mahāyānābhidharmasamuccayaśāstre mūlavastuni saṃprayogaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ /
saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ 		dmigs pa mngon par sdud pa'i phan yon 'thob ste /
ji lta ji ltar dmigs pa mngon par sdud pa de lta de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'phel lo /
mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
samāsataḥ saṃprayogaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ /
avinirbhāga saṃprayogaḥ miśrībhāva saṃprayogaḥ samavadhānasaṃprayogaḥ sahabhāvasaṃprayogaḥ kṛtyānuṣṭhānasaṃprayogaḥ saṃpratipattisaṃprayogaśca 		rnam pa drug tu blta ste /
tha dad pa med pas mtshungs par ldan pa dang 'dres par 'gyur pas mtshungs par ldan pa dang phrad pas mtshungs par ldan pa dang lhan cig 'byung bas mtshungs par ldan pa dang bya ba bsgrubs pas mtshungs par ldan pa dang mthun par rtogs pas mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
avinirbhāgasaṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ tha dad pa med pas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
sarveṣāṃ deśināṃ paramāṇuparyāpannānāṃ rūpāṃśikānāmanyonyamavinirbhāgaḥ /
miśrībhāvasaṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ 		rdul phra rab kyi phyogs la phyogs can thams cad tha dad pa med pa'o /
'dres par gyur pas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
paramāṇorūrdhvaṃ sarveṣāṃ deśināṃ rūpāṃśikānāṃ parasparaṃ miśrībhāvaḥ /
samavadhānasaṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ 		rdul phra rab las gong ma phyogs can rnams 'dres par gyur pa'o /
phrad pas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
deśināmeva samudāyināṃ rūpaparaṃparāyāṃ samavadhānam phyogs can 'dus pa rnams nyid phan tshun phrad pa'o /
sahabhāvasaṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ lhan cig 'byung bas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
ekasmin kāye skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ sahakālapravṛttiḥ samamutpatti sthitinirodhāḥ phung po dang khams dang skye mched gang yin pa dag lhan cig 'byung bas 'khod pa ste /
kṛtyānuṣṭhānasaṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ /
ekasmin kṛtyāṃnuṣṭhāne parasparaṃ saṃprayogaḥ 		skye ba gcig pa dang gnas pa'i ngang gcig pa dang 'gag pa gcig pa rnams so /
bya ba bsgrubs pas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
yathā dvayorbhikṣvoranyatarabhikṣoḥ kriyānuṣṭhāne anyo 'yaṃ saṃprayogaḥ 'di lta ste /
dge slong gnyis rtsod pa gang yang rung ba la mtshungs par zhugs pa lta bu'o /
saṃpratipatti saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ /
cittacaitasikānāmekasminnālambane 'nyonyaṃ saṃpratipattiḥ 		mthun par rtogs pas mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams dmigs pa gcig la mthun par rtogs pa'o /
sa saṃpratipattisaṃprayogaḥ punaranekārthakaḥ /
yathā parabhāvena saṃprayogaḥ na svabhāvena 		mthun par rtogs pas mtshungs par ldan pa de yang gzhan gyi dngos pos yin gyi bdag gi dngos pos ni ma yin no /
mthun pa gnyis yin gyi mi mthun pa gnyis ni ma yin no /
aviruddhyoḥ saṃprayogo na viruddhayoḥ dus 'dra ba gnyis yin gyi dus mi 'dra ba gnyis ni ma yin no /
sadṛśakālayoḥ saṃprayogo avisadṛśakālayoḥ sabhāgadhātubhūmikayoravisabhāgadhātubhūmikayoḥ /
sarvatragasaṃprayogastadyathā vedanā saṃjñācetanāsparśamanaskāra vijñānānām /
api khalu kliṣṭasarvatragaḥ saṃprayogo manasi caturṇṇāṃ kleśānām 		mthun pa'i khams dang sa pa gnyis yin gyi mi mthun pa'i khams dang sa pa gnyis ni ma yin no /
mtshungs par ldan pa kun tu 'gro ba ni 'di lta ste /
tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa dang reg pa dang yid la byed pa dang rnam par shes pa rnams so /
yang mtshungs par ldan pa kun tu 'gro ba nyon mongs pa can ni yid dang nyon mongs pa bzhi po rnams so /
kādācitkaḥ saṃprayogastadyathā citte śraddhādīnāṃ kuśalānāṃ rāgādīnāṃ ca kleśopakleśānām res 'ga' mtshungs par ldan pa ni 'di lta ste /
sems la dad pa la sogs pa dge ba rnams dang 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams so /
āvasthikaḥ saṃprayogaḥ sukhāyā vedanāyāḥ sasaṃprayogāyāḥ gnas skabs las gyur ba'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni bde ba'i tshor ba mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'i'o /
evaṃ duḥkhāyā aduḥkhāsukhāyāḥ /
avicchinnaḥ saṃprayogaḥ sacittikāyāmavasthāyām 		sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i yang de bzhin no /
rgyun mi 'chad par mtshungs par ldan pa ni lus sems dang bcas pa'i dus na'o /
vicchinnaḥ saṃprayogo 'cittakasamāpattyantaritasya rgyun chad pa'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni sems med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pas bar du chod pa'i'o /
bahirmukhaḥ saṃprayogo yadbhūyasā kāma pratisaṃyuktānāṃ cittacaitasikānām phyi rol tu bltas pa'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni 'dod pa'i khams dang rab tu ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams las phal cher ro /
antarmukhaḥ saṃprayogaḥ yadbhūyasā samāhitabhūmikānāṃ cittacaitasikānām nang du bltas pa'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni mnyam par gzhag pa'i sa ba rnams kyi sems dang sems las byung ba rnams las phal cher ro /
ucitaḥ saṃprayogaḥ pārthagjanikānāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ tadekatyānāṃ ca śaikṣāśaikṣāṇām 'dris pa'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni so so'i skye ba rnams kyi sems dang sems las byung ba rnams dang slob pa dang mi slob pa de dag las kyang kha cig gi'o /
anucitaḥ saṃprayogaḥ lokottarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāmādyataduttarāṇāṃ lokottarapṛṣṭhalabdhānāṃ ca ma 'dris pa'i mtshungs par ldan pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa rnams kyi sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi dang po dang de'i 'og ma rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes la thob pa rnams kyi'o /
saṃprayogakuśalaḥ kamanuśaṃsaṃ pratilabhate mtshungs par ldan pa la mkhas pas phan yon ci zhig 'thob ce na /
cittamātre vedanādīnāṃ sāṃkleśikānāṃvyāvadānikānāñca dharmāṇāṃ saṃprayogaṃ jānāti /
tacca jānanātmā vedayate saṃjānāti cetayate smarati saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate cetayatya bhiniveśaṃ prajahāti nairātmyamavatarati 		sems tsam la tshor ba la sogs pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos rnams kyis mtshungs par ldan pa dang ldan pa ma yin pa shes so /
de shes na bdag tshor bar byed do /
'du shes su byed do /
sems par byed do /
dran par byed do /
athābhidhamasamuccayaśāstre mūlavastuni samanvāgamaparicchedaścaturthaḥ kun nas nyon mongs so /
rnam par byang ngo zhes mngon par zhen pa spangs zhing bdag med pa la 'jug go /
samanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ ldan pa gang zhe na /
lakṣaṇataḥ pūrvavat mtshan nyid kyis ni snga ma bzhin no /
tatprabhedaḥ punaḥ trividhaḥ /
bījasamanvāgamaḥ vaśitāsamanvāgamaḥ samudācārasamanvāgamaśca 		rab tu dbye bas ni sa bon dang ldan pa dang dbang dang ldan pa dang kun tu 'byung ba dang ldan pa'o /
vījasamanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ sa bon dang ldan pa gang zhe na /
kāmadhātau jāto bhūtaḥ kāmapratisaṃyuktaiḥ kleśopakleśaiḥ rūpārūpyapratisaṃyuktaiśca kleśopakleśairvījasamancāgamena samancāgataḥ upapattiprātilābhikaiśca 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur pa ni 'dod pa'i khams dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams dang skye bas 'thob pa'i dge ba rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa'o /
kuśalaiḥ /
rūpadhātau jāto bhūtaḥ kāmapratisaṃyuktaiḥ klaiśopakleśaiḥ vījasamanvāgamena samanvāgato 'samanvāgataśca vaktavyaḥ 		gzugs kyi khams su skyes par 'gyur pa ni /
'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa ma yin pa zhes kyang bya'o /
rūpapratisaṃyuktairārūpyapratisaṃyuktaiśca klaiśopakleśaiḥ bījasamanvāgamena samanvāgato 'samanvāgataśca vaktavyaḥ gzugs dang rab tu ldan pa dang gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams dang skye bas 'thob pa'i dge ba rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa'o /
gzugs med par skyes par gyur pa ni /
ārūpyapratisaṃyuktaiḥ kleśopakleśaiḥ bījasamanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ upapattiprātilābhikaiśca kuśalaiḥ 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa dang gzugs dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang; nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pa dang ldan pa ma yin pa zhes kyang bya'o /
traidhātu kapratipakṣa lābhī yasya yasya prakārasya pratipakṣa utpannastasya bījasamanvāgamenāsamanvāgataḥ /
yasya pratipakṣo notpannastasya bījasamanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ /
vaśitāsamanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ /
prayogikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ vaśitāsamanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ laukikānāṃ lokottarāṇāṃ vā dhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattyādīnāṃ tadekatyājāṃcā vyākṛtānām 		gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams dang skye bas 'thob pa'i dge ba rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa'o /
khams gsum pa'i gnyen po thob pa ni /
rnam pa gang dang gang gi gnyen po byung ba de dang de'i sa bon dang ldan pa ma yin gyi /
gang gi gnyen po ma byung ba de'i sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa'o /
dbang dang ldan pa gang zhe na /
sbyor ba las byung ba'i dge ba'i chos 'jig rten pa rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa la sogs pa dang lung du ma bstan pa de dag las kyang kha cig ni dbang dang ldan pas ldan pa'o; /
samudācārasamanvāgamaḥ katamaḥ /
skandhadhātvāyatanānāṃ yo ya eva dharmaḥ saṃmukhībhūtaḥ kuśalo vā akuśalo vā avyākṛto vā tasya samudācārasamanvāgamena samanvāgataḥ /
samucchinnakuśalamūlaḥ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ bījasamanvāgamena samanvāgato 'samanvāgataśca vaktavyaḥ 		kun tu 'byung ba dang ldan pa gang zhe na /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams las dge ba'am mi dge ba'am /
lung du bstan pa'am /
lung du ma bstan pa yang rung chos gang dang gang mngon du gyur pa de dang de'i kun tu 'byung ba dang ldan pas ldan pa'o /
dge ba'i rtsa ba chad pa ni dge ba'i chos rnams kyi sa bon dang ldan pas ldan pa dang ldan pa ma yin zhes kyang bya'o /
ātyantikaḥ punaḥ saṃkleśasamanvāgamaḥ aparinirvāṇadharmakāṇāmicchantikānāṃ draṣṭavyaḥ kun nas nyon mongs pa dang gtan du ldan pa ni yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can gyi 'dod chen pa rnams kyi yin par blta ste /
mokṣahetuvaikalyādātyantika eṣāṃ hetvasamanvāgamaḥ /
samanvāgamakuśalaḥ kamanuśaṃsaṃ pratilabhate 		de dag la thar pa'i rgyu med pa'i phyir gtan du ste /
rgyu dang mi ldan pa'o /
ldan pa la mkhas pas phan yon ci zhig 'thob ce na /
ācayāpacayajño bhavati dharmāṇām /
tathā ācayāpacayajño na kasyāṃ cillaukikyāṃ saṃpattau vipattau vā ekāntikasaṃjñī bhavati yāvadevānunayapratighaprahāṇāya 		chos rnams kyi 'phel ba dang 'grib pa shes par 'gyur ro /
de ltar 'phel ba dang 'grib pa shes na /
'jig rten pa'i phun sum tshogs pa'am /
rgud pa gang la yang gcig tu nges par 'du shes par mi 'gyur gyi 'di lta ste /
abhidharmasamuccaye lakṣaṇasamuccayo nāma prathamaḥ samuccayaḥ rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba spong bar 'gyur ro /
chos mngon pa kun las btus pa las /
[athābhidharmasamuccayaśāstre viniścayasamuccaye satyaparicchedaḥ prathamaḥ mtshan nyid kun las btus pa zhes bya ba ste /
kun las btus pa dang po'o /
bam po gsum pa /
viniścayaḥ katamaḥ /
satyaviniścayo dharmaviniścayaḥ prāptiviniśca sāṃkathyaviniścayaśca /
satyaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ 		rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
bden pa rnam par nges pa dang chos rnam par nges pa dang 'thob pa rnam par nges pa dang 'brel ba'i gtam rnam par nges pa'o /
bden pa rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
catvāyāryasatyāni duḥkhaṃ samudayo nirodho mārgaśca 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag ste /
sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam mo /
duḥkhasatyaṃ katasat /
tatsattvajanmato janmādhiṣṭānataśca veditavyam 		sdug bsngal gyi bden pa gang zhe na /
de ni sems can skye ba dang skye ba'i gnas kyis kyang rig par bya'o /
sattvajanma katamat sems can skye ba gang zhe na /
