narakasattvajanmatiryakpreteṣu manuṣyeṣu pūrvavideheṣvapagodānīyeṣu jāmbūdvīpeṣu uttareṣu kuruṣu deveṣu caturmāhārājakāyikeṣu trāyastriṃśeṣu yāmeṣu tuṣiteṣu nirmāṇaratiṣu paranirmitavaśavartiṣu brahmapurohiteṣu mahābrāhmeṣuparīttābheṣva pramāṇābheṣu ābhāsvareṣu parīttaśubheṣvapramāṇaśubheṣu śubhakṛtsneṣvanabhrakeṣu puṇyaprasaveṣu vṛhatphaleṣva saṃjñisattveṣvabṛheṣvatapeṣu sudṛśeṣu sudarśaneṣvakaniṣṭheṣvākāśānantyāyataneṣu vijñānānantyāyataneṣvākiñcanyāyataneṣu naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyataneṣu sems can dmyal ba rnams dang dud 'gro rnams dang yi dags rnams dang mi rnams dang shar gyi lus 'phags dang nub kyi ba lang spyod dang 'dzam bu gling dang byang gi sgra mi snyan dang rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams dang sum cu rtsa gsum dang 'thab bral dang dga' ldan dang 'phrul dga' dang gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang tshangs ris dang tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don dang tshangs chen dang 'od chung dang tshad med 'od dang 'od gsal dang dge chung dang tshad med dge dang dge rgyas dang sprin med dang bsod nams skyes dang 'bras bu che dang 'du shes med pa'i sems can dang; mi che ba dang mi gsung ba dang gya nom snang dang shin tu mthong dang 'og min dang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang ci yang med pa'i skye mched dang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched rnams su sems can skye ba'o /
janmādhiṣṭhānaṃ katamat skye ba'i gnas gang zhe na /
bhājanalokaḥ snod kyi 'jig rten te /
vāyumaṇḍale apmaṇḍalampratiṣṭhitam rlung gi dkyil 'khor la ni chu'i dkyil 'khor brten to /
apmaṇḍale pṛthivīmaṇḍalam chu'i dkyil 'khor la ni sa'i dkyil 'khor ro /
pṛthivīmaṇḍale sumeruḥ saptakāñcanaparvatāḥ catvāro dvīpāḥ aṣṭāvantaradvīpāḥ abhyantaraḥ samudro vāhyasamudraścatasraḥ sumerupariṣaṇḍāḥ caturmahārājakāyikānāṃ vāpastriṃśānāṃ sthānāntarāṇi cakracāḍaḥ parvataḥ ākāśe vimānāni yāmānāṃ tuṣitānāṃ nirmāṇaratīnāṃ paranirmitavaśavarttināṃ devānāṃ rūpāvacarāṇāṃ ca asurāṇāṃ sthānāntarāṇi nārakāṇāṃ sthānāntarāṇi /
uṣṇanarakāḥśītanarakāḥ pratyekanarakāśca tadekatyānāṃ ca tiryakpretānāṃ sthānāntarāṇi yāvadādityāḥ paricaranto diśo 'vabhāsayante vairocanāstāvatsāhasrake loke sahasraṃ candrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ sūryaṇāṃ sahasraṃ sumerūṇāṃ parvatarājāṇāṃ sahasraṃ caturṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ sahasraṃ caturmahārājakāyikānāṃ devānāṃ sahasraṃ trāyastriṃśānāṃ sahasraṃ yāmānāṃ sahasraṃ tuṣitānāṃ sahasraṃ nirmāṇaratīnāṃ sahasraṃ paranirmitavaśavarttināṃ sahasraṃ brahmalaukikānāmidamucyate sahasracūḍiko lokadhātuḥ 		sa'i dkyil 'khor la ni ri rab dang gser gyi ri bdun dang gling bzhi dang bar gyi gling brgyad dang nang gi rgya mtsho dang phyi'i rgya mtsho dang ri rab kyi bang rim dang rgyal chen bzhi'i ris dang sum cu rtsa gsum gyi gnas gzhan rnams dang khor yug gi ri dang nam mkha' la gzhal med khang rnams dang 'thab bral dang dga' ldan dang 'phrul dga' dang; gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang gzugs na spyod pa rnams dang lha ma yin gyi gnas gzhan dag dang sems can dmyal ba pa rnams kyi gnas gzhan dag dang tsha ba'i sems can dmyal ba rnams dang grang ba'i sems can dmyal ba rnams dang nyi tshe ba'i sems can dmyal ba rnams dang dud 'gro dang yi dags de dag kha cig gi gnas gzhan rnams dang nyi ma rnam par snang byed kun tu rgyu zhing phyogs snang bar byed pa ji snyed pa de snyed ni stong gi 'jig rten na /
zla ba stong dang nyi ma stong dang ri'i rgyal po ri rab stong dang shar gyi lus 'phags stong dang 'dzam bu gling stong dang nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang byang gi sgra mi snyan stong dang rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha dang sum cu rtsa gsum dang 'thab bral dang dga' ldan dang 'phrul dga' dang gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi kha rnams kyi gnas gzhan stong dang tshangs pa'i 'jig rten gyi gnas gzhan stong po 'di ni stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o /
sahasraṃ sahasracūḍikānāṃ dhātūnāmucyate dvitīyo madhyamasāhasro lokadhātuḥ stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa 'di ni stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o /
sahasraṃ madhyamasāhasradhātūnāmucyate tṛtīyo mahāsāhasro lokadhātuḥ stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa 'di ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o /
evaṃ sa trisāhasro mahāsāhasro lokadhātuḥ mahācakravāḍa parvatamaṇḍala pariveṣṭitaḥ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams ni khor yug chen pos kun tu bskor to /
sa ca trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātuḥ saprasaṃvarttavivarttaḥ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di ni mnyam du 'jig cing 'chags so /
tathā ca devaḥ cakrākārān vṛṣṭivindūn nirantaraṃ niravacchinna mākāśād varṣati 'di lta ste dper na char gyi rgyun gnya' shing tsam 'bab na /
bar snang la char gyi rgyun 'bab pa rnams kyi bar dang mtshams med pa de bzhin du /
tathā ca pūrvasyāṃ diśi nirantaraṃ niravacchinna mapramāṇo lokadhātuḥ saṃvarttiṣyate vā vivarttiṣyate vā saṃvarttate vā saṃvṛttastiṣṭhati vā vivarttate vā vivṛttastiṣṭhati vā shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'jig pa dang 'chags pa rnams kyi bar dang mtshams med de gzhan dag ni 'jig go /
gzhan dag ni zhig nas 'dug go /
gzhan dag ni 'chags so /
gzhan dag ni chags nas 'dug go /
yathā pūrvasyāṃ diśi tathā sarvāsu daśasu dikṣu shar phyogs ji lta bar phyogs bcu thams cad kyang de bzhin no /
yaśca sattvaloko yaśca bhājanalokaḥ karmakleśaḥ janitaḥ karmakleśādhipateyaśca sarvamucyate duḥkhasatyam /
pariśuddhalokadhātustu na duḥkhasatyasaṃgṛhīḥto na karmakleśa janitaḥ na karmakleśādhipateyaśca 		sems can gyi 'jig rten gang yin pa dang snod kyi 'jig rten gang yin pa las dang nyon mongs pas bskyed pa /
las dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba 'di mtha' dag ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'o /
yongs su dag pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams de dag ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ma yin pa blta ste /
de dag las dang nyon mongs pas bskyed pa ma yin /
las dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba ma yin gyi /
kevalaṃ mahāpraṇidhānena vyavadānakuśalamūlādhipatinā ākṛṣyate tadutpattisthānaṃ cācintyaṃ kevalaṃ buddhena budhyate na dhyāyināṃ dhyānagocaraḥ kiṃ punaḥ cintayatām smon lam dang dge ba'i rtsa ba'i dbang gis byung ba dag go /
de lta bas na sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul yin pa'i phyir skye ba'i gnas de dag ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste /
de dag ni bsam gtan pa rnams kyi bsam gtan gyi yul yang ma yin na /
rtog ge pa rnams kyi yul ma yin pa lta smos kyang ci dgos /
api khalu duḥkhalakṣaṇaprabhedā aṣṭau /
"jātirduḥkhaṃ jarā duḥkhaṃ vyādhiduḥkhaṃ maraṇaṃ duḥkham apriyasaṃprayogo duḥkhaṃ priyaviprayogo duḥkhaṃ yadapīcchanna labhate tadapi duḥkhaṃ saṃkṣiptena pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham" 		yang skye ba ni sdug bsngal lo /
rga ba ni sdug bsngal lo /
na ba ni sdug bsngal lo /
'chi ba ni sdug bsngal lo /
mi sdug pa dang phrad pa ni sdug bsngal lo /
sdug pa dang bral ba ni sdug bsngal lo /
gang 'dod pa btsal te ma rnyed pa de yang sdug bsngal lo /
mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga ni sdug bsngal lo /
jātiḥ kimupādāya duḥkham /
saṃbādhaduḥkhatāṃ tadanyaduḥkhāśrayatāṃ copādāya /
jarā kimupādāya duḥkham 		ci'i phyir skye ba sdug bsngal zhe na /
dogs pa'i sdug bsngal nyid dang de las gzhan pa'i sdug bsngal gyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro /
ci'i phyir rga ba sdug bsngal zhe na /
kāle viparīṇatiduḥkhatāmupādāya /
vyādhi kimupādāya duḥkham /
bhūteṣu viparīṇatiduḥkhatāmupādāya /
maraṇaṃ kimupādāya duḥkham /
jīvitavipraṇāśaduḥkhatāmupādāya 		na tshod gyur pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
ci'i phyir na ba sdug bsngal zhe na /
khams gyur pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
ci'i phyir 'chi ba sdug bsngal zhe na /
srog gyur pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
apriyasaṃprayogaḥ kimupādāya duḥkham /
saṃyogaja duḥkhatāmupādāya 		ci'i phyir mi sdug pa dang phrad pa sdug bsngal zhe na /
phrad pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
priyaviprayogaḥ kimupādāya duḥkham /
viprayogaja duḥkhatāmupadāya 		ci'i phyir sdug pa dang bral ba sdug bsngal zhe na /
bral pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
yadapīcchanna labhate tat kimupādāya duḥkham ci'i phyir gang 'dod pa btsal te ma rnyed pa de yang sdug bsngal zhe na /
kāmyaphalābhāvaja duḥkhatāmupādāya /
saṃkṣiptenapañcopādānaskandhāḥ kimupādāya duḥkham /
dauṣṭhulyaduḥkhatāmupādāya /
evamaṣṭau saṃgṛhītāni ṣaḍ bhavanti 		re ba 'bras bu med pa sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
ci'i phyir mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga sdug bsngal zhe na /
gnas ngan len sdug bsngal nyid kyi phyir ro /
de dag ni brgyad yin yang drug tu 'gyur ro /
saṃvādhaduḥkhaṃ vipariṇati duḥkhaṃ saṃprayogaduḥkhaṃ viprayogaduḥkhaṃ kāmyaphalābhāvaduḥkhaṃ dauṣṭhulyaduḥkhaṃ ca /
evaṃ ṣaḍ bāhulyenāṣṭau bhavanti 		drug yin yang brgyad du 'gyur te /
dogs pa'i sdug bsngal dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang phrad pa'i sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i sdug bsngal dang re ba 'bras bu med pa'i sdug bsngal dang gnas ngan len gyi sdug bsngal lo /
ṣaḍ samānānyaṣṭau bhavanti gang sdug bsngal nyid gsum gsungs na /
yaduktaṃ tisro duḥkhatāḥ /
tāsu aṣṭau duḥkhāni saṃgṛhitāni bhavanti 		ci sdug bsngal nyid gsum po dag gis sdug bsngal rnam pa brgyad bsdus sam /
tatra kathaṃ tisṛṣu saṃgṛhītānyaṣṭau aṣṭasu vā saṃgṛhītāstisraḥ sdug bsngal rnam pa brgyad kyis sdug bsngal nyid gsum bsdus she na /
pāraṃparṣalakṣaṇa saṃgrahāt /
jātirdukhaṃ jarā duḥkhaṃ vyādhirduḥkhaṃ maraṇaṃ duḥkham apriyasaṃprayogo duḥkhamiti santānaduḥkhaduḥkhatā 		gcig gis gcig bsdus te /
skye ba'i sdug bsngal dang rga ba'i sdug bsngal dang na ba'i sdug bsngal dang 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal dang mi sdug pa dang phrad pa'i sdug bsngal gang gsungs pa 'dis ni sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid yongs su bstan to /
priyaviprayogo duḥkhaṃ yadapīcchanna labhate tadapi duḥkhaṃ tadvipariṇāmaduḥkhatā sdug pa dang bral ba'i sdug bsngal dang gang 'dod pa btsal te ma rnyed pa de yang sdug bsngal zhes gang gsungs pa 'dis ni 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid yongs su bstan to /
saṃkṣiptena pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkhaṃ tat saṃskāraduḥkhatā /
yaduktaṃ dvividhe duḥkhe iti 		mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga sdug bsngal lo zhes gang gsungs pa 'dis ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid yongs su bstan to /
tat saṃvṛtisatyena duḥkhaṃ paramārthasatyena duḥkhaṃ ca /
katamat saṃvṛtisatyena duḥkhaṃ katamat paramārthasatyena duḥkham 		kun rdzob kyi bden par sdug bsngal ba dang don dam pa'i bden par sdug bsngal bzhes gang gsungs pa la kun rdzob kyi bden par sdug bsngal ba ni gang yin /
don dam pa'i bden par sdug bsngal ba ni gang yin zhe na /
jātirduḥkhaṃ yāvat yadapīcchann labhate tadapi duḥkhamiti saṃvṛtisatyena duḥkham /
yaduktaṃ saṃkṣiptena pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkhamiti paramārthasatyena duḥkham 		skye ba'i sdug bsngal nas 'dod pa btsal te ma rnyed pa de yang sdug bsngal zhes bya ba'i bar ni kun rdzob kyi bden par sdug bsngal ba'o /
mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga sdug bsngal lo zhes gsungs pa ni don dam pa'i bden par sdug bsngal ba'o /
duḥkhasatyasya sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ katamat /
anityalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhalakṣaṇaṃ śūnyalakṣaṇamanātmalakṣaṇaṃ ca /
anityalakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i spyi'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
mi rtag pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid dang sdug bsngal ba'i mtshan nyid dang stong ba'i mtshan nyid dang bdag med pa'i mtshan nyid do /
samāsato dvādaśavidham /
asallakṣaṇaṃ vināśalakṣaṇaṃ vipariṇatilakṣaṇaṃ viyogalakṣaṇaṃ sannihitalakṣaṇaṃdharmatālakṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇalakṣaṇaṃ prabandhalakṣaṇaṃ vyādhyādi lakṣaṇaṃ cittacittākāravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ bhogasaṃpattirvipatti lakṣaṇaṃ bhājanalokasaṃvarttavivarttalakṣaṇam 		mi rtag pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
gang med pa'i mtshan nyid dang rnam par 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid dang 'gyur ba'i mtshan nyid dang 'bral ba'i mtshan nyid dang nye ba'i mtshan nyid dang chos nyid kyi mtshan nyid dang skad cig gi mtshan nyid dang rgyun gyi mtshan nyid dang nang la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid dang sems sna tshogs kyi rnam par 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid dang longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa rgud pa'i mtshan nyid dang snod 'jig pa dang 'chags pa'i mtshan nyid do /
asallakṣaṇaṃ katamat /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣu sarvakāli kātmātmīyatā nityābhāvaḥ 		med pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na; gang phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la bdag dang bdag gi dus rtag tu med pa'o /
vināśalakṣaṇaṃ katamat rnam par 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
saṃskārāṇāmutpannānāṃ nirodhaḥ /
taktālaṃ bhūtvābhāvaḥ /
vipariṇatilakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		gang 'du byed skyes pa rnams kyi rnam par 'jig pa'o /
'gyur ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
saṃskārāṇāmanyathābhāvaḥ /
prabandhāsādṛśyena pravṛttiḥ /
viyogalakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		gang 'du byed rnams gzhan dang gzhan du 'gyur ba'o /
'bral ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
saṃskāreṣu vaśitvabhraṃśaḥ paraiḥsvīkaraṇaṃ vā /
sannihitalakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		gang 'du byed rnams la dbang byed pa nyams pa dang gzhan dag gis bdag gir byas pa'o /
samupasthitānityatā nye ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
yattadānīmevānubhūyamānānityatā mi rtag pa nyid kyis non pa'o /
dharmatālakṣaṇaṃ katamat chos nyid kyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
āgāminyanityatā /
yāmāvaśyamanubhaviṣyati /
kṣaṇalakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		mi rtag pa nyid 'byung ba rgyus 'brel pa'o /
skad cig gi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
saṃskārāṇāṃ kṣaṇādūrddhamanavasthānam /
prabandhalakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		'du byed rnams skad cig gcig las phan chad du mi gnas pa'o /
rgyun gyi mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
anādimati saṃskāre utpannaniruddhā nāṃ prabandhāprahāṇam thog ma med pa'i dus kyi 'du byed rnams kyi skye ba'i rgyun mi 'chad pa'o /
vyadhyādi lakṣaṇa katamat /
caturṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ kālopabhogaḥ jīvitavipariṇāmaḥ 		nad la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
khams dang na tshod dang srog rnams 'gyur ba'o /
cittacittākāra vṛttilakṣaṇaṃ katamat sems sna tshogs kyi rnam par 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
kadācit sārāgaṃ cittaṃ saṃbhavati kadācid vītarāgaṃ cittaṃ saṃbhavati /
yadvat sadveṣaṃ vā vītadveṣaṃ vā samohaṃ vā vītamohaṃ vā saṃkṣiptaṃ vā vihisāṃ vā nimnaṃ vā unnataṃ vā uddhataṃ vā anuddhataṃ vā upaśāntaṃ vā anupaśāntaṃ vā samāhita vā asamāhitaṃ vā 		res 'ga' 'dod chags dang bcas pa'i sems dang res 'ga' 'dod chags dang bral ba dang de bzhin du zhe sdang dang bcas pa dang; zhe sdang dang bral ba dang gti mug dang bcas pa dang gti mug dang bral ba dang bsdus pa dang g yengs pa dang bying ba dang rab tu gzung ba dang rgod pa dang mi rgod pa dang nye bar ma zhi ba dang nye bar ma zhi ba dang nye bar zhig ba dang mnyam par gzhag pa dang mnyam par ma bzhag pa la sogs pa'i rnam par sems kyi 'byung ba gang yin pa'o /
evamādi cittasaṃsāravṛttiḥ /
bhogasaṃpattivipatti lakṣaṇaṃ katamat /
saṃpattīnāmante vipattirvināśaḥ /
bhājanalokasaṃvartta vivartta lakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		longs spyod 'byor ba rgud pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
'byor ba thams cad kyi mtha' ni rgud pa nyid do /
snod 'jig pa dang 'chags pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
agnyambuvāyubhistrividhaḥ saṃvarttavivarttaḥ 'jig par byed pa gsum ste /
me dang chu dang rlung ngo /
tisṛṇāṃ saṃvarttarnānāṃ śīrṣāṇi dvitīya tṛtīya caturthadhyānāni 'jig pa na bsdus pa gsum ste /
bsam gtan gnyis pa dang gsum pa dang bzhi pa'o /
caturthadhyāne vāhyānāṃ vimānānāṃ tu vāhyābhāvat eva saṃvarttavivarttaḥ /
kevalaṃ tairdevaiḥ tāni vimānāni saha nirvarttante saha nirudhyante etaducyate saṃvartta vivarttaḥ /
api khalu trayo 'ntarakalpāḥ durbhikṣavyādhiśastrairbhavanti 		bsam gtan bzhi pa la ni gzhal med khang rnams dang lhan cig 'byung ba dang lhan cig 'gags pas 'jig cing 'chags so /
bskal pa bar ma gsum ste /
mu ge'i bskal pa bar ma dang nad kyi bskal pa bar ma dang mtshon cha'i bskal pa bar ma ste /
hīnasya trividhakalpāsyānte taiḥ śastrādibhirniryāṇaṃ bhavati /
yadālokadhātuḥ saṃvṛtto bhavati /
eko 'ntarakalpa prathamaḥ apakarṣaḥ 		de dag gis bskal pa tshar phyin par 'gyur ro /
mar 'bri ba bar gyi bskal pa gcig dang yar 'phel ba dang mar 'bri ba bcva brgyad dang yar skye ba gcig ste /
ekāntarakalpaḥ paścima utkarṣaḥ bar gyi bskal pa nyi shur 'jig rten 'jig go /
aṣṭādaśa antarakalpā utkarṣāpakaya bar gyi bskal pa nyi shur 'jig rten zhig par 'dug go /
evaṃ ca viṃśatimantarakalpān lokadhātuḥ saṃvarttate /
viṃśatimātarakalpāt lokadhāturvivarttate 		bar gyi bskal pa nyi shur 'jig rten 'chags so /
bar gyi bskal pa nyi shur 'jig rten chags nas 'dug go /
viṃśatimantarakalpān lokadhāturvivṛttastiṣṭhati /
saṃkalikāścaite 'śītirantarakalpā eko mahākalpo bhavati /
tayā kalpasaṃkhyāyā rūpārūpyācarāṇāṃ devānāmāyuḥpramāṇaṃ varṇyate 		de dag ni bar gyi bskal pa brgyad cu ste /
de ni bskal pa chen po'o /
bskal pa bgrang ba'i tshul des gzugs na spyod pa rnams dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad do /
yaduktam anyatare, sattvā āyuḥkṣayād vā puṇya kṣayād vā karmakṣayād vā tasmādadhiṣṭhānāt cyavante iti sems can de dag gi tshe zad cing bsod nams zad la las kyang zad nas /
gnas de nas shi 'pho bar 'gyur ro /
tatra āyudāyaḥ katamaḥ tshe zad pas ji lta bu zhe na /
kāle maraṇam /
puṇyakṣayaḥ katamaḥ /
akāle maraṇam apuṇyamaraṇam 		'chi ba'i dus la bab pa'o /
bsod nams zad pas ji lta bu zhe na /
dus ma yin par 'chi ba ste /
yena sattvā āsvāda samāpattyāṃ rajyante /
puṇyakṣayācca hetoḥ te jīvitāccyavante /
karmakṣayaḥ katamaḥ 		'di ltar sems can de dag snyoms par 'jug pa'i ro myang bas bsod nams zad par 'gyur te /
des na dus la ma bab kyang 'chi'o /
las zad pas ji lta bu zhe na /
upapadyavedanīyakarmaṇaḥ aparaparyāvedanīyakarmaṇaśca ubhayo kṣayānmaraṇa der skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba dang lan grangs gzhan la myong bar 'gyur ba'i las yongs su gtugs pa'o /
duḥkhalakṣaṇaṃ katamat /
tisro duḥkhatāḥ aṣṭākā vā duḥkhaṃ ṣaḍākāraṃ vā duḥkhaṃ bāhulyena pūrvamuktaṃ tad duḥkhaṃ nāma /
kiṃ pratītyasūtre uktaṃ yadanityaṃ tad duḥkhamiti /
ubhayāṃśikīmanityatāṃ pratītya duḥkhalakṣaṇaṃ prajñāyate 		sdug bsngal gyi mtshan nyi gang zhe na /
sdug bsngal nyid gsum dang sdug bsngal rnam pa brgyad ni sdug bsngal zhes bya ba'o /
ci'i phyir gang mi rtag pa de sdug bsngal zhes gsungs she na /
mi rtag pa nyid ni gnyis kyi char gtogs pa ste /
utpādāṃśikīmanityatāṃ pratītya duḥkhaduḥkhatā prajñāyate skye ba'i char gtogs pa dang 'jig pa'i char gtogs pa'o /
vyayāṃśikīmanityatāṃ pratītya vipariṇāmaduḥkhatā prajñāyate skye ba'i char gtogs pa'i mi rtag pa nyid la brten nas sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so /
ubhayāṃśīkimanityatāṃ pratītya saṃskāraduḥkhatā prajñāyate 'jig pa'i char gtogs pa'i mi rtag pa nyid la brten nas 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so /
tathā ca saṃskārānityatāṃ saṃskāravipariṇāmatāṃ ca saṃdhāyoktaṃ bhagavatā mayā yatkiṃcid veditamidamatra duḥkhasyeti /
api khalu utpādavyayadharmadvayānugateṣu saṃskāreṣu jātyādayo 'ṣṭau duḥkhāni 		de gnyi ga'i char gtogs pa'i mi rtag pa nyid la brten nas 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so /
de la dgongs te bcom ldan 'das kyis ngas 'du byed mi rtag pa nyid dang 'du byed 'gyur ba nyid la dgongs nas /
prajñāyante ityabhisaṃdhāya buddhena bhāṣitaṃ yadanityaṃ tad duḥkhamiti gang ci tshor yang rung /
'di ni 'dir sdug bsngal du gsungs so zhes bka' stsal to /
api ca anityeṣu saṃskāreṣu jātyādikaṃ duḥkhaṃ prajñāyate iti anityato duḥkhaṃ na sarve saṃskārā ityatrādhisandhirveditavyaḥ /
śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ katamat 		yang skye ba dang 'jig pa'i chos nyid dang rjes su 'brel ba'i 'du byed rnams la skye ba la sogs pa sdug bsngal brgyad mngon te /
de'i phyir sdug bsngal zhes bya'o /
stong pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
teṣu tasya abhāvaḥ /
anena nayena samanupaśyanāśūnyatā 		gang la gang med pa de ni des stong par yang dag par rjes su mthong ba ste /
punaḥ teṣu anyasya bhāvaḥ /
anena nayena yathābhūtajñānabhāvaḥ 		'di la lhag ma gang yin pa de ni 'dir yod pa'o zhes yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so /
etad vatāraśūnyatocyate /
yathābhūtajñānamaviparīto 'rthaḥ 		'di ni stong pa nyid la 'jug pa yang dag pa'i lta ba ste /
phyin ci ma log pa zhes bya'o /
teṣu abhāvaḥ katamaḥ gang na ci zhig med ce na /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣu nityadhruvakūṭasthāvipariṇāmadharmātmātmīyābhāvaḥ phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la rtag pa dang brtan pa dang ther zug pa dang mi 'gyur ba'i chos can dang bdag dang bdag gi med do /
anena nayena teṣāṃ śūnyatā de lta bas na de dag ni des stong ngo /
teṣu anyasya bhāvaḥ katamaḥ /
te ṣveva nairātmyam 		de la lhag ma yod pa ci zhig ce na /
gang bdag med pa de nyid de /
tacca ātmano nāstitā anātmano 'stitā satī śūnyatā de ltar bdag ni med kyi bdag med pa ni yod par stong pa nyid khong du chud par bya'o /
etadabhisaṃdhāyoktaṃ bhagavatā sato yathābhūtajñānaṃ bhāvaḥ 'di las dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis yod pa yang yod par /
asato yathābhūtajñānamabhāvaḥ /
api khalu trividhā śūnyatā 		med pa yang med par yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so /
zhes gsungs so /
yang stong pa nyid rnams pa gsum ste /
svabhāvaśūnyatā tathābhāvaśūnyatā prakṛtiśūnyatā ca ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa nyid dang de bzhin du yod pa ma yin pa'i stong pa nyid dang rang bzhin gyi stong pa nyid do /
ādyā parikalpitā draṣṭavyā /
tṛtīyā pariniṣpannasvabhāvā draṣṭavyā /
anātmalakṣaṇaṃ katamat /
yathātmavāde sthitasya ātmalakṣaṇasya skandhadhātvāyataneṣu tallakṣaṇasyābhāvaḥ 		dang po ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid nye bar gzung bar blta'o /
gnyis pa ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid nye bar gzung ba'o /
gsum pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid nye bar gzung bar blta'o /
bdag med pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
ji ltar bdag tu smra ba rnams kyis bdag tu btags pa'i mtshan nyid des /
phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams mtshan nyid dang bral ba'o /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣu ātmalakṣaṇābhāvatāmupādāya phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams ni bdag gi mtshan nyid kyis bdag med pa'o /
idamucyate anātmalakṣaṇam /
etadabhisaṃghāyoktaṃ bhagavatā sarve dharmā anātmāna iti 		'di la dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis chos thams cad bdag med pa'o zhes gsungs so /
bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di dag thams cad ni nga'i ba med do /
api coktaṃ bhagavatā naitat sarvaṃ mama naiṣo 'hamasmi na me sa ātmā iti /
evametaṃ yathābhūtaṃ saṃprajñāya draṣṭhavyam iti tasya ko 'rtha uktaḥ 		'di ni nga ma yin pa'o /
'di ni nga'i bdag ma yin pa ste /
de ni 'di bzhin no zhes yang dag pa'i shes rab kyis yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du blta bar bya'o /
bahirdhāvastabhisaṃdhāyoktaṃ naitat sarvaṃ mameti zhes gsungs pa 'di'i don ci zhe na /
phyi'i dngos po 'di ni bdag gi ma yin no /
kuta etat /
bahirdhāvastuni kalpitātmīyalakṣaṇam /
ataḥ ātmīyaniṣkarṣaṇam 		nang gi dngos po 'di ni nga ma yin no /
'di ni nga'i bdag ma yin pa'o zhes bya bar dgongs nas gsungs pa ste /
adhyātmavastuni parikalpitātmātmīyalakṣaṇam /
ata ātmātmīyobhayaniṣkarṣaṇam 		'di ltar phyi'i dngos po la ni bdag gi rnam par dang nang la ni bdag dang bdag gi rnam par bkag go /
pūrvamuktam anityaṃ kṣaṇalakṣaṇamiti /
tat kathaṃ jñāyate /
yathā cittacaitasikānāṃ kṣaṇikatā tathā rūpādīnāmapi kṣaṇikatā draṣṭavyā /
cittopāttatāmupādāya cittaikayogakṣematāmupādāya cittavikāratadvikāratāmupādāya cittāśrayatāmudāpādāya cittādhipatyasaṃbhūtatāmupādāya cittvaśavarttināṃ copādāya 		skad cig gi mtshan nyid ni mi rtag pa nyid do zhes gsungs pa de ji lta bu zhe na /
ji ltar sems dang sems las byung ba skad cig ma yin pa de ltar gzugs kyang skad cig par blta ste /
sems kyis zin pa dang sems dang grub pa dang bde ba gcig pa dang sems 'gyur na de 'gyur ba dang sems kyi gnas yin pa dang sems kyi dbang gis byung ba dang sems dbang sgyur ba'i phyir ro /
api khalu atyantavikāropālabdhitāmupādāya utpannasya cānapekṣya pratyayaṃ svarasavināśitāmupādāya rūpasyāpi kṣaṇikatā draṣṭavyā /
yaduktaṃ yatkiṃcidrūpaṃ sarvantaccatvāri mahābhūtāni catvāri ca mahābhūtānyupādāyeti 		yang mthar 'gyur bar dmigs pa dang skyes nas kyang rkyen la mi ltos par rang gi ngang gis rnams par 'jig pa'i phyir gzugs kyang skad cig pa nyid du blta'o /
gzugs gang yin pa ci yang rung ste /
de thams cad 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag dang 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa'o /
tatkiṃ sandhāyoktam /
saṃbhavaṃ sandhāyoktam 		zhes gang gsungs pa de ci las dgongs te gsungs she na /
srid pa la dgongs nas gsungs so /
ekadeśāśrayībhāvārtha upādāyārthaḥ /
yatra punaḥ samudāye yadbhūtamupalabhyate tattatrā stiti vaktavya 		phyogs gcig la brten pa'i dngos po'i don ni rgyur byas pa'i don te /
'dus pa gang las 'byung ba gang dmigs pa de ni de na yod do zhes brjod par bya'o /
asti ekabhautikaḥ asti dvibhautikaḥ asti yāvatsārvabhautikaḥ /
upādāyarūpe 'pi yadupādāyarūpaṃ yasmin samudāya upalabhyate tattatrāstīti veditavyam /
yatpunarūcyate paramāṇusaṃcitto rūpa samudāya iti tatra niḥśarīraḥ paramāṇurveditavyaḥ /
buddhyā paryantaprabhedatastu paramāṇuvyavasthānaṃ piṇḍasaṃjñāvibhāghanatāmupādāya rūpe dravyāḥ pariniṣpattipraveśatāṃ copādāya 		'byung ba gcig las gyur pa'i 'dus pa yang yod /
'byung ba gnyis las gyur pa yod pa nas /
'byung ba thams cad las gyur ba yang yod do /
rgyur byas pa'i gzugs la yang rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gang 'dus pa gang la dmigs pa de ni de na yod pa'o zhes rig par bya'o /
rdul phra rab bsags pa ni gzugs 'dus pa'o zhes gang brjod pa de la rdul phra rab lus med par rig par bya'o /
blos mthar rab tu phye nas rdul phra rab tu rnam par gzhag ste /
ril po'i 'du shes rnams par gzhig pa dang gzugs la rdzas su yongs su grub pa med par 'jug par bya ba'i phyir ro /
tat punaretad duḥkhamasti vipulamasaṃlikhitaṃ saṃlikhitaṃ saṃlikhitā saṃlikhitaṃ ca /
asti madhyamasaṃlikhitam asti tanukamasaṃlikhitam asti tanuttaraṃ saṃlikhitam asti tanutamaṃ saṃlikhitam astyaduḥkhaṃ duḥkhapratibhāsaṃ mahāsaṃlekhapratyupasthānaṃ ca 		yang sdug bsngal 'di ni shin tu rgyas la ma bsrabs pa dang bsrabs pa dang bsrabs pa yang ma yin la ma bsrabs pa'ang yin pa yang yod /
bar ma ma bsrabs pa yang yod /
bsrabs lam bsrabs pa yang yod /
ches bsrabs la bsrabs pa yang yod /
shin tu ches bsrabs la bsrabs pa yang yod /
sdug bsngal ma yin la sdug bsngal du snang zhing bsrabs pa chen por nye bar gnas pa yang yod do /
katamadvipulaṃ duḥkhamasaṃlikhitam sdug bsngal shin tu rgyas la ma bsrabs pa gang zhe na /
yatkāmāvacaramanupacitakuśalamūlānām gang 'dod pa na spyod pa dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bsags pa rnams kyi'o /
katamatsaṃlikhitam /
tadevotpannamokṣabhāgīyānām 		bsrabs pa gang zhe na /
de nyid thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa skyes pa rnams kyi'o /
katamatsaṃlikhitāsaṃlikhitam bsrabs pa yang yin la ma bsrabs pa yang yin pa gang zhe na /
tadeva laukikavairāgyāyāvaropitakuśalamūlānām /
katamanmadhyamasaṃlikhitam 		de nyid 'jig rten pas 'dod chags dang bral ba ba nyid du bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags pa rnams kyi'o /
bar ma ma bsrabs pa gang zhe na /
rūpadhātūpapannānāṃ vivarjitamokṣabhāgīyānām gzugs kyi khams su skyes pa thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnam par spangs pa rnams kyi'o /
katamattanukamasaṃlikhitam bsrabs la ma bsrabs pa gang zhe na /
ārūpyopapannānāṃ vivarjitamokṣabhāgīyānām gzugs med par skyes par thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams par spangs pa rnams kyi'o /
katamattanuttaraṃ saṃlikhitam /
yacchaikṣāṇām 		ches bsrabs la bsrabs pa gang zhe na; gang slob pa rnams kyi'o /
katamattanutamaṃ saṃlikhitam shin tu ches bsrabs la bsrabs pa gang zhe na /
yadaśaikṣāṇāṃ jīvitendriyapratyayaṃ ṣaḍāyatanam /
katamadaduḥkhaṃ duḥkhapratibhāsaṃ mahāsaṃlekhapratyupasthānam 		gang mi slob pa rnams kyi srog gi dbang po'i rkyen gyi ming dang gzugs so /
sdug bsngal ma yin la sdug bsngal du snang zhing bsrabs pa chen por nye bar gnas pa gang zhe na /
yatpāramiprāptānāṃ bodhisattvānāmacintya bhavopapattiṣu gang byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa rnams kyi ste /
bsams bzhin du srid par skye ba'i phyir ro /
yaduktaṃ maraṇaṃ duḥkhamiti /
tatra maraṇaṃ trividham 		'chi ba sdug bsngal lo zhes gang gsungs pa de la 'chi ba rnam pa gsum ste /
kuśalacittasyāvyākṛtacittasya ca /
paṭuke cittaprakāre svakuśala mūlabalādhānato vā paropasaṃhārato vā kuśalacittasya maraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam 		dge ba'i sems yod pa dang mi dge ba'i sems yod pa dang lung du ma bstan pa'i sems yod pa ste; rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs bskyed pas sam /
gzhan gyis bsgrubs pas kyang rung ste /
sems kyi rgyu ba gsal ba ni dge ba'i sems yod pa'i 'chi bar blta'o /
rang gi mi dge ba'i sems bskyed pas sam /
paṭuka eva cittaprakāre svākuśalamulabalādhā nato vā paropasaṃhārato vā akuśalacittasya maraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam gzhan gyis bsgrubs pas kyang rung ste /
sems rgyu ba gsal ba ni mi dge ba'i sems yod pa'i 'chi bar blta'o /
paṭuke vā cittaprakāre apaṭuke vā tadubhayavai kalyādabhisaṃskārāsamarthasya vā avyākṛtacittasya maraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam sems kyi rgyu ba gsal yang rung mi gsal yang rung rkyen de gnyi ga ma tshang ba'i phyir mngon par 'du byed mi nus pa yang rung ste /
lung du ma bstan pa'i sems yod pa'i 'chi bar blta'o /
śubhakāriṇaḥ adhaḥkāya statprathamataḥ śītībhavati dge ba byed pa'i lus ni thob ma nyid smad grang bar 'gyur /
aśubhakāriṇaḥ punaḥ ūrdhvaṃkāyaḥ śītībhavati /
tatrāśubhakāriṇo 'ntarābhavo 'bhinirvarttate 		mi dge ba byed pa'i lus ni stod grang bar 'gyur ro /
de la mi dge ba byed pa'i bar ma do'i srid pa mngon par 'grub pa ni /
tadyathā kṛṣṇasya kutapasya nirbhāso 'ndhakāratamisrāyā vā rātryāḥ dper na phyar ba nag po'am /
mtshan mo mun pa mun nag tu snang ba lta bu'o /
aśubhakāriṇastadyathā śuklasya parasya nirbhāsajyotsnāyā vā rātryāḥ dge ba byed pa ni dper na snam bu dkar po'am /
zla ba'i 'od dang bcas pa'i mtshan mor snang ba lta bu'o /
antarābhavaḥ kāmadhātau rūpadhātau copapadyamānasyārūpadhātoścayamānasya /
sa ca manomayo gandharva ityapi 		bar ma do'i srid pa ni 'dod pa'i khams dang gzugs kyi khams su skye ba na'o /
gzugs med pa nas ni 'chi 'pho ba na'o /
de ni yid las byung ba dang dri za zhes kyang bya'o /
paraṃ saptāhaṃ tiṣṭhatyantareṇa cyavate de ltar thogs na zhig bdun gnas te /
de tshun chad kyis 'chi 'pho'o /
ekadā ca vyāvarttate ji ste na ldog go /
tatrasthaśca karmopacinoni sabhāgāṃśca sattvān paśyati de na gnas pa yang las sog go /
skal pa mnyam pa'i sems can rnams kyang mthong ngo /
yatra copapadyate tadākṛtirapratihatagatiśca gang du skye bar 'gyur ba de'i byad gzugs so /
'gro ba la thags thogs med do /
ṛddhimāniva vāśugāmī upapattyāyatane pratihanyate rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa bzhin du myur du 'gro zhing skye ba'i gnas su thogs so /
upapattyāyatane tulāvanāmonnāmayogena cyavate pratisandhi ca vadhnāti /
antarābhavasthaścopapattyāyatane rāgamutpādayati 		srang mda'i mthon dman gyi tshul du 'chi 'pho zhing nyid mtshams sbyor ro /
bar ma do'i srid pa na gnas pa ni skye ba'i gnas la 'dod chags bskyed de /
yadanyaśca kleśaḥ pratyayo bhavati /
saharāgeṇāntarābhavo nirudhyate kalalaṃ ca savijñānakamutpadyate 		de las gzhan pa'i nyon mongs pa ni rkyen du 'gyur ro /
'dod chags dang bcas par bar ma do'i srid pa 'gag cing nur nur po rnam par shes pa dang bcas pa 'byung ste /
sa ca vipākastata ūrdhvamindriyābhinrivṛttiḥ yathā pratityasamutpāde catṛsṛṣvāyoniṣu de ni rnam par smin pa'o /
de'i 'og tu rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba las ji skad 'byung ba bzhin /
aṇḍajāyāṃ jarayujāyāṃ saṃsvedajāyāmupapadukāyañca /
atha viniścaye satyaparicchede pratheme dvitīyo bhāgaḥ 		skye gnas bzhi po sgo nga las skye ba dang mngal nas skye ba dang drod gsher las skye ba dang brdzus te skye bar dbang po mgon par 'grub bo /
samudayasatyaṃ katamat kun 'byung ba'i bden pa gang zhe na /
kleśaḥ kleśādhipateyañca karma /
prādhānyanirddeśastu ? śāstu bhagavatā tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikī nandīrāgasahagatā tatra tatrābhinandinī samudayasatyanirdeśena nirdiṣṭā /
prādhānyārthaḥ katamaḥ 		nyon mongs pa dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba'i las so /
gtso bor bstan pa ni /
bcom ldan 'das kyis sred pa yang 'byung ba can dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang lan [*ldan?] pa de dang der mngon par dga' ba la kun 'byung ba'i bden par bstan pas bstan to /
gtso bo'i don gang zhe na /
yaḥ sarvatragārthaḥ gang thams cad du 'gro ba'i don to /
sarvatragārthaḥ katamaḥ thams cad du 'gro ba'i don gang zhe na /
tatha hi tṛṣṇā vastusarvatragā avasthāsarvatragā adhvasarvatragā dhātusarvatragā eṣaṇā sarvatragā prakārasarvatragā ca keśaḥ katamaḥ 'di ltar sred pa dngos po thams cad du 'gro ba dang gnas skabs thams cad du 'gro ba dang dus thams cad du 'gro ba dang khams thams cad du 'gro ba dang tshor ba thams cad du 'gro ba dang rnam pa thams cad du 'gro ba'o /
parisaṃkhyānato 'pi lakṣaṇato 'pyutthāna to 'pyālambanato 'pi saṃprayogato 'pi paryāyato 'pi vipratipattito 'pi dhatuto 'pi nikāyato 'pi prahāṇato 'pi kleśo draṣṭavyaḥ nyon mongs pa gang zhe na /
grangs dang mtshan nyid dang 'byung ba dang dmigs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang rnam grangs dang log par zhugs pa dang khams dang ris dang spong bas kyang nyon mongs par blta'o /
parisaṃkhyānaṃ katamat /
ṣaṭ kleśā daśa vā 		grangs gang zhe na /
nyon mongs pa drug gam bcu'o /
ṣaṭ kleśāḥ katamat nyon mongs pa drug gang zhe na /
rāgaḥ pratigho māno 'vidyā vicikitsā dṛṣṭiśca 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa dang the tshom dang lta ba'o /
ta eva dṛṣṭeḥ pañcākārjabhedena daśa bhavanti de dag nyid lta ba rnams pa lnga'i bye brag gis bcur 'gyur ro /
lakṣaṇaṃ katamat mtshan nyid gang zhe na /
yo dharma utpadyamāno 'praśāntalakṣaṇa utpadyamānena yena kāya cittaprabandhāpraśamapravṛttiḥ /
idaṃ kleśalakṣaṇam 		chos gang 'byung ba na rab tu ma zhi ba'i mtshan nyid du 'byung ste /
de byung bas sems kyi rgyud rab tu ma zhi bar 'byung ba de nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid do /
utthānaṃ katamat /
kleśānuśayaścāprahīṇo bhavati kleśasthānīyaśca dharma ābhāsagato bhavati /
tatra ca ayoniśo manaskāraḥ pratyavasthito bhavati 		'byung ba gang zhe na /
nyon mongs pa'i bag la nyal ma spangs par gyur pa dang nyon mongs pa'i gnas kyi chos kyang snang bar gyur pa dang de la yang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa nye bar gnas pa yin te /
evaṃ kleśa utpadyate /
idamucyate utthānam 		de lta bu las nyon mongs pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
dmigs pa gang zhe na /
ālambanaṃ katamat sarvakleśaprayogaḥ /
sarvakleśālambanaṃ sarvakleśavastvālambanaṃ ca /
api khalu kāmāvacaraḥ kleśaḥ sthāpayitvā avidyā dṛṣṭi vicikitsāṃ ca tadanyaḥ urdhvabhūmyanālambanaḥ 		nyon mongs pa thams cad ni nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi dmigs par blta'o /
nyon mongs pa'i gzhi yang dmigs pa'o /
ma rig pa dang lta ba dang the tshom ma gtogs par 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa ni sa gong ma la mi dmigs so /
ūrdhvabhūmikaḥ kleśaḥ adhobhūmyanālambanaḥ /
tadbhūmito vītarāgatvāt /
nirodhamārgasatyā lambanaḥ kleśo nirodhamargālambanānabhiśliṣṭaḥ /
tatparikalpastvasyālambanamityucyate /
kleśaḥ punardvividhaḥ /
avastukālambanaḥ savastukālambanaśca /
avastukālambanaḥ katamaḥ dṛṣṭayo dṛṣṭisaṃprayuktāśca dharmāḥ /
tadanyaḥ savastukālambana ityucyate 		sa gong ma pa'i nyon mongs pa ni sa 'og ma la dmigs pa ma yin no /
'gog pa dang lam la dmigs pa'i nyon mongs pa gang yin pa de ni de dag la dmigs pa ma yin par blta ste /
de'i dmigs pa ni des yongs su rtog pa'o /
gzhi med pa la dmigs pa'i nyon mongs pa ni lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
de las gzhan pa ni gzhi dang bcas pa la dmigs pa'o /
saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
rāgaḥ pratighena na saṃprayujyate 'dod chags ni khong khro ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
pratighavadvicikitsayāpi na saṃprayujyate khong khro ba dang ji lta bar the tshom dang yang de bzhin no /
śiṣṭeṣu saṃprayogo labhyate lhag ma ni de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
yathā rāgastathā pratigho 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ /
pratigho rāgeṇa mānena dṛṣṭyā ca na saṃprayujyate 		'dod chags dang khong khro ba ji lta ba de bzhin du khong khor ba yang 'dod chags dang nga rgyal dang lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
mānaḥ pratighena vicikitsayā ca na saṃprayujyate nga rgyal ni khong khro ba dang the tshom dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
avidyā dvividhā /
sarvakleśasaṃprayuktā avidyā 		ma rig pa ni nyon mongs pa thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang ma 'dres pa yang yin no /
asāmānyā avidyā /
asāmānya avidyā katamā /
satyeṣvajñānam 		ma 'dres pa ni bden pa rnams mi shes pa'o /
lta ba ni khong khro ba dang the tshom dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
dṛṣṭiḥ pratighena vicikitsayā ca na saṃprayujyate the tshom ni 'dod chags dang nga rgyal dang lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
krodhādaya upakleśā anyo 'nyaṃ na saṃprayujyante khro ba la sogs pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams ni phan tshun mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no /
āhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ ca sarvatrākuśale sāmānyena saṃprayujyete ngo tsha med pa dang khrel med pa ni mi dge ba thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan no /
styānamauddhatyamāśraddhyaṃ kausīdyaṃ pramādaśca sarvatra kliṣṭe saṃprayujyate rmugs pa dang rgod pa dang ma dad pa dang le lo dang bag med pa ni nyon mongs pa can thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan no /
paryāyaḥ katamaḥ rnam grangs gang zhe na /
sarvakleśā nānārthāśrayā nānavasthāḥ paryāyāḥ /
saṃyojanaṃ bandhanaṃ anuśayaḥ upakleśaḥ paryavasthānam oghaḥ yogaḥ upādānam granthaḥ nivaraṇam khilaḥ malaḥ nighaḥ śalyaḥ kiṃcanaḥ duścaritam āsravaḥ vighātaḥ paridāhaḥ raṇaḥ jvaraḥ vanasaḥ vibandhaḥ 		kun tu sbyor ba dang 'ching ba dang bag la nyal dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang kun nas dkris pa dang chu bo dang sbyor ba dang nye bar len pa dang mdud pa dang sgrib pa dang tha ba dang dri ma dang sdig pa dang zug rdu dang ci yang dang nyes par spyod pa dang zag pa dang phongs pa dang yongs su gdung pa dang 'khrug pa dang 'thab pa dang rims nad dang nags sbyor dang gags zhes bya ba dag go /
saṃyojanāni kati kathaṃ saṃyojanaṃ kutra saṃyojanam /
saṃyojanāni nava /
anunayasaṃyojanam pratighasaṃyojanam mānasaṃyojanam avidyāsaṃyojanam dṛṣṭisaṃyojanam parāmarśasaṃyojanam vicikitsāsaṃyojanam īrṣyāsaṃyojanam mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ ca 		kun tu sbyor ba rnams ni du zhig /
ji ltar gang du sbyor zhe na /
kun tu sbyor ba dgu ste /
rjes su chags pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang khong khro ba'i kun tu sbyor ba dang nga rgyal gyi kun tu sbyor ba dang ma rig pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang lta ba'i kun dang sbyor ba dang mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang the tshom gyi kun tu sbyor ba dang phrag dog gi kun tu sbyor ba dang ser sna'i kun tu sbyor ba'o /
anunayasaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
traidhātuko rāgaḥ 		rjes su chags pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni khams gsum pa'i 'dod chags so /
anunayasaṃprayojanena saṃprayuktaḥ traidhātukaṃ nodvejayati rjes su chags pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni khams gsum pa la yid 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro /
anudvegena kuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tena āyatyāṃ duḥkhābhinivṛtto duḥkhena saṃyujyate 		yid mi 'byung bas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod do /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang kun tu sbyor ro /
pratighasaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
sattveṣu duḥkhe duḥkhasthānīyeṣu na dharmeṣu cittasya vihiṃsā /
pratighasaṃyojanena saṃprayukto pratighanimitteṣu cittaṃ nopekṣate /
anupekṣayā ca akuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tena āyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhābhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate 		khong khro ba'i kun tu sbyor ba ni sems can dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi gnas kyi chos rnams la sems kyi kun nas mnar sems pa'o /
khong khro ba'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni khong khro ba'i rgyu las sems yal bar mi 'dor te /
des na mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod do /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
mānasaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
sapta mānāḥ 		nga rgyal gyi kun tu sbyor ba ni nga rgyal bdun te /
māno 'timāno mānatimāno 'smimāno 'bhimāna ūnamāno mithyāmānaśca /
mānaḥ katamaḥ /
hīnān śreyānasmi a sadṛśena sadṛśo 'smīti vā yā cittasyonnatiḥ 		nga rgyal dang che ba'i nga rgyal dang nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang cung zad snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang log pa'i nga rgyal lo /
nga rgyal gang zhe na /
chung ngu bas bdag che ba'am /
mtshungs pa dang mtshungs so snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
atimānaḥ katamaḥ che ba'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
sadṛśāt śreyānasmi śreyasā sadṛśo 'smīti vā yā cittasyonnatiḥ mtshungs pa bas bdag che ba'am /
che ba dang mtshungs so snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
mānātimānaḥ katamaḥ nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal gang zhe na /
śreyasaḥ śreyānasmīti yā cittasyonnatiḥ che ba bas kyang bdag ches che'o snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
asmimānaḥ katamaḥ /
pañcasūpādānaskandheṣvātmātmīyābhiniveśādyā cittasyonnatiḥ 		nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po rnams la bdag gam bdag gir yang dag par rjes su lta ba'i sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
abhimānaḥ katamaḥ mngon pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
aprāpta uttare viśeṣā dhigame prāpto mayeti yā cittasyonnatiḥ gong ma'i khyad par thob par bya ba ma thob par bdag gis thob bo snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
ūnamānaḥ katamaḥ /
vahvantaraviśiṣṭādalpāntarahīno 'smīti yā cittasyonnatiḥ 		cung zad snyam pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
ches 'phags pa bas bdag cung zad gcig gis chung ngo snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
log pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
mithyāmānaḥ katamaḥ yon tan ma yin pa dang ldan pa la /
aguṇavato guṇavānasmīti yā cittasyonnatiḥ bdag yon tan dang ldan no snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
mānasaṃyojanena saṃprayukta ātmātmīyau na saṃjānāti nga rgyal gyi kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni ngar 'dzin pa dang nga yir 'dzin pa yongs su mi shes so /
asaṃjñānāt ātmātmīyagrahaḥ akuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalā samudācāraśca yongs su ma shes na ngar 'dzin pa dang nga yir 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen nas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod de /
tenāyatyāṃ duḥkhābhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
traidhātukamajñānam 		ma rig pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni khams gsum pa'i mi shes pa'o /
avidyasaṃyojanena saṃprayuktā duḥkhadharmān samudayadharmān nādhyavasyati ma rig pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni sdug bsngal gyi chos rnams dang kun 'byung ba'i chos rnams la lhag par chags so /
anadhyavasāyena akuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca de dag la lhag par chags pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod do /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥsvābhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
tisro dṛṣṭhayaḥ /
satkāyadṛṣṭirantāgrāhadṛṣṭirmithyāḥdṛṣṭiśca 		lha ba'i kun tu sbyor ba ni lta ba gsum ste /
'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang log par lta ba'o /
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanena saṃprayukto mithyāniḥsaraṇaṃ parikalpitavipratisāraṃ paryeṣane abhiniviśate /
mithyāniḥsaraṇābhiniveśenākuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhabhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate 		lta ba'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni log pas nges par 'byung ba yongs su tshol lo /
mngon par zhen to /
log pas nges par 'byung ba la mngon par zhen pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod de /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca 		mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
parāmarśasaṃyojanena saṃprayukto mithyāniḥsaraṇopāyaṃ kalpayatyabhiniviśate /
mithyāniḥsaraṇopāyāminiveśenākuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhābhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate 		mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni log pas nges par 'byung ba'i thabs la mngon par zhen pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod do /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
satyeṣu vimatiḥ 		the tshom gyi kun tu sbyor ba ni bden pa rnams la yid gnyis za ba'o /
vicikitsāsaṃyojanena saṃprayukto buddhadharmasaṃgheṣu ratneṣu vicikitsate ratnatrayaṃ na samudāvarati the tshom gyi kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni sangs rgyas dkon mchog la som nyi za zhing /
chos dkon mchog dang dge 'dun dkon mchog la som nyi za ba'o /
dkon mchog rnams la som nyi za bas legs par bsgrub par mi 'gyur ro /
ratnatrayāsamudācāreṇākuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsanudācāraśca dkon mchog rnams la legs par mi bsgrub pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod de /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhābhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sangs rgyas dang sbyor ro /
īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
lābhasatkārādhyavasitasya parasaṃpattāvamarṣakṛtaścetaso vyāroṣaḥ 		phrag dog gi kun tu sbyor ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par chags pas pha rol gyi phung sum tshogs pa la mi bzod par byas pa'i sems khong nas 'khrug pa'o /
īrṣyāsaṃyojanena saṃprayukto lābhasatkārān anunayati dharmaṃ na gurukaroti phrag dog gi kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti gces su 'dzin pa yin gyi chos gces su 'dzin pa ma yin no /
lābhasatkāragurukāreṇā kuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhabhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate 		rnyed pa dang bkur sti gces su 'dzin pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod de /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ katamat /
lābhasatkārādhyavasitasya pariṣkāreṣu cetasa āgrahaḥ 		ser sna'i kun tu sbyor ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par chags pa nyid yod byed rnams la sems kun tu 'dzin pa'o /
mātsaryasaṃyojanena saṃprayukta upacayamanunayati ta dvarjanatāṃ ca na satkaroti /
upacayānunayenākuśalasamudācāraḥ kuśalāsamudācāraśca /
tenāyatyāṃ laukikaduḥkhabhinivṛttau duḥkhena saṃyujyate /
bandhanaṃ trividham /
rāgabandhanaṃ dveṣabandhanaṃ mohabandhanaṃ ca 		ser sna'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni sogs pa gces su 'dzin pa yin gyi yo byed bsnyungs pa gces su 'dzin pa ma yin te /
sogs pa gces su 'dzin pas mi dge ba spyod cing dge ba mi spyod de /
des phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par byed pas sdug bsngal dang sbyor ro /
'ching ba ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi 'ching ba dang zhe sdang gi 'ching ba dang; gti mug gi 'ching ba'o /
rāgabandhanena sattvānāṃ viparīṇāmaduḥkhatāyāṃ bandhanam 'dod chags kyi 'ching bas ni 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid la 'ching bar 'gyur ro /
dveṣabandhanena sattvānāṃ duḥkhaduḥkhatāyāṃ bandhanam zhe sdang gi 'ching bas ni sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid la 'ching bar 'gyur ro /
mohabandhanena sattvānāṃ saṃskāraduḥkhatāyāṃ bandhanam gting mug gi 'ching bas ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid la 'ching bar 'gyur ro /
apica rāgadveṣamohānniśritya kuśalasamudācāreṣu na vaśavarttitāṃ labhate yang 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug la brten nas /
dge ba la sbyor ba na 'dod pa bzhin du byed pa mi 'thob ste /
ata ucyate bandhanam /
anuśayāḥ sapta /
kāmarāgānuśayaḥ pratighānuśayaḥ bhavarāgānuśayaḥ mānānuśayaḥ avidyānuśayaḥ dṛṣṭayanuśayaḥ vicikitsānuśayaśca 		de'i phyir yang de dag ni 'ching ba rnams so /
bag la nyal ni bdun te /
'dod pa la 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal dang khong khro ba'i bag la nyal dang; srid pa'i 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal dang nga rgyal gyi bag la nyal dang ma rig pa'i bag la nyal dang lta ba'i bag la nyal dang the tshom gyi bag la nyal lo /
kāmarāgānuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
kāmarāgapakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		'dod pa la 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal ni 'dod pa la 'dod chags kyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
pratighānuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
pratighapakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		khong khro ba'i bag la nyal ni khong khro ba'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
bhavarāgānuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
rūpārūpyarāgapakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		srid pa'i 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i 'dod chags kyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
mānānuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
mānapakṣīyaṃ doṣṭhulyam /
avidyānuśayaḥ katamaḥ avidyāpakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		nga rgyal gyi bag la nyal ni nga rgyal gyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
ma rig pa'i bag la nyal ni ma rig pa'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
dṛṣṭyanuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
dṛṣṭipakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		lta ba'i bag la nyal ni lta ba'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
vicikitsānuśayaḥ katamaḥ /
vicikitsāpakṣīyaṃ dauṣṭhulyam 		the tshom gyi bag la nyal ni the tshom gyi phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len to /
kāmaiṣāṇāyā aviratasya kāmarāgapratighānuśayāvanuśayāte 'dod pa tshol ba ma spangs pas ni 'dod pa la 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal dang khong khro ba'i bag la nyal rgyas par 'gyur ro /
bhaveṣaṇāyā aviratasya bhavarāgānuśayo 'nuśete srid pa tshol ba ma spangs pas ni srid pa'i 'dod chags kyi bag la nyal rgyas par 'gyur ro /
mithyābrahmacaryaiṣaṇāyā aviratasya mānāvidyādṛṣṭi vicikitsānuśayā anuśerate /
te sattvā hīnapratipakṣaṃ labhante mado mānaścotpadyate āryasatyeṣu saṃmohaśca 		log pas tshangs par spyod pa tshol bam spangs pas ni nga rgyal gyi bag la nyal dang ma rig pa'i bag la nyal dang lta ba'i bag la nyal dang the tshom gyi bag la nyal rgyas par 'gyur te /
'di ltar de dag ni gnyen po chung du tsam gyis kyang khengs par 'gyur ro /
bden pa rnams la rmongs par 'gyur ro /
mithyāmokṣaṃ mokṣopāyaṃ ca saṃtorayanti buddhaśāsanadharmavinayeṣu vimatiḥ vicikitsā ca log pas thar pa dang thar pa'i thabs la rtog par byed do /
sangs rgyas rnams kyi bstan pa dam pa'i chos 'dul ba la som nyi za'o /
the tshom za'o /
upakleśastu yakleśāste upakleśā api bhavanti /
upakleśāstu na kleśāḥ /
kleśān sthāpayitvā tadanyaḥ kliṣṭaḥ saṃskāraskandhasaṃgṛhītaḥ sarvaścaitasiko dharmaḥ /
sa punaḥ katamaḥ /
ṣaḍrāgādīn kleśān sthāpayitvā kliṣṭaḥ saṃskāraskandhasaṃgṛhītaḥ krodhādikaścaitasiko dharmaḥ /
api khalu rāgo dveṣo mohaśca caitasikā upakleśā ucyante 		nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams ni nyon mongs pa gang dag yin pa de dag nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyang yin no /
nye ba'i nyon mongs pa yin la nyon mongs pa ma yin pa yang yod de /
nyon mongs pa rnams ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa sems las byung ba'i 'du byed kyi phung po nyon mongs pa can no /
yang 'dod chags ni sems las byung ba'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o /
zhe sdang dang gti mug ni sems las byung ba'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa ste /
yaiścitte upakleśo na vairāgyaṃ na viumokṣo nāvaraṇaprahāṇam /
ata ucyante upakleśāḥ /
tathā ca bhagavatoktam dīrgharātraṃ vo rāgadveṣamohā upakliśyantui vikṣipanti citraṃ saṃkliśyanti /
paryavasthānānyaṣṭau /
styānaṃ middhamauddhatyaṃ kaukṛtyamīrṣyā mātsaryamāhikyamanapatrāpyaṃ ca /
punaḥ punaḥ udvegena cittaṃ paryayanahyantīti paryavasthānāni 		nye ba'i nyon mongs pa des sems nye ba'i nyon mongs pa can du gyur na /
chags pa dang bral bar mi 'gyur /
grol bar mi 'gyur te /
sgrib pa de ma spangs pa'i phyir ro /
bcom ldan 'das kyis ji skad du /
sems 'di yun ring po nas 'dod chags kyis kun nas nyon mongs pa can du gyur pa /
zhe sdang dang gti mug gis kun nas nyon mongs pa can du gyur pa zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
kun nas dkris pa ni brgyad de rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod pa dang 'gyod pa dang phrag dog dang ser sna dang ngo tsha med pa dang khrel med pa'o /
tathāca śamathapragrahanimittabhāvanākāle tatsanniśraya brahmacaryā diśuddhi saṃgṛhītaśīla kāle cittaṃ paryavanahyanti zhi gnas kyi dus dang rab tu 'dzin pa'i dus dang btang snyoms kyi dus dang de dag gi gzhi dang po rnam par dag pa'i dus na /
yang dang yang shas cher sems la kun nas 'khri bar byed pas kun nas dkris pa dag go /
oghaścaturvidhaḥ /
kāmaughaḥ mavaughaḥ dṛṣṭcoghaḥ avidyaughaśca /
stroto 'nukūlaḥ pravāhāvartta oghārthaḥ 		chu bo ni bzhi ste 'dod pa'i chu bo dang srid pa'i chu bo dang lta ba'i chu bo dang ma rig pa'i chu bo'o /
rgyun phyogs su khyer bar byed pa'i phyir chu bo dag go /
saṃkeśānvayataḥ /
ādyaḥ kāmaiṣaṇābhāvanā 		'dod pa tshol ba la zhugs pa'i ni dang po'o /
dvitīyaḥ bhavaiṣaṇābhāvanā srid pa tshol ba la zhugs pa'i ni gnyis pa'o /
aparāvubhau mithyābrahmacaryaiṣaṇābhāvanā /
āśrayāśritasaṃbandhayogena /
yogaścaturvidhaḥ /
kāmayogaḥ bhavayogaḥ dṛṣṭiyogaḥ avidyāyogaśca 		log bas tshangs par spyod pa tshol ba la zhugs pa'i ni tha ma gnyis te /
gnas pa dang gnas 'brel pa'i tshul gyis so /
sbyor ba ni bzhi ste /
'dod pa'i sbyor ba dang srid pa'i sbyor ba dang lta ba'i sbyor ba dang ma rig pa'i sbyor ba'o /
visaṃyogaparipanthakaro yogārthaḥ 'bral ba'i bar du gcod pa'i phyir sbyor ba rnams te /
viśuddhiviparyayataḥ /
te punaryathāyogameṣaṇātrayabhāvanā /
upādānāni catvāri 		de dag kyang tshol ba la zhugs pa gsum po rnams kyi yin te /
ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
nye bar len pa ni bzhi ste /
kāmopādānaṃ dṛṣṭyupādānaṃ śīlavratopādānamātmavādopādānaṃ ca /
vivādamūlopādānaṃ paunarbhavikopādānaṃ copādānaṃ draṣṭavyam 		'dod pa'i nye bar len pa dang lta ba'i nye bar len pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyi nye bar len pa dang bdag tu smra ba'i nye bar len pa'o /
rtsod pa'i rtsa ba nye bar len pa'i phyir te /
de'i phyir yang srid pa nye bar len pa'i phyir nye bar len pa rnams so /
tena kiṃ bhavati /
kāmarāgavibandhagredhāsaṃkleśahetunā gṛhiṇo 'nyo 'nyaṃ vivadanti /
tadu vivādamūlaṃ prathamamupādanam 		'dod pa la 'dod chags dang ltag par zhen pa dang rnam par bcings pa dang yongs su zhen pa dang kun tu 'dod chags kyi rgyus khyim pa rnams dang khyim pa rnams su rtsod do /
rtsod pa de'i rtsa ba ni dang po yin no /
dṛṣṭirāgavibandhagredhā saṃkleśahetunā pravrajitā anyo 'nyaṃ vivadanti /
tad vivādamūlamaparamupādānatrayam 		lta ba la 'dod chags dang lhag par zhen pa dang rnam par bcings pa dang yongs su zhen pa dang kun tu 'dod chags kyi rgyus rab tu byung ba rnams dang rab tu byung ba rnams su rtsod de /
rtsod pa de'i rtsa ba ni nye bar len pa gsum po dag ste /
dvāṣaṣṭirdṛṣṭigatayo dṛṣṭyupādānam lta bar gyur pa drug cu rtsa gnyis ni lta ba'i nye bar len pa'o /
nānāvṛtaśīlaiḥ kṛcchraṃ tapaḥ śīlavratopādānam /
tadāśritā ca satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ ātmavādopādānam /
dṛṣṭiśīlavratopādānābhyāṃ tīrthyā anyo 'nyaṃ vivadanti 		phal cher brtul zhugs dang dka' thub drag po so so tha dad pa dag ni tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyi nye bar len pa'o /
de dag gi gnas 'jig tshogs la lta ba ni bdag tu smra ba'i nye bar len pa'o /
lta ba'i nye bar len pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyi nye bar len pas ni mu stegs can nang phan tshun rtsod do /
ātmavādopādāne tu tīrthyā anyo 'nyaṃ na vivadanti bdag tu smra ba'i nye bar len pas ni mu stegs can rnams dang chos 'di pa rnams su rtsod do /
dhārmikaiḥ sārdhamanyo 'nyaṃ vivadanti /
evaṃ ca vivādamūle 'bhiniveśāt paunarbhavikaduḥkhavipākopādānākṣepāccopādānānyucyante 		de ltar de dag rtsod pa'i rtsa ba nye bar len pa la mngon par zhen pas phyi ma la yang srid pa nye bar len to /
des na nye bar len pa rnams zhes bya'o /
granthāścatvāraḥ mdud pa ni bzhi ste /
abhidhyākāyagranthaḥ vyāpādakāyagranthaḥ śīlavrata parāmarśakāyagranthaḥ tatsatyābhiniveśopādānakāyagranthaśca /
samāhitamanaḥsvabhāvasya kāyasya parigranthārthena grantho veditavyaḥ /
tena kiṃ bhavati 		brnab sems lus kyi mdud pa dang gnod sems lus kyi mdud pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa lus kyi mdud pa dang 'di bden no zhes mchog tu 'dzin cing mngon par zhen pa lus kyi mdud pa'o /
caturvidhaṃ cittaṃ vikṣipyate /
vittādiṣu anunayahetoḥ cittaṃ vikṣipyate 		mnyam par gzhag pa'i yid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus kyi bar du gcod pa'i phyir mdud pa rnams te /
vivādastuṣu apratipattihetoḥ cittaṃ vikṣipyate /
duṣkaraśīlavrataduḥkhahetoḥ cittaṃ vikṣipyate /
ayoniśo jñeya santīraṇahetoḥ cittaṃ vikṣipyatee /
nivaraṇāni pañca /
kāmacchandanivaraṇam vyāpādanivaraṇam styānamiddhanivaraṇam auddhatyakaukṛtyanivaraṇam vicikitsānivaraṇaṃ ca 		'di ltar g yeng ba'i rgyu ni bzhi ste /
zang zing cung zad tsam gyi rgyus sems g yeng ba dang rtsod pa la legs par mi bsgrub pa'i rgyu dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs drag pos sdug bsngal bar gnas pa'i rgyu dang tshul bzhin ma yin pas shes bya la rtog pa'i rgyus sems g yeng bar byed do /
sgrib pa ni lnga ste /
'dod pa la 'dun pa'i sgrib pa dang gnod sems dang rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod pa dang 'gyod pa dang the tshom gyi sgrib pa ste /
kuśalapakṣasyāsaṃprakhyānaṃ nivaraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam /
tacca pravrajyāyāmabhiratau codanāyāṃ pratipattau śamathe pragrahe upekṣāyāṃ ca 		rab tu byung ba la mngon par dga' ba'i dus dang bskul ba na legs par bsgrub pa'i dus dang zhi gnas kyi dus dang rab tu 'dzin pa'i dus dang btang snyoms kyi dus na dge ba'i phyogs mi rtogs pa'i rgyu yin pas sgrib pa rnams so /
khilastrividhaḥ tha ba ni gsum ste /
rāgakhilo dveṣakhilo mohakhilaśca 'dod chags kyi tha ba dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi tha ba'o /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya pūrvābhyāsena rāgādicaryāpariniṣpādanam 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
sngon goms pa'i tshul gyis 'dod chags la sogs pa la spyod par 'gyur te /
cittasyādāntatayā akarmaṇyatayā durvimokṣatayā ca sattvaistasyāścaryāyā durbhedyatvāt khila ityucyate spyod pa de ma spangs pas sems las su mi rung ba dang dpral dka' bar 'gyur ba de dag ni tha ba rnams zhes bya'o /
malāstrayaḥ dri ma ni gsum ste /
rāgamalo dveṣamalo mohamalaśca /
tacca rāgadveṣamohānniśritya dauśīlam 		'dod chags kyi dri ma dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi dri ma'o /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
tat saṃprajānabdiḥ sabrahmacāribhirgrāme vā araṇye vā tathā kurvantaṃ paśyadbhirucyate ayaṃ khalvāyuṣmān karotyevaṃ kṛtyaṃ caratyevamācaritaṃ grāmakaṇṭaka āmiṣo 'śuciḥ de'i ngo bo'i 'chal ba'i tshul khrims lhag par spyod de /
grong na 'dug kyang rung dgon pa na 'dug kyang rung /
tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa mkhas pa rnams kyis mthong na /
ato malā nāma /
nighāstrayaḥ /
rāganigho dveṣanigho mohanighaśca /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya dīrghakālaṃ punaḥ punarjātimaraṇeṣu vilaśyante ityucyante nighāḥ /
śalyāstrayaḥ /
rāgaśalyo dveṣaśalyo mohaśalyaśca /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya bhave bhavopakaraṇeṣu vā adhyeṣaṇāsamutpādena prabandhānupacchedena buddhe dharme saṃghe duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgeṣu vā vicikitsāsamutpādena vā śalyā nāma 		gang gi phyir 'di skad du /
tshe dang ldan pa 'di ni 'di lta bu byed pa 'di lta bu spyod pa ste /
mi gtsang ba grong gi tsher ma'o /
zhes brjod par 'gyur ba de dag ni dri ma rnams zhes bya'o /
sdig pa ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi sdig pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi sdig pa'o /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas dus ring por skye ba dang 'chi ba myong bar 'gyur ba de dag ni sdig pa rnams zhes bya'o /
zug rdu ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi zug rdu dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi zug rdu'o /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad rnams la shin tu 'dod pa skyes shing gnas te /
sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun rnams dang sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam rnams la the tshom za ba de dag ni zug rdu rnams zhes bya'o; /
kiṃcanāstrayaḥ /
rāgakiṃcano dveṣakiṃcano mohakiṃcanaśca 		ci yang ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi ci yang dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi ci yang ngo /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya vittasaṃcayeṣu sabhayāḥ savairā bhūyo vihāravikṣepāḥ kiṃcanā nāma 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas 'jigs pa dang bcas pa kho na dang bcas shing g yeng ba mang bar gnas pa de dag ni ci yang rnams zhes bya'o /
duścaritāni trīṇi /
rāgaduścaritaṃ dveṣaduścaritaṃ mohaduścaritaṃ ca 		nyes par spyod pa ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi nyes par spyod pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi nyes par spyod pa'o /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya kāyavāṅmanoduścaritāni carantīti duścaritānītyucyate /
punaḥ rāgadveṣamohānniśrityotpannānāṃ bahūnāmakuśaladuścaritānāmakuśalamūlatvena tribhirvyavasthānam /
tat katham /
sattvā loke āmiṣakiṃcitkahato caranti /
loke 'pakāra nimittaparikalpahatoḥ duścaritaṃ caranti 		'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas lus kyis nyes par spyod pa spyod pa dang ngag dang yid kyis nyes par spyad pa spyod pa de dag ni nyes par spyod pa rnams zhes bya'o /
yang zang zing ngan pa cung zad tsam gyi rgyu dang gnod par bya ba'i rgyu la yongs su rtog pa'i rgyu dang chos log pa la mngon par zhen pa'i rgyus sems can rnams nyes par spyod pa spyod de /
loke mithyādharmābhiniveśahetoḥ duścaritaṃ caranti /
iti te rāgadveṣamohā duścaritāni akuśalamūlāni 		de lta bas na 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug ni nyes par spyod pa'i rtsa ba rnams zhes bya'o /
āsravāsrayaḥ /
kāmāsravo bhavāsravo 'vidyāsravaśca /
cittāvesāraṃ strataṃ kurvantī tyāsravāḥ ityucyante /
te punaḥ katham /
bahirdhā visāraṃ niśritya kāmāsravaḥ 		zag pa ni gsum ste /
'dod pa'i zag pa dang srid pa'i zag pa dang ma rig pa'i zag pa'o /
sems rnam par 'phro bar zag par byed pa dang phyi rol tu bltas te zag pa'i phyir 'dod pa'i zag pa'o /
antardhāvisāraṃ niśritya bhavāsravaḥ /
tadubhayāśrayavisāraṃ niśritya avidyāsravaḥ 		nang du bltas te zag pa'i phyir srid pa'i zag pa'o /
zag pa de gnyi ga'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ma rig pa'i zag pa'o /
vighātāstrayaḥ /
rāgavighāto dveṣavighāto mohavighātaśca 		phongs pa ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyis phongs pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gis phongs pa'o /
rāgadveṣamohānniśritya bhave pariṣkareṣu vā eṣaṇā /
abhāve vighāte sarvadā dāridya duḥkhādibhiḥ kliṣṭā bhavantīti vighātāḥ 		'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas srid pa'i yo byad 'dod pa'i phongs pas gnod par byed pa de dag ni phongs pa rnams zhes bya'o /
paridāhāstrayaḥ /
rāgaparidāho dveṣaparidāho mohaparidāhaśca 		yongs su gdung ba ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi yongs su gdung ba dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi yongs su gdung ba'o /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa ayoniśo nimittābhiniveśo 'nuvyañjanābhiniveśaśca 'dod chags dang zhes sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas tshul bzhin ma yin par mtshan mar 'dzin pa dang mngon rtags su 'dzin par 'gyur te /
tena nimittānuvyañjanābhiniveśena kāyaṃ cittaṃ ca paridahantīti paridāhāḥ /
upāyāsāstrayaḥ /
rāgopāyāso dveṣopāyāso mohopāyasaśca /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa tatra tatra ratiradhyavasānaṃ ca 		mtshan mar 'dzin pa dang mngon par rtags su 'dzin pa des lus yongs su gdung bar 'gyur ba dang sems yongs su gdung bar 'gyur ba de dag ni yongs su gdung ba rnams zhes bya'o /
'khrug pa ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi 'khrug pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi 'khrug pa'o /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
tadvipariṇāme śokaparidevanāduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyasaiḥ spṛṣṭā bhavantītyu pāyāsāḥ /
raṇāstrayaḥ /
rāgaraṇo dveṣaraṇo moharaṇaśca /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa śastrādānadaṇḍādibhiḥ raṇayanti nānāvidhaṃ bhaṇḍanaṃ kalahaṃ kurvantīti rāgādayo raṇā ucyante 		gang du dga' ba dang lhag par chags par gyur pa de rnams par gyur cing gzhan du gyur na mya ngan dang sgra sngags 'don pa dang sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba dang 'khrug pa rnams kyis reg par 'gyur pa de dag ni 'khrug pa rnams zhes bya'o /
'thab pa ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi 'thab pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi 'thab pa'o /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
chad pas gcod pa dang mtshon cha len pa dang dbyug pa len pa dang 'thab pa dang mtshang 'dru ba dang rtsod pa dang 'gyed pa 'byung ba de dag ni 'thab pa rnams zhes bya'o /
jvarāstrayaḥ /
rāgajvaro dveṣajvaro moha jvaraśca 		rims nad ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi rims nad dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi rims nad do /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa adharmarāgeṇa mahādahanena paridahanti viṣamalobhena mahādahanena paridahanti mithyādharmeṇa mahādahanena paridahantīti jvarā nāma 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
chos ma yin pa la 'dod chags pa yongs su gdung ba chen pos yongs su gdung bar 'gyur ba dang mi mthun pas chags pa yongs su gdung ba chen pos yongs su gdung bar 'gyur ba dang chos log pa'i yongs su gdung ba chen pos yongs su gdung bar 'gyur ba de dag ni rims nad rnams zhes bya'o /
vanasāstrayaḥ nags sbyor ni gsum ste /
rāgavanaso dveṣavanaso mohavanasaśca /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa jātimaraṇamūleṣu saṃskāreṣu saṃyojayanti saṃjanayanti sattvān nānāvidhakāyeṣu pañcagatisaṃsāreṣu abhinirvarttayantīti rāgādayo vanasā ityucyante 		'dod chags kyi nags sbyor dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi nags sbyor ro /
'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
skye ba'i rtsa ba can 'du byed rnams la chags te /
'gro ba lnga'i 'khor bar lus rnam pa sna tshogs mngon par 'grub par byed pa de dag ni nags sbyor rnams zhes bya'o /
vibandhāstrayaḥ /
rāgavibandho dveṣavibandho mohavibandhaśca 		gags ni gsum ste /
'dod chags kyi gags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi gags so /
rāgadveṣamohasanniśrayeṇa kāyasāpekṣatā vittasāpekṣatā bodhyabhāvaḥ kolāhalaratiḥ parittakuśaladharmalābhe 'pi santoṣaḥ /
taiḥ kuśaladharmānna bhāvayantīti vibandhāḥ ucyante 		'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag la brten nas /
lus la lta ba dang bcas pas dge ba la mi sbyor ba dang longs spyod la lta ba dang bcas pa dang blo ma byang ba dang 'dre zhing gnas pa dang cung zad tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pas dge ba la mi sbyor ba de dag ni gags rnams zhes bya'o /
evamādayaḥ kleśārthānāṃ paryāyā apramāṇāḥ /
vipratipattiḥ katamā /
rāgaḥ pratighaśca dvau kleśau viṣaye dṛṣṭau ca vipratipannau 		log par zhugs pas ji lta bu zhe na /
'dod chags ni yul dang lta ba la log par rtogs pa'o /
'dod chags ji lta bar khong khro ba yang de bzhin no /
mānaḥ sattveṣu dṛṣṭau ca vipratipannaḥ nga rgyal ni sems can rnams dang lta ba la log par rtogs pa'o /
satkāyāntagrāhamithyādṛṣṭayo jñeye vipratipannāḥ 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang log par lta ba ni shes bya la log par rtogs pa'o /
dṛṣṭiparāmarśaśīlavrataparāmarśau dṛṣṭau vipratipannau lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa ni lta ba la log par rtogs pa'o /
vicikitsā pratipakṣe vipratipannā the tshom ni gnyen po la log par rtogs pa'o /
avidyā sarvatra vipratipannā ma rig pa ni thams cad la log par rtogs pa'o /
daśa kleśā duḥkhe samudaye ca vipratipannāḥ /
tannidānapadasthānataḥ 		nyon mongs pa bcu po thams cad ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba la de'i rgyu dang gzhi'i gnas kyis kyang log par rtogs pa'o /
punaḥ daśa kleśā nirodhe mārge ca vipratipannāḥ /
taistatrotrāsasaṃjananataḥ 		nyon mongs pa bcu po thams cad ni 'gog pa dang lam la yang de la skrag pa skyed pas log par zhugs pa'o /
dhātu katamaḥ /
pratighaṃ sthāpayitvā tadanye sarve traidhātukapratisaṃyuktāḥ 		khams kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
khong khro ba ma gtogs par khams gsum pa thams cad do /
pratighastu kāmadhātupratisaṃyuktaḥ khong khro ba ni 'dod pa dang ldan pa'o /
api khalu rāgaḥ kāmadhātau sukhasaumanasyopekṣābhi saṃprayujyate 'dod chags ni 'dod pa'i khams na bde ba dang yid bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
yathā kāmadhātau tathā prathamadvitīyadhyānayoḥ /
tṛtīyadhyāne sukhopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate 		'dod pa'i khams la ji ltar bar bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa'ang de bzhin no /
gsum pa na ni bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
tadūrdhvamupekṣayā saṃprayujyate de yan chad du btang snyoms kho na dang mtshungs par ldan no /
pratigho duḥkhadaurmanasyosukhopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate khong khro ba ni sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
mānaḥ kāmadhātau saumanasyopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate nga rgyal ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
prathamadvitīyadhyānayo sukhasaumanasyopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate /
tṛtīyadhyāne sukhopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate 		bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa la ni bde ba dang yid bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
gsum pa la ni bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
tadūrdhvamupekṣayaiva saṃprayujyate de yan chad du ni btang snyoms kho na dang mtshungs par ldan no /
yathā mānastathā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ antagrāhadṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca nga rgyal ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang lta ba mchog tu 'dzin par lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa yang de bzhin no /
mithyādṛṣṭiḥ kāmadhātau daurmanasyasaumanasyopekṣābhiḥ saṃprayujyate log par lta ba ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no; /
rūpadhātāvārupyadhātau ca yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
vicikitsā kāmadhātau dauramanasyopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate the tshom ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
rūpadhātāvārūpyadhātau ca yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate /
avidyā dvividhā 		gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
saṃprayuktā asāmānyā ca /
sarvakleśasaṃprayogataḥ saṃprayuktā avidyā yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate 		ma rig pa ni nyon mongs pa thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan pa yin pas gang na tshor ba gang yod pa de dang der mtshungs par ldan pa can zhes bya'o /
āsāmānyā avidyā kāmadhātau daurmanasyopekṣābhyāṃ saṃprayujyate ma rig pa ma 'dres pa gang yin pa de ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no /
tadūrdhvadhātau yathāveditaṃ saṃprayujyate de yan chad du ni tshor ba gang yod pa de dang mtshungs par ldan no /
kathaṃ sarvakleśā upekṣayā saṃprayujyante ci'i phyir nyon mongs pa thams cad btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan zhe na /
sarvakleśānāmaudāsīnyamāgamyāstagamanatāmupādāya tha mal par 'dug pa la brten nas nub par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
api khalu rāgaḥ kāmadhātau ṣaḍvijñānakāyikaḥ /
yathā rāgastathā pratigho 'vidyā ca 		'dod chags ni 'dod pa'i khams na rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug dang mtshungs par ldan no /
'dod chags ji lta bar khong khro ba dang ma rig pa yang de bzhin no /
rāgo rūpadhātau caturvijñānakāyikāḥ gzugs kyi khams na ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs bzhin dang mtshungs par ldan no /
ārūpyadhātau manovijñānakāyikaḥ /
yathā rāgastathā avidyā /
māno dṛṣṭirvicikitsā ca sarvatra manovijñānakāyikāḥ /
api khalu rāgaḥ pratigho mānaśca kāmadhātau vastvekadeśapravṛttikāḥ 		gzugs med pa'i khams na ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang mtshungs par ldan no /
'dod chags ji lta bar ma rig pa yang de bzhin no /
nga rgyal dang lta ba dang the tshom ni thams cad du yang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang mtshungs par ldan no /
'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal ni 'dod pa'i khams na dngos po'i phyogs gcig la 'jug go /
kāmadhātuvad rūpadhātāvārūpyadhātāvapi śiṣṭāḥ kleśāḥ sarvatra sarvavastu pravṛttikāḥ 'dod pa'i khams na ji ltar bar gzugs kyi khams dang gzugs med pa'i khams na yang de bzhin no /
lhag ma rnams ni thams cad du yang dngos po mtha' dag la 'jug go /
nikāyaḥ katamaḥ /
dvau kleśanikāyau /
darśanaprahātavyanikāyo bhāvanāprahātavyanikāyaśca 		ris kyis ji lta bu zhe na /
nyon mongs pa'i ris gnyis te /
mthong bas spang bar bya ba dang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'o /
darśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ punaścaturvidhaḥ /
duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ samudayadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ /
nirodhadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaḥ mārgadarśanaprahātavyanikāyaśca /
kāmadhātau duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyā daśa kleśāḥ /
duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyavat samudayadarśanaprahātavyāḥ nirodhadarśanaprahātavyā mārgadarśanaprahātavyāśca 		'dod pa'i khams na sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni bcu'o /
sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba ji lta bar kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams kyang de bzhin no /
gzugs kyi khams na sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni dgu'o /
sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams ji lta bar kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam mthong bas spang bar bya ba rnams kyang de bzhin no /
rūpadhātau duḥkhādicaturvidhadarśanaprahātavyāḥ pratyekaṃ navakleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham /
rūpadhātuvadārūpyadhātāvapi /
evaṃ ca darśanaprahātavyakleśanikāyā dvādaśādhikaṃ śataṃ kleśāḥ /
kāmadhātau bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ ṣaṭkleśāḥ /
sahajā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ antaprāhadṛṣṭiḥ rāgaḥ pratigho māno 'vidyā ca /
rūpadhātau bhāvanāprahātavyāḥ pañca kleśāḥ sthāpayitvā pratigham 		gzugs kyi khams na ji lta bar gzugs med pa'i khams na'ang de bzhin te /
de dag mdor bsdu na nyon mongs pa brgya rtsa bcu gnyis ni mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i ris so /
'dod pa'i khams na bsgom pas spang bar bya ba drug ste /
'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba lhan cig skyes pa dang 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa'o /
gzugs kyi khams na khong khro ba ma gtogs par lnga'o /
rūpadhātuvadārūpyadhātāvapi /
evaṃ ca bhāvanāprahātavyanikāyāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ kleśāḥ 		gzugs kyi khams na ji lta bar gzugs med pa'i khams na'ang de bzhin te /
de dag mdor bsdu na bcu drug ni bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i ris so /
prahāṇaṃ katamat spong bas ji ltar bu zhe na /
tathā paryāyaprahāṇaṃ tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam /
tasmāt pratilambhāt prahāṇam 		ji ltar spong ba dang yid la byed pa ci 'dra ba dang gang zhig gang las spong ba'o /
tathā paryāyaprahāṇaṃ katamat /
parijñānataḥ parivarjanataḥ pratipakṣalābhataśca 		ji ltar spong zhe na /
yongs su shes pa dang yongs su spong ba dang gnyen po rnyed pas so /
parijñānaṃ katamat /
tannidānavastuparijñānam svabhāvaparijñānam ādīnavaparijñānaṃ ca 		yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
de'i gzhi'i dngos po yongs su shes pa dang ngo bo nyid yongs su shes pa dang nyes dmigs yongs su shes pa'o /
parivarjanaṃ katamat yongs su spong ba gang zhe na /
tatkālotpannasyānādānam 'byung bar gyur pa dang du mi len pa'o /
pratipakṣalābhaḥ katamaḥ gnyen po rnyed pa gang zhe na /
anutpannasyānutpādata utpannasya varjanato vā pratipakṣa lābhamārgaḥ /
tena manaskāreṇa prahāṇam 		ma skyes pa spang ba'i phyir lam rnyed pa gang yin pa'o /
yid la byed pa ci 'dra bas spong zhe na /
kīdṛśena manaskāreṇa kiṃ prajahāti 'dres pa la dmigs pas spong ste /
asaṃbhinnālambanena manaskāreṇa sarvadharmā anātmāna iti paśyati /
anityākārā iti kleśān prajahāti /
anityākāra parikarmataḥ 		chos thams cad bdag med pa'o zhes bya ba'o /
mi rtag pa'i rnam pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa gang yin pa de dag ni bdag med pa'i rnam pa'i yongs su sbyong bar byed pa'o /
tasmāt pratilambhāt prahāṇam gang zhig gang las spong zhe na /
kasmāt pratilambhāt prajahāti 'das pa ni 'gags pa'i phyir ma yin no /
nātītāt niruddhataḥ /
nānāgatāt anutpannataḥ /
na pratyutpannāt asahabhāvataḥ 		ma 'ongs pa ni ma byung ba'i phyir ma yin no /
de ltar byung ba ni lam dang mnyam du mi 'jug pa'i phyir ma yin no /
kevalaṃ kleśadauṣṭhulyapratilambhāt prajahātīti prahāṇam 'on kyang nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len gang la yod pa de las spong ngo /
yathā yathā dauṣṭhulyamutpadyate tathā tathā pratipakṣa utpadyate yathā yathā pratipakṣa utpadyate tathā tathā dauṣṭhulyanirodhaḥ /
samaṃ samam 		gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa gang gi gnyen po gang byung ba gnyen po'i rnam pa de 'byung ba dang gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa de 'gog pa ni mnyam pas mnyam ste /
yathā loke jyotirutpadyate tamaśca nirudhyate /
tadvisaṃyogato yadānāgatakleśo 'nutpannadhamaṣu avatiṣṭhate tat prahāṇamucyate 		snang ba dang mun pa 'byung ba dang 'gog pa bzhin no /
gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa dang bral bas ma 'ongs pa na nyon mongs pa mi skye ba'i chos can du gnas pa de ni spong ba'o /
kleśādhipateyaṃ karma katamat /
cetanā karma cetayitvā karma ca /
sarvaṃ karmalakṣaṇaṃ nāma /
punaḥ karma pañcavidham /
upalabdhikarma kāritrakarma vyavasāyakarma pariṇatikarma prāptikarma ca 		las gang zhe na /
sems pa'i las dang bsams pa'i las te /
las kyi mtshan nyid mdor bsdus pa'o /
yang las rnam pa lnga ste /
dmigs pa'i las dang byed pa'i las dang rtsol ba'i las dang bsgyur ba'i las dang 'thob pa'i las so /
asmiṃstvarthe yad bhūyasā vyavasāyakarmābhipretam /
cetanākarma katamat 		skabs 'dir phal cher rtsol ba'i las su 'dod do /
sems pa'i las gang zhe na /
puṇyakarma apuṇyakarma āniṃjyakarma ca /
cetayitvā karma katamat 		sems mngon par 'du byed pa yid kyi las te /
bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'o /
bsams pa'i las gang zhe na /
kāyakarma vākkarma manaskarma ca lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las so /
tāni trīṇi kāyavāṅmanaskarmāṇi akuśalāni kuśalāni ca lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las de yang dge ba dang mi dge ba'o /
akuśalāni katamāni daśākuśalakarmapathāḥ /
prāṇātipātaḥ adattādānam kāmamithyācāraḥ mṛṣāvādaḥ piśunavāk paruṣavāk saṃbhinnapralāpaḥ abhidyā vyāpādaḥ mithyādṛṣṭiśca 		mi dge ba ni mi dge ba'i las kyi lam bcu ste /
'di lta ste /
srog gcod pa dang ma byin par len pa dang 'dod pa la log par g yem pa dang brdzun du smra ba dang phra ma dang tshig rtsub po dang tshig kyal ba dang brnab sems dang gnod sems dang log par lta ba'o /
kuśalāni katamāni /
daśa kuśalakarmāpathāḥ 		dge ba ni dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams te /
prāṇātipātād viratiḥ adattādānādviratiḥ kāmamithyācārādviratiḥ mṛṣāvādādviratiḥ piśunavāco viratiḥ paruṣavāco viratiḥ saṃbhinnapralāpādviratiḥ anabhidhyā avyāpādaḥ samyagdṛṣṭiśca /
apica prāṇātipātādīnāṃ yathāyogaṃ pañca lakṣaṇaprabhedāḥ /
vastutaḥ āśayataḥ prayogataḥ kleśataḥ niṣṭhāgamanataśca /
yaduktaṃ sūtre cetanākarma 		'di lta ste /
srog gcod pa spong ba nas tshig kyal ba'i bar du spong ba dang brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa dang yang dag par lta ba'o /
srog gcod pa la sogs pa rnams kyi mtshan nyid ni gzhi dang bsam pa dang sbyor ba dang nyon mongs pa dang zin par byas pas kyang rig par bya'o /
sems pa las gyur pa'i las zhes gang 'byung ba la sems pa las gyur ba gang zhe na /
katamāni cetanākarmāṇi parājñaptisaṃcetanīyatākarma paramasaṃjñaptisaṃcetatīyatākarma avijñāyasaṃcetanīyatākarma mūlābhiniveśasacetanīyatākarma viparyāsasaṃcetanīyatākarma ca /
teṣu mūlābhiniveśasaṃcetanīyatākarma viparyāsaṃcetana yatā karma ca /
teṣu mūlābhiniveśasaṃcetanīyatā karmaviparyāsasaṃcetanīyatākarmabhyāṃ yadi kṛtaṃ bhavatyupacitaṃ ca na nāsya vipākaḥ pratisaṃvedyate 		gzhan gyis bsgo ba sems pa las gyur pa dang gzhan gyis gsol ba btab pa sems pa las gyur pa dang mi shes pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang rtsa ba la mngon par zhen pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang phyin ci log gi sems pa las gyur ba'o /
de la rtsa ba las mngon par zhen pa'i sems pa las gyur pa dang phyin ci log gi sems pa las gyur pa'i las byas shing bsags pa'i rnam par smin pa ni myong bar mi 'gyur ba ma yin no /
kṛtaṃ samudācārasamutthāpitam las kyi byed pa ni kun tu spyod pa'o /
upacitaṃ ca vāsanā samupacitam bsags pa ni bag chags 'phel ba'o /
yadūktaṃ sūtre niyatavedanīyaṃ karma iti /
katame niyaptāḥ karmakiyāniyamaḥ vipākapatisaṃvedanāniyamaḥ avasthāniyamaśca 		myong bar nges pa'i las zhes gang 'byung ba las nges pa gang zhe na /
las byed par nges pa dang rnam par smin pa myong bar nges pa dang dus nges pa'o /
tanna daśānāmakuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalaṃ triṣu apāyeṣu de la mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni ngan song rnams su'o /
mṛdūmadhyādhimātrāṇāṃ tiryakpretanarakeṣu vipākaḥ rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni so so dang mthun par mi'i lus dang yongs su gzungs ba mi 'byor ba'o /
nipyandaphalaṃ pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇa manuṣyeṣūpanannānā mātmabhāvaparigrahayorvipattiḥ /
adhipatiphalaṃ pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇaiva vāhyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ vipattiḥ /
yathoktaṃ sūtre 		bdag po'i 'bras bu ni so so dang mthun pa nyid du phyi'i dngos po mi 'byor ba'o /
de yang mdo las ji skad du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du'o /
daśānāṃ kuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalaṃ devamanuṣyamatiṣūpapadyamānānāṃ deveṣu manuṣyeṣu vā vipākaḥ rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni de dag nyid du so so dang mthun par lus dang yongs su gzung ba phun sum tshogs pa'o /
niṣyandaphalaṃ tadāyataneṣu pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇa ātmābhāvaparigrahayoḥ saṃpattirabhinirvarttate /
adhipattiphalaṃ tadāyataneṣu pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇaiva vāhyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ saṃpattirabhinirvarttate /
kuśalānāmakuśalānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ sugatau durgatau ca vipāko 'bhinirvarttate 		bdag po'i 'bras bu ni de dag nyid du so so dang mthun pa'i phyi'i dngos po phun sum tshogs pa'o /
dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyis ni bde 'gro dang ngan 'gror skye ba 'phen pa dang yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i las su rig par bya'o /
'phen pa ni gang gis rnam par smin pa 'phen pa'o /
taccākṣepakeṇa karmaṇā paripūrakeṇa ca karmaṇā yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ni gang gis skyes pa na 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa myong ba'o /
ākṣepakaṃ karma katamat /
yena phala vipāko 'bhinirvarttate 		las gcig gis lus gcig 'phen par byed pa'i las kyang yod /
las gcig gis lus du ma 'phen par byed pa'i las kyang yod /
paripūrakaṃ karma katamat las du mas lus gcig 'phen pa'i las kyang yod /
yenopapanna iṣṭāniṣṭaphalaṃ vedayate las du mas lus du ma 'phen pa'i las kyang yod do /
yena ekena karmaṇā ekamātmabhavanākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā ekamātmabhāvamākṣipati vā anekena karmaṇā anekamātmabhāvamākṣipati vā /
ekaḥ sattvo 'nekena karmaṇā samanvāgataḥ 		las mang po dang po dang ldan pa'i sems can ji ltar rim gyis rnam par smin pa myong bar 'gyur zhe na /
de la gang shin tu lci bar gyur pa de thog mar rnam par smin par 'gyur ro /
tatra vipākaphalavedanāyāḥ kaḥ kramaḥ yang na 'chi ba'i dus na gang mngon du gyur pa'o /
kāye yad audārikaṃ pūrvaṃ pacyate cyutikāle pratyupasthitaṃ vā pūrvaṃ bahulīkāratāṃ gataṃ vā atrasamācaritaṃ vā /
tadvipākaḥ pūrvaṃ pacyate /
yaduktaṃ sūtre trividhaṃ karma puṇyakarma apuṇya karma āniṃjyakarma ca /
puṇyakarma katamat 		yang na gang goms par gyur pa'o /
yang na gang thog mar spyad pa de thog ma nyid du rnam par smin par 'gyur ro /
bsod nams kyi las dang bsod nams ma yin pa'i las dang mi g yo ba'i las zhes gang 'byung ba la /
bsod nams gang zhe na /
kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ kuśalaṃ karma gang 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'o /
apuṇyakarma katamat /
akuśalaṃ karma 		bsod nams ma yin pa gang zhe na /
gang mi dge ba'o /
āniṃjyakarma katamat mi g yo ba'i las gang zhe na /
rūpārūpyapratisaṃyuktaṃ kuśalaṃ karma gang gzugs dang gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'o /
yaduktaṃ sūtre avidyālambanāḥ saṃskārāḥ puṇyāniṃjyā apuṇyāniṃjyāśceti ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'i 'du byed rnams so zhes gang gsungs pa de la /
katame puṇyāniṃjyā avidyālambanāḥ saṃskārā utpadyante /
dvividhaḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ 		ji ltar na bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi g yo ba'i 'du byed rnams ma rig pa'i rkyen las byung ba yin zhe na /
rmongs pa ni gnyis te /
