gnas ni 'dun pa'o /
'bad pa ni brtson 'grus so /
śamathagragrahopekṣānimittamanasikāreṣu chandaṃ janayati layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇe vīryamārabhate evaṃ tadanantaraṃ cittaṃ pragṛṇhāti pradadhātīpratyucyate /
bhāvanā phalaṃ katamat /
aśeṣavipakṣahāniḥ pratipakṣapratilambhaḥ pratipakṣavṛddhiśca 		zhi gnas dang rab tu 'dzin pa dang btang snyoms kyi mtshan ma yid la byed pa la brtson 'grus rtsom mo /
bying ba dang; rgod pa sel ba yang brtson 'grus nyid de /
'di ltar de'i 'og tu sems rab tu 'dzin pa dang rab tu 'jog pa smos so /
'bras bu gang zhe na /
mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma lus par nyams pa dang gnyen po thob pa dang 'phel ba'o /
taducyate bhāvanāphalam /
caturṛddhipādānāmālambanaṃ katamat /
niṣpajñena samādhinā yatkaraṇīyaṃ kṛtyam /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ 		rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
ting nge 'dzin gyis grub pa'i bya ba'o /
ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
samādhiḥ /
sahāyaḥ katamaḥ /
chandovīryaṃ cittaṃ mīmāṃsā tatsaṃprayuktāśca cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ 		ting nge 'dzin to /
grogs gang zhe na /
'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
chandasamādhiḥ katamaḥ /
yatsatkṛtya prayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām 		'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
gang gus par sbyor ba la brten nas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
vīryasamadhiḥ katamaḥ brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
yatsātatya prayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām gang rgyun du sbyor ba la brten nas /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
cittasamādhiḥ katamaḥ /
pūrvasamādhibhāvanāmāgamya svarasena spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām 		sems kyi ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
gang sngon ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pa la brten nas /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ katamaḥ dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
deśanādharmaśravaṇamāgamya pratyātmaṃ pratisaṃkhyāya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām gang gzhan gyis bstan nas chos rab tu rnams par 'byed pa la brten nas /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
punaḥ chandasamādhiḥ yat chandaṃ janayan spṛśati cittasyaikagratām yang 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang 'dun pa bskyed pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
vīryasamādhiḥ yat vīryamārapramāṇaḥ spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang 'bad cing brtson 'grus rtsom pa na /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
cittasamādhiḥ yat cittaṃ pradadhat spṛśati cittasyaigratām sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang sems rab tu 'jog pa na /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ yat cittaṃ pragṛṇhan spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām /
bhāvanā katamā 		dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang sems rab tu 'dzin pa na /
sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
bsgom pa gang zhe na /
aṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāmabhyāsaḥ spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad goms par byed pa ste /
katame aṣṭau /
chandaḥ vyāyāmaḥ śraddhā praśrabdhiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyaṃ cetanā upekṣā ca 		spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad ni /
'dun pa dang rtsol ba dang dad pa dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang dran pa dang shes bzhin dang sems pa dang btang snyoms so /
te punaraṣṭau samāsataścaturdhā saṃgṛhyante 'di dag brgyad yin du zin kyang bzhir 'gyur te /
vyāyasāyikaḥ anugrāhakaḥ aupanivandhikaḥ prātipakṣikaśca 'bad pa dang phan 'dogs pa dang nye bar 'dogs pa dang gnyen po'o /
chandavīryacittamīmāṃsābhāvanā punardvividhā /
nidānaṃ saṃkṣepavikṣepa parivarjanabhāvana alīnatvāvikṣepatadubhayāśrayānukūlabhāvanā ca 		yang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa rnams kyi sdud pa dang g yeng ba gzhi dang bcas par yongs su spangs pa dang zhum pa med pa dang g yeng ba med pa dang de gnyi ga'i gnas dang mthun pa bsgom mo /
phalaṃ katamat 'bras bu gang zhe na /
kuśalasamādhiparikarmataḥ yathākarmaṃ dharmābhijñā yathācittamabhijñāpradarśanam /
api ca teṣu teṣu dharmeṣu adhigamaḥ prātiḥ karmaṇyatā vaśitā kāritraṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nānāvidhānāmṛdudhyādīnāṃ vastūnāṃ niṣpādanamadhiguṇānāṃ nirhāraśca /
pañcendriyāṇāmālambanaṃ katamat 		de ltar ting nge 'dzin legs par yongs su spyang ba byas na /
chos mngon par shes par bya ba gang dang gang mngon du bya bar 'dod pa de dang de la sems mngon par gtod pa de rang rang gi gnas kyi chos rnams la mngon du 'gyur ba'i skal ba can du 'gyur ro /
dbang po rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
catvāryāryasatyāni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams so /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ /
śraddhā vīrya smṛtiḥ samādhiḥ prajñā ca /
sahāya katamaḥ /
tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikā dharmāḥ /
bhāvanā katamā 		ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab po /
grogs gang zhe na /
de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
bsgom pa gang zhe na /
yat śraddhendriyeṇa satyeṣu abhisaṃpratyayasamutthānaṃ prayogabhāvanā dad pa'i dbang po ni bden pa rnams la mngon par yid ches pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
vīryendriyeṇa satyeṣu utpannābhisaṃpratyayasyābhisaṃbodhyarthaṃ vyāyāmasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā mngon par yid ches pa skyes pa ni bden pa mngon par rtogs par bya ba'i phyir spro ba'i tshul gyis brtson 'grus bsgom par 'gyur ro /
smṛtīndriyeṇa satyeṣu ārabdhavīryasya smṛtisaṃprayogā dharmasaṃmopasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni bden pa rnams la nye bar gnas pa'i dran pa mi brjed pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
samādhīndriyeṇa satyeṣu saṃprayukta smṛteḥ cittaikāgratāsamutthānaprayogabhāvanā bden pa rnams la dran pa nye ba gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni sems rtse gcig pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
prajñendriyeṇa satyeṣu samāhitacittasya pravicayasamutthānaprayogabhāvanā /
bhāvanāphalaṃ katamat /
satyābhisamayasamutthānataḥ uṣmagatamūrdhaparikarmataśca kṣāntilaukikāgradharmanirhāraḥ 		bden pa rnams la mnyam par gzhag pa'i shes rab ni rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'i tshul gyis bsgom par 'gyur ro /
'bras bu gang zhe na /
bden pa myur du mngon par rtogs par byed pa dang dro bar gyur pa dang rtse mo dang bzod pa dang chos kyi mchog rnams bsgrub pa'o /
yathā pañcendriyāṇi tathā pañca balāni /
eṣāṃ viśeṣaḥ taiḥ vipakṣāntarāyanirllekho 'navamudyateti balānītyucyante 		dbang po rnams la ji lta bar stobs rnams la yang de bzhin no; /
'di ni bye brag yin te /
mi mthun pa'i phyogs nges par bsrabs pas /
mi brdzi ba'i phyir stobs rnams so /
sapta bodhyaṅgānāmālambanaṃ katamat byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ yathābhūtatā 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag gi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
smṛtiḥ dharmavicayaḥ vīryaṃ prītiḥ praśrabdhiḥ samādhiḥ upekṣā ca /
smṛtiḥ saṃniśrayāṅgam 		dran pa dang chos rnam par 'byed pa dang brtson 'grus dang dga' ba dang shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms so /
dran pa ni gnas kyi yan lag go /
dharmavicayaḥ svabhāvāṅgam chos rnam par 'byed pa ni ngo bo nyid kyi yan lag go /
vīryaṃ niryāṇāṅgam /
prītiḥ anuśaṃsāṅgam 		brtson 'grus ni nges par 'byung ba'i yan lag go /
dga' ba ni phan yon gyi yan lag go /
praśrabdhiḥ /
samādhiḥ upekṣā cāsaṃkleśāṅgam /
asaṃkleśataḥ asaṃkleśāśrayataḥ asaṃkleśasvabhāvataśca /
sahāyaḥ katamaḥ /
tatsaṃprayuktāśrittacaitasikā dharmāḥ /
bhāvanā katamā 		shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i yan lag ste /
gang gis kyang kun nas nyin mongs par mi 'gyur ba dang gang du yang kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ba dang kun nas nyin mongs pa gang yang med pa'o /
grogs gang zhe na /
de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
bsgom pa gang zhe na /
vivekaniśritaṃ virāganiśritaṃ nirodhaniśritaṃ vyavasargapariṇataṃ smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgam dran pa yang dag byung chub kyi yan lag /
dben pa la gnas pa /
'dod chags dang bral ba la gnas pa /
'gog pa la gnas pa /
rnam par spong bas yongs su bsgyur ba bsgom pa'o /
yathā smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgaṃ tathā yāvat upekṣāsaṃbodhyaṅgam dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag ji lta bar btang snyoms yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag gi bar du yang de bzhin no /
ebhiḥ catubhiḥ padairyathākramaṃ catuḥsatyālambanābodhyaṅgabhāvanā paridīpitā /
bhāvanāphalaṃ katamat 		'dis ni bden pa la dmigs pa byang chub kyi yan lag bsgom pa yongs su bstan to /
'bras bu gang zhe na /
darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇam /
aṣṭānāmāryamārgāṅgānāmālambanaṃ katamat 		mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa'o /
lam gyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
taduttarakālaṃ caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ yathābhūtatā de'i 'og tu 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams kyi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba'o /
svabhāvaḥ katamaḥ /
samyagdṛṣṭiḥ samyakkarmmāntaḥ samyagājīvaḥ samyagvyāyāmaḥ samyaksmṛtiḥ samyaksamādhiśca /
samyagadṛṣṭiuḥ paricchedāṅgam /
samyaksaṃkalpa parasaṃprāpaṇāṅgam 		ngo bo nyid gang zhe na /
yan lag brgyad de /
yang dag pa'i lta ba dang yang dag pa'i rtog pa dang yang dag pa'i ngag dang yang dag pa'i las kyi mtha' dang yang dag pa'i 'tsho ba dang yang dag pa'i rtsol ba dang yang dag pa'i dran pa dang yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin to /
yang dag pa'i lta ba ni yongs su gcod pa'i yan lag go /
yang dag pa'i rtog pa ni gzhan go bar byed pa'i yan lag go /
samyagvākkarmāntājīvāḥ parasaṃpratyapāṅgam /
darśanaśīlājīvaviśuddhitāmupādāya 		yang dag pa'i ngag dang las kyi mtha' dang 'tsho ba ni gzhan yid ches par byed pa'i yan lag ste /
lta ba dang tshul khrims dang 'tsho ba rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro /
samyagvyāyāmaḥ kleśāvaraṇaviśodhanāṅgam /
samyaksamādhiḥ vaiśeṣikaguṇāvaraṇa viśodhanāṅgam /
sahāyaḥ katamaḥ /
tatsaṃprayuktāścittacaitasikādharmāḥ /
bhāvanā katamā /
bhāvanā tu bodhyaṅgavat /
bhāvanā phalaṃ katamat 		yang dag pa'i rtsol ba ni nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i yan lag go /
yang dag pa'i dran pa ni nye ba'i nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par spyod pa'i yan lag go /
yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni yon tan khyad par can la sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i yan lag go /
grogs gang zhe na /
de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
bsgom pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag bzhin no /
'bras bu gang zhe na /
paricchedaḥ parasaṃprāpaṇaṃ parasaṃpratyayaḥ kleśāvaraṇaviśodhanamupakleśāvaraṇaviśodhanaṃ vaiśeṣikaguṇāvaraṇaviśodhanaṃ ca yongs su gcod pa dang gzhan go bar byed pa dang; gzhan yid ches par byed pa dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa dang yon tan khyad par can la sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'o /
catasraḥ pratipadaḥ katamāḥ /
duḥkhā pratipad dhandhābhijñā duḥkhā pratipat kṣiprābhijñā sukhā pratipad dhandhābhijñā sukhā pratipat kṣiprābhijñā 		lam bzhi gang zhe na /
mngon par shes pa bul la dka' ba dang mngon par shes pa myur la dka' ba dang mngon par shes pa bul la sla ba dang mngon par shes pa myur la sla ba ste /
prathamā mṛdvindriyāṇāmanupalabdhamauladhyānam dang po ni dbang po rtul po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan ma thob pa'i'o /
dvitīyā tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmanupalabdhamauladhyānam gnyis pa ni dbang po rnon po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan ma thob pa'i'o /
tṛtīyā mṛdvindriyāṇāmupalabhamauladhyānam gsum pa ni dbang po rtul po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan thob pa'i'o /
caturthī tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmupalabdhamaula dhyānam /
catvāri dharmapadāni katamāni 		bzhi pa ni dbang po rnon po dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan thob pa'i'o /
chos kyi gnas bzhi gang zhe na /
alobhādveṣāṇāṃ samyak smṛtiḥ samyak samādhiḥ /
alobhādveṣāṇāmadhiśīlaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ /
samyaksmṛtānāmadhicittaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ /
samyaksamādhitānāmadhiprajñaśikṣāviśuddhiḥ 		brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa dang yang dag pa'i dran pa dang yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin te /
brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa ni lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rnams par sbyong ba'o /
yang dag pa'i dran pa ni lhag pa'i sems so /
yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni lhag pa'i shes rab bo /
śamathaḥ katamaḥ zhi gnas gang zhe na /
adhyātmaṃ cittasya upanibandhaḥ sthāpanā saṃsthāpanā avasthāpanā upasthāpanā damanaṃ śamanaṃ vyupaśamanam ekotīkaraṇaṃ samādhānaṃ ca /
vipaśyanā katamā 		'di lta ste /
nang nyid la sems 'jog pa dang rgyun du 'jog pa dang blan te 'jog pa dang nye bar 'jog pa dang 'dul bar byed pa dang zhi bar byed pa dang rnam par zhi bar byed pa dang rtse gcig tu byed pa dang mnyam par 'jog pa'o /
lhag mthong gang zhe na /
'di lta ste /
yā dharmān vicinoti pravivinoti parivitarkkayati parimīmāṃsamāpataye /
ca kāma pratipakṣadauṣṭhulyanimittasaṃyojanataḥ kāmābhibhavānāṃ viparyāsataḥ aviparyastacittasyāvasthāpanataśca /
api khalu śamathavipaśyanāmāgamya catvāro mārgāḥ 		chos rnams la rnam par 'byed pa dang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa dang yongs su rnam par rtog pa dang yongs su dpyod par byed pa ste /
gnas ngan len dang mtshan ma'i gnyen po nyid dang phyin ci log las 'byin pa dang phyin ci log ma yin pa la sems 'jog pa'i phyir ro /
yang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong la brten nas lam bzhir 'gyur te /
ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī na vipaśyanāyāḥ /
tatprakāraṃ śamathaṃ niśritya vipaśyanāmāpanā 		la la ni zhi gnas thob pa yin gyi /
lhag mthong ni ma thob pa ste /
de zhi gnas la brten nas lhag mthong la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ vipaśyanāyā lābhī na śamathasya /
tatprakārāṃ vipaśyanā niśritya śamathabhāvanā 		la la ni lhag mthong thob pa yin gyi zhi gnas ni ma thob pa ste /
de lhag mthong la brten nas zhi gnas la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ na śamathasya lābhī nāpi vipaśyanāyāḥ la la ni zhi gnas kyang thob pa ma yin la lhag mthong yang thob pa ma yin te /
tatsaṃbaddhacittasya layau ddhatyāpakarṣaṇād yugapadubhayamārga bhāvanā de chos la rgod pa mngon par tshar bcad pa'i sems kyis gnyi ga la brtson par byed do /
ekatyaḥ śamathasya lābhī vipaśyanāyāśca la la ni zhi gnas dang lhag mthong yan thob pa yin te /
tasya śamathavipaśyanobhayamārga yuktasya samaṃ yugapat pravṛttiḥ de zhi gnas dang lhag mthong yang 'dres par gyur nas mnyam par zung du 'jug go /
trīṇīndriyāṇi dbang po ni gsum ste /
ajñātamājñāsyāmīndriyam ājñendriyam ājñātāvīndriyaṃ ca mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa dang kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po'o /
ajñātamājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ katamat mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
prayogamārge pañcadaśasu ca darśanamārgacittakṣaṇeṣu yadindriyam sbyor ba'i lam dang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bco lnga la gang dbang byed pa'o /
ājñendriyaṃ katamat kun shes pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
ṣoḍaśāt darśanamārgacittakṣaṇādrūdhvaṃ sarvasmin śaikṣamārge yadindriyam mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa la brten nas slob pa'i lam thams cad la gang dbang byed pa'o /
ājñātāvīndriyaṃ katamat kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po gang zhe na /
aśaikṣamārgeyadindriyam mi slob pa'i lam la gang dbang byed pa'o /
prathamadhyānabhūmikānāṃ bhāvanāmārge kāmāvacarāṇi kuśalamūlakānyapi bhāvanāṃ gacchanti bsam gtan dang po'i sa pa'i lam bsgom pa na 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bsgom par 'gyur te /
teṣu vibhutvalābhataḥ /
yathā prathamadhyānabhūmikānāṃ kāmāvacarāṇi kuśalamūlakāni bhāvanāṃ gacchanti tathā sarvepāmūrdvabhūmikānāṃ bhāvanāmārge adhobhūmikāni kuśalamūlakāni bhāvanāṃ gacchanti 		de dag la dbang 'byor ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
bsam gtan dang po'i sa pa na 'dod pa na spyod pa rnams la ji lta ba de bzhin du sa gong ma ba'i lam thams cad bsgom pa na /
sa 'og ma ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bsgom par 'gyur te /
teṣu vibhutvalābhataḥ /
niṣṭhāmārgaḥ katamaḥ 		de dag la dbang 'byor ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
vajropamaḥ samadhiḥ mthar phyin pa'i lam gang zhe na /
sarvadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratipraśrabdheḥ sarvasaṃyogānāṃ prahāṇāt sarvavisaṃyogānāmadhigamācca gnas ngan len thams cad rgyun gcod pa dang 'phrad pa'i 'thob pa rnams kyi rgyun chad pa dang bral ba'i 'thob pa rnams thob pa'i phyir /
tadanantaraṃ nirantarāśrayapravṛttiḥ prāptakṣayajñānam anutpādajñānaṃ daśāśaikṣā dharmāḥ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la brten nas de ma thag tu gnas ma lus par gyur te /
zad pa shes pa dang mi skye ba shes pa'o /
katame daśa /
aśaikṣasya samyagdṛṣṭiryāyada śaikṣasya samyaksamādhiḥ aśaikṣasya samyagvimokṣaḥ aśaikṣasya samyag jñānaṃ ca /
evamādayo dharmā niṣṭhāmārga ucyate 		mi slob pa'i chos bcu yang yin te /
mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba nas /
mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bar dang mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i rnam par grol ba dang mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i shes pa'o /
katamāni sarvadauṣṭhulyāni /
saṃ kṣepataścaturviśatiḥ /
tadyathā sarvatragamabhilāpadauṣṭhulyaṃ veditadauṣṭhulyaṃ kleśadauṣṭhulyaṃ karmadauṣṭhulyaṃ vipākadauṣṭhulyaṃ kleśāvaraṇādauṣṭhulyaṃ karmāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ vipākāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ nivaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ vitarkkadauṣṭhulyaṃ āhāradauṣṭhulyaṃ maithunadauṣṭhulyaṃ svapnadauṣṭhulyaṃ vyādhidauṣṭhulyaṃ jarādauṣṭhulyaṃ maraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ pariśramadauṣṭhulyaṃ dṛḍhadauṣṭhulyam audārikadauṣṭhulyaṃ madhyadauṣṭhulyaṃ sūkṣmadauṣṭhulyaṃ samāpattyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ jñeyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ ca 		gnas ngan len thams cad gang zhe na /
mngon par brjod pa'i gnas ngan len kun tu 'gro ba dang tshor ba'i gnas ngan len dang nyin mongs pa'i gnas ngan len dang las kyi gnas ngan len dang rnam par smin pa'i gnas ngan len dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas len dang las kyi sgrib pa'i gnas len dang rnam par smin pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas len dang grib pa'i gnas len dang rtog pa'i gnas len dang zas kyi gnas ngan len dang 'khrig pa'i gnas len dang rmi lam gyi gnas ngan len dang nad kyi gnas ngan len dang rga ba'i gnas ngan len dang 'chi ba'i gnas ngan len dang yongs su ngal ba'i gnas ngan len dang gnas ngan len brtan pa dang gnas ngan len chen po dang gnas ngan len 'bring po dang gnas ngan len chung ngu dang nyin mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len to /
saṃyogaḥ katamaḥ /
dauṣṭhulyāciteṣu saṃyogalābhateti vijñaptiḥ 		'phrad pa'i 'thob pa rnams gang zhe na /
gnas ngan len bsags pa la 'thob pas zhes gdags so /
visaṃyogaḥ katamaḥ /
dauṣṭhulyavikṣipteṣu visaṃyogalābhateti vijñaptiḥ /
vajropamaḥ samādhiḥ katamaḥ 		'bras ba'i 'thob pa rnams gang zhe na /
gnas ngan len zad pa la bral ba'i 'thob pa zhes gdags so /
rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na /
bhāvanāmārgagatasya taduttaraṃ saṃyojanaprahāṇamārgavasthāyāṃ yaḥ samādhiḥ prayogamārgasaṃgraho vā ānantaryamārgasaṃgraho vā /
prayogamārgasaṃgrahastu tataḥ paraṃ sarvairāvaraṇairacchādyaḥ sarvāvarāṇānāṃ ca bhedaka iti /
ānantaryamārgasaṃgrahastu yadanantaraṃ kṣayajñānānutpādajñānotpattiḥ 		sbyor ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa dang bar chad med pa'i lam gyis bsdus pa'o /
sbyor ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa ni gang phan chad sgrib pa thams cad kyis mi phyed cing /
sgrib pa thams cad ni shigs pa'o /
bar chad med pa'i lam gyis bsdus pa ni gang gi 'og tu zad par shes pa dang mi skye ba shes pa 'byung ba ste /
sa ca samādhiḥ nirantaraḥ dṛḍhaḥ ekarasaḥ vyāpī ca /
etadarthapratibimbanārthaṃ bhagavatoktaṃ tadyathā mahāśailaparvato 'khaṇḍo 'cchidro 'śuṣira ekaghanaḥ susaṃvṛtto daśadigvātākampyaśca 		ting nge 'dzin de yang bar med pa brtan pa /
sra ba /
ro gcig pa /
khyab pa'o /
'di la dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dper na /
brag chen po ma grub pa /
ser ka med pa /
khong stong ma yin pa /
gcig 'dus pa /
shin tu mkhregs pa de ni shar phyogs kyi rlung gis kyang mi sgul cing mi g yos so /
katamā nāma nirantarāśrayapravṛttiḥ shar phyogs ji lta bar phyogs thams cad kyang de bzhin no zhes gsungs so /
aśaikṣamārgalābhinaḥ trividhā āśrayapravṛttiḥ /
katamāstisraḥ /
cittāśrayamapravṛttiḥ māryāśrapapravṛttiḥ dauṣṭhulyāśrayapravṛttiśca 		gnas ma lus par gyur pa gang zhe na /
gang mi slob pa'i lam thob pa'i sems kyi gnas gyur pa dang lam gyi gnas gyur pa dang gnas ngan len gyi gnas gyur pa'o /
kṣayajñānaṃ katamat zad pa shes pa gang zhe na /
hetukṣayeṇa yad śānaṃ labhyate kṣayaviṣayā lambanaṃ vā rgyu zad nas shes pa gang yin pa'am /
zad pa la dmigs pa'o /
anutpādajñānaṃ katamat mi skye ba shes pa gang zhe na /
phalaprahāṇena yad jñānaṃ labhyate phalānutpattiviṣayālambanaṃ vā 'bras bu spangs nas shes pa gang yin pa'am /
'bras bu mi skye ba la dmigs pa'o /
daśāśaikṣā dharmāstu aśaikṣāṇāṃ śīlaskandhaṃ samādhiskandhaṃ prajñāskandhaṃ vimuktiskandhaṃ vimuktijñānadarśanaskandhaṃ cādhikṛtya veditavyāḥ mi slob pa'i chos bcu ni mi slob pa'i tshul khrims kyi phung po dang ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po dang shes rab kyi phung po dang rnam par grol ba'i phung po dang rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phung po'i dbang du byas par shes par bya'o /
tathā ca mārgasatyasya catvāraḥ prakārabhedāḥ /
mārgalakṣaṇaṃ nyāyalakṣaṇaṃ pratipadlakṣaṇaṃ nairyāṇikalakṣaṇaṃ ca /
kimupādāya mārgalakṣaṇam 		yang lam gyi bden pa'i rnam pa ni mtshan nyid bzhir rig par bya ste /
lam gyi mtshan nyid dang rigs pa'i mtshan nyid dang sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid dang nges par 'byin pa'i mtshan nyid do /
ci'i phyir lam gyi mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
tattvārthaparimārgaṇatāmupādāya /
kimupādāya nyāyalakṣaṇam /
kleśapratipakṣatāmupādāya 		de kho na'i don yongs su tshol ba'i phyir ro /
ci'i phyir rigs pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya pratipallakṣaṇam /
cittāviparyāsapratipādanātāmupādāya 		ci'i phyir sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
sems phyin ci ma log par sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
kimupādāya nairyāṇikalakṣaṇam ci'i phyir nges par 'byin pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya zhe na /
nityapadayānatāmupādāya rtag pa'i gnas su 'gro ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
satyeṣu ṣoḍaśākārāḥ laukikā lokottarāśca /
laukikānāṃ lokottarāṇāṃ ca katamaḥ prabhedaḥ /
jñeye akuśalapraveśakuśalyapraveśastrabhāvaprabhedataḥ sāvaraṇanirāvaraṇasvabhāvaprabhedataḥ savikalpanirvikalpasvabhāvaprabhedataśca /
kena hetunā satyeṣu anityaduḥkhādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa lauaukikākārāḥ 		bden pa rnams la rnam par bcu drug ni 'jig rten pa yang yod 'jig rten las 'das pa yang yod de /
'jig rten pa rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa dag byed brag ci yod ce na /
shes bya la legs par ma zhugs pa dang legs par zhugs pa dang sgrib pa dang bcas pa dang sgrib pa med pa dang; rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa dang rnam par rtog pa med pa'i phyir te /
tathāgata aprativedhataḥ kleśānuśayataḥ abhilāpamukhena prapañcanataśca /
lokottarākārāḥ tadviparyayeṇa /
lokottarākāreṣu varttamāno 'nityārthaṃ paśyati sākṣādanubhavati notvanityaṃ paśyati abhilāpaprapañcamukhena /
yathā anityākārā anityārthe evaṃ śiṣṭhākarāḥ śiṣṭārtheṣu yathāyogaṃ veditavyāḥ /
atha viniścaye dharmaparicchedo dvitīyo bhāgaḥ /
dharmaviniścayaḥ katamaḥ /
āryaśāsanaṃ dvādaśāṅgadharmaḥ /
katamāni dvādaśāṅgāni /
sūtraṃ geyaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ gāthā udānaṃ nidānam avadānam itivṛtakaṃ jātakaṃ vaipulyam adbhutadharmaḥ upadeśaśca 		'di ni bye brag go /
'di ltar 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam pa la 'jug pa na mi rtag pa'i don mthong gi mi rtag pa nyid ces bya bar mthong ba ni ma yin no /
mi rtag pa nyid kyi don la ji lta ba de bzhin du rnam pa lhag ma rnams la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
bden pa rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba ste /
kun las btus pa gnyis pa'o /
chos rnam par nges pa gang zhe na /
chos zhes bya ba ni mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde dang lung du bstan pa'i sde dang tshigs su bcad pa'i sde dang ched du brjod pa'i sde dang gleng gzhi'i sde dang rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde dang de lta bu byung ba'i sde dang skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde dang shin tu rgyas pa'i sde dang rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde dang gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde'o /
sūtraṃ katamat mdo'i sde gang zhe na /
yadabhipretārthaṃ sūcanākāreṇa gadyabhāṣitam gang smos pa'i tshul gyis rkyang par gsungs pa ste /
daśānuśaṃsān saṃpaśyan tathāgataḥ sūcanākāreṇa dharmaṃ deśayati sukhaṃ vyavasthāpayati sukhaṃ deśayati /
śrotāpi sukhamudgṛṇhāti dharmagauravatayā kṣipraṃ bodhi saṃbhārān paripūrayati āśudharmatāṃ pratividhyati /
buddhe 'vetyaprasādaṃ labhate dharme saṃghe cāvetya prasādaṃ labhate 		phan yon bcu gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa mdor smos pa'i tshul gyis chos ston te /
rnam par gzhag par sla ba dang bshad sla ba dang gzung sla ba dang chos la gus pas myur du tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang myur du chos nyid rtogs par 'gyur ba dang sangs rgyas la shes nas dad pa thob pa dang chos dang dge 'dun la shes nas dad pa thob pa dang mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'i mchog la reg pa dang 'brel ba'i gtam gyis gtan la 'bebs pas dam pa rnams kyi sems mgu bar byed de /
paramadṛṣṭadharmasukhavihāraṃ spṛśati mkhas pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ba'o /
sāṃkathyaviniścayena satāṃ cittamārādhayati dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde gang zhe na /
paṇḍitaḥ paṇḍita iti saṃkhyāṃ gacchati /
geyaṃ katamat 		mdo'i sde de nyid du dbus dang mtha' mar tshigs su bcad de dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'o /
sūtrāṇāṃ madhye vā ante vā gāthayā yad gīyate /
sūtreṣu anirūpito 'rtho vā yad vyākhyāyate /
ato geyamityucyate /
vyākaraṇaṃ katamat /
tat sthāneṣu samatikrāntānāmatītānāmārya śrāvakāṇāṃ prāptyutpattiprabhedavyākaraṇam /
api ca sūtreṣu nirūīpitārthasya sphuṭīkaraṇam /
vivṛtyābhisandhivyākaraṇāt /
gāthā katamā /
sūtreṣu pādayogena deśyate /
dvipadī tripadī catuṣpadī paṃcapadī ṣaṭpadī vā /
udānaṃ katamat 		yang drang ba'i don gyi mdo sde rtogs par byed pas dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'o /
lung du bstan pa'i sde gang zhe na /
gang las nyan thos 'das te shi ba'i 'dus byas pa dang 'byung ba lung ston pa'o /
yang nges ba'i don gyi mdo sde ni lung du bstan pa'i sde'o /
tshigs su bcad pa'i sde gang zhe na /
tshigs su sbyar nas gsungs pa ste /
de ni rtsa ba gnyis pa dang rtsa ba gsum pa dang rtsa ba bzhi pa dang rtsa ba lnga pa dang rtsa ba drug pa'o /
sūtreṣu kadācit tathāgatena āttamanaskena yadudāhṛtam /
nidānaṃ katamat /
pṛṣṭena yad bhāṣitam 		ched du brjod pa'i sde gang zhe na /
gang yin rangs nas brjod pa'o /
gleng gzhi'i sde gang zhe na /
sotpattikaṃ śikṣāprajñāptekaṃ vā /
ato 'pi nidānam 		gang gi ched du gsungs pa dang byung ba dang bcas pa'i bslab pa bcas pa gsungs pa'o /
avadānaṃ katamat /
sūtreṣu sadṛṣṭāntakaṃ bhāṣitam 		rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde gang zhe na /
dpe dang bcas par gsungs pa'o /
itivṛttakaṃ katamat de lta bu byung ba'i sde gang zhe na /
yadāryaśrāvakāṇāṃ pūrvalaukikaṃ vṛttaṃ deśayati /
jātakaṃ katamat 		gang sngon gyi sbyor ba dang ldan pa'o /
skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde gang zhe na /
yat bodhisattvacaritapiṭakasaṃprayuktaṃ vṛttaṃ deśayati /
vaipulyaṃ katamat 		gang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang ldan pa'o /
shin tu rgyas pa'i sde gang zhe na /
bodhisattvapiṭakasaṃprayuktaṃ bhāṣitam gang byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod dang ldan pa'o /
yaducyate vaipulyaṃ tad vaidalyamapyucyate vaitulyamapyucyate shin tu rgyas pa ji lta ba de bzhin du rnam par 'thag pa dang mtshungs bral yang de bzhin no /
kimarthaṃ vaipulyamucyate ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa zhes bya zhe na /
sarvasattvānāṃ hitasukhādhiṣṭhānataḥ udāragambhīradharmadeśanātaśca sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i gnas yin pa dang rgyas pa dang rgya che ba dang zab ba'i rnam par chos bstan pa'i phyir ro /
kimarthamucyate vaidalyam ci'i phyir rnam par 'thag pa zhes bya zhe na /
sarvāvaraṇavidalanataḥ sgrib pa thams cad rnam par 'thag pa'i phyir ro /
kimarthamucyate vaitulyam ci'i phyir mtshungs bral zhes bya zhe na /
upamānadharmāṇāṃ tulanābhāvataḥ mtshungs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
adbhutadharmaḥ katamaḥ rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde gang zhe na /
yatra śrāvakabodhisattvatathāgatānāṃ paramā dbhutāścaryadharmāṇāṃ deśanā /
upadeśaḥ katamaḥ 		gang las nyan thos dang byang chub sems dpa' dang sangs rgyas rnams kyi ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos bstan pa'o /
sarvagambhoragūḍha dharmalakṣaṇānāmaviparītaṃ vyākhyānam /
evaṃ sūtrādīni dvādaśāṅgānyāryaśāsanāni triṣu piṭakeṣu saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti /
katamāni trīṇi /
sūtrapiṭakaṃ vinayapiṭakam abhidharmapiṭakaṃ ca /
tāni punardvividhāni /
śrāvakapiṭakaṃ bodhisattvapiṭakaṃ ca /
sūtraṃ geyaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ gāthā udānaṃ caitāni pañca śrāvakāṇāṃ piṭakasya sūtrapiṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti /
nidānamavadānamitivṛttakaṃ jātakaṃ caitāni catvāri dvayoḥ piṭakayoḥ saparivāre vinayapiṭake saṃgṛhītāni bhavanti 		gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde gang zhe na /
gang du chos kyi mtshan nyid phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'o /
mdo'i sde la sogs pa 'di dag ni sde snod gsum du 'gyur te /
mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde dang lung du bstan pa'i sde dang tshigs su bcad pa'i sde dang ched du brjod pa'i sde gang yin pa 'di ni nyan thos kyi mdo sde'i sde snod do /
gleng gzhi'i sde dang rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde dang da lta bu byung ba'i sde dang skyes pa'i rabs kyi sde 'khor dang bcas pa 'di ni 'dul ba'i sde snod do /
vaipulyamadbhutadharmaśca ete dve bodhisattvapiṭakasya sūtrapiṭake saṃgṛhīte bhavataḥ shin tu rgyas pa'i sde dang rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi sde gang yin pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i mdo sde'i sde snod do /
upadeśa ekaḥ śrāvakabodhisattvapiṭakayoḥ abhidharmapiṭake saṃgṛhīto bhavati /
kimupādāya tathāgatasya piṭakatrayavyavasthānam 		gtan la dbab par bstan pa'i sde ni gnyi ga'i chos mngon pa'i sde snod do /
ci'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis sde snod gsum rnam par gzhag ce na /
vicikitsopakleśapratipakṣakā matāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam /
antadvayānuyogopakleśapratipakṣakāmatāmupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam /
svayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśagrahopakleśapratipakṣakāmatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam 		nye ba'i nyon mongs pa the tshom gyi gnyen po'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
nye ba'i nyon mongs pa mtha' gnyis dang ldan pa'i gnyen po'i phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
rang gi lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po'i phyir chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
punaḥ śikṣātrayavyutpattikāmatāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam /
adhiśīlādhicittaśikṣāniṣpādanakāmatāmupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam /
adhiprajñaśikṣāniṣpādanakāmatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam 		yang bslab pa gsum brjod pa'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
lhag pa'i tshul khrims dang lhag pa'i sems kyi bslab pa bsgrub pa'i phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
lhag pa'i shes rab kyi bslab pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
punaḥ samyag dharmārthavyutpattikāmatāmupādāya sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānam /
dharmārthasākṣātkriyāpadasthānaprabhāvitā mupādāya vinayapiṭakavyavasthānam /
jñānināṃ sāṃkathyaviniścayadharmasaṃbhogasukha vihārāśrayatāmupādāya abhidharmapiṭakavyavasthānam 		yang chos dang don brjod pa'i phyir mdo sde'i sde snod rnam pa ci'i phyir gzhag go /
chos dang don mngon du bya ba'i gzhi'i gnas kyi phyir 'dul ba'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
'bel ba'i gtam gyis gtan la 'bebs pas chos la rdzogs par longs spyod pas bde ba la reg par gnas par bya ba'i phyir /
sa eṣa piṭakatrayasaṃgṛhīto dharmaḥ kasya gocaraḥ chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag go /
chos 'di dag gang gi spyod yul yin zhe na /
śrutamaya cintāmayabhāvanāmayānāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ gocaraḥ thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba dang bsgoms pa las byung ba'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams kyi spyod yul lo /
yaduktaṃ sutre cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ sālambanāḥ sākāraḥ sāśrayāḥ sasaṃprayogāśca sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams ni dmigs pa dang bcas pa dang rnam pa dang bcas pa dang gnas dang bcas pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa zhes kyang bya'o /
teṣāmasmin dharme ālambanaṃ katamat chos kyi nang nas de dag gi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
sūtrādikam /
ākāraḥ katamaḥ 		mdo'i sde la sogs pa'o /
rnam pa gang zhe na /
skandhādayastatsaṃprayuktāścārthāḥ phung po la sogs pa dang ldan pa'i don rnams so /
āśrayaḥ katamaḥ /
paravijñaptiḥ smṛtirvāsanā ca 		gnas gang zhe na; gzhan las rnam par rig pa dang dran pa dang bag chags so /
saṃprayogaḥ katamaḥ mtshungs par ldan pa gang zhe na /
anyo 'nyasahāyabhāvena ālambane ākāraiḥ saṃpratipattiḥ gcig gi grogs gcig yin pa'i tshul gyis rnam pas dmigs pa yang dag par rtogs pa'o /
dharme ālambanaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ chos la dmigs pa'i rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na /
saṃkṣepeṇa caturvidhaḥ ākhyātaḥ /
vyāpyālambanaṃ caritaviśodhanālambanaṃ kauśalyālambanaṃ kleśaviśodhanālambanaṃ ca 		khyab pa'i dmigs pa dang spyod pa rnams par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa dang mkhas pa'i dmigs pa dang nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa'o /
vyāpyālambanaṃ punaścaturvidham /
savikalpapratibimbālambanaṃ nirvikalpaprativimbālambanaṃ vastuparyantālambanaṃ kāryapariniṣpattyālambanaṃ ca 		khyab pa'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs brnyan dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan dang dngos po'i mtha' dang dgos pa yongs su grub pa'o /
savikalpapratibimbālambanaṃ katamat /
adhimuktimanaskāreṇa yat śamathavipaśyanāviṣayālambanam 		rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs brnyan gang zhe na /
mos pa yid la byed pas gang zhe gnas dang lhag mthong gi dmigs pa'o /
nirvikalpaprativimbālambanaṃ katamat /
tattvamanaskāreṇa yat śamathavipaśyanāviṣayālambanam 		rnam par mi rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan gang zhe na /
de kho na yid la byed pas gang zhe gnas dang lhag mthong gi dmigs pa'o /
vastuparyantālambanaṃ katamat dngos po'i mtha' gang zhe na /
sarvadharmāṇāṃ kṣayabhāvikatā yathāvadbhāvikatā ca gang chos rnams kyi ji snyed yod pa dang ji lta ba bzhin du yod pa'o /
kṣayabhāvikatā katamā ji snyed yod pa ni /
skandhadhātvāyatanāni phung po dang khams dang; skye mched rnams so /
yathāvadbhāvikatā katamā ji lta ba bzhin du yod pa ni /
catvāri āryasatyāni ṣoḍaśākārāḥ tathatā sarve anityāḥ saṃskārāḥ sarve duḥkhā saṃskārāḥ sarve 'nātmāno dharmāḥ nirvāṇaṃ śāntaṃ śūnyamapraṇihitamanimittaṃ ca /

dgos pa yongs su grub pa gang zhe na /

brgyad do /

bhūyorāgacaritānāmaśubhaviṣayālambanam 'dod chags la spyod pa rnams kyi ni mi sdug pa'o /

bhūyomohacaritānāṃ nikāyapratyayatā pratītyasamutpādaviṣayālambanam gti mug la spyod pa rnams kyi ni rkyen 'di las byung ba rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'o /
madamānacaritānāṃ dhātuprabhedaviṣayālambanam nga rgyal la spyod pa rnams kyi ni khams rab tu dbye ba'o /

kauśalyālambanaṃ pañcavidham mkhas pa'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
skandhakauśalyaṃ dhātukauśalyam āyatanakauśalyaṃ pratītyuasamutpādakauśalyaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ ca /
sthānāsthānakauśalyena kamarthaṃ paśyati 		phung po la mkhas pa dang khams la mkhas pa dang skye mched la mkhas pa dang rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'o /
gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa ji ltar blta zhe na /
jñeye pratityasamutpādakauśalyaṃ paśyati /
sthānāsthānakauśalyapratītyasamutpādakauśalyayoḥ kaḥ prabhedaḥ 		rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa las blta'o /
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa bye brag ci yod ce na /
yat dharmā dharmānabhiniṣyandayanti nahyeṣāṃ nirhetuko nāpi viṣamahetuka utpāda itīdaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam /
hetuphalānurūpye vedayitotpāda itīdaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyam 		chos rnams las chos rnams mngon par 'byung ba'i phyir rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa'i rgyu yongs su spangs pas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mkhas pa'o /
rgyu dang mthun par 'bras bu 'byung ba yongs su gzung ba'i phyir gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'o /
kleśaviśodhanalambanaṃ katamat nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa gang zhe na /
yad adhobhūmikānāmaudarikatā ūrdhvabhūmikānāṃ śāntatā tathatā catvāryasatyāni ca sa 'og ma rnams kyi ni rags pa nyid do /

catasṛbhiryuktibhiḥ /
apekṣāyuktiḥ kāryakāraṇayuktiḥ upapattisādhanayuktiḥ dharmatāyuktiśca 		bzhis dpyod de /

apekṣāyuktiḥ katamā ltos pa'i rigs pa gang zhe na /
yā saṃskārāṇāmutpattau pratyayāpekṣā gang 'du byed rnams 'byung ba na rkyen la ltos pa'o /
kāryakāraṇayuktiḥ katamā bya ba byed pa'i rigs pa gang zhe na /
pṛthaglakṣaṇānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ kāryakāraṇāni gang rang gi mtshan nyid tha dad pa'i chos rnams so so rang gi bya ba byed pa'o /

upapattisādhanārthaṃ sādhyasyārthasya prāmāṇāviruddha upadeśaḥ /
dharmatāyuktiḥ katamā /
anādikālāt svalakṣaṇasāmānyalakṣaṇasthitadharmeṣu yā dharmatāpariniṣpattiḥ sā dharmatā 		gang bsgrub pa'i don tshad ma dang mi 'gal bar ston pa'o /

iti dharmeṣu vicāraṇā /
dharmeṣu katamāḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti 		chos la rigs pas dpyod pa la brtson pa'i kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
catasraḥ paryeṣaṇāḥ saṃbhavanti /
nāmaparyeṣaṇā vastuparyeṣaṇā svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā ca /
nāmaparyeṣaṇā katamā 		kun tu tshol ba bzhi ste /
ming kun tu tshol ba dang dngos po kun tu tshol ba dang ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba dang bye brag tu 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba'o /
ming kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
dharmeṣu nāmakāyapadakāyavyañjanakāyānāmapariniṣpannaṃ svalakṣaṇamiti yā santīraṇā /
vastuparyeṣaṇā katamā /
dharmāṇāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāmapariniṣpakṣaṃ khalakṣaṇamiti yā saṃtīraṇā /
svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā katamā /
dharmāṇā mabhidhānābhidheyasaṃbandhe svabhāvaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatāsantīraṇā /
viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā katamā /
dharmāṇāmabhidhānābhidheyasambandhe viśeṣaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatāsantīraṇā 		gang ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams kyi rang gi mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par rtog pa'o /
dngos po kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
gang de bzhin du phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyi mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par rtog pa'o /
ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
gang brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel pa la ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtog pa'o /
khyad par du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba gang zhe na /
gang brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel pa la khyad par du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtog pa'o /
iti dharmaparyeṣaṇābhāvanā /
dharmeṣu yathābhūtaparijñānāni katamāni saṃbhavanti 		chos kun tu tshol ba la brtson pa'i yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin tu yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
catvāri yathābhūtaparijñānāni /
nāmaparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ vastuparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ 		yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa bzhi ste /
ming tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa dang dngos po tshol bar rtogs pa dang ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa dang khyad par du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa'o /
nāmaparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat /
yathābhūtasya nāmānupalabdhijñānam 		ming tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
ming mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
vastuparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat dngos po tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /

svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat /
yathābhūtasya dravyasvabhāvānupalabdhijñānam 		ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
ngo bo nyid rdzas su mi dmigs par shes pa'o /
viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣitaṃ yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ katamat /

dharmamāśritya samādhiprayuktasya yogabhūmiḥ katamā jñeyā 		khyad par du 'dogs pa tshol bar rtogs pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gang zhe na /
bye brag rdzas su mi dmigs par shes pa'o /

pañcākārāḥ /
ādhāraḥ ādhānam ādarśaḥ ālokaḥ āśrayaśca 		de ni rnam pa lngar blta ste /
gzhi dang skyed pa dang me long lta bu dang snang ba dang gnas so /

grāhyagrāhakānupalabdhijñānam gzung ba dang 'dzin pa mi dmigs par shes pa'o /

sva niruktavyañjanajñatāmupādāya 		chos mngon pa dang 'dul ba mngon pa'i mtshan nyid shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
ji ltar na yi ge la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
nges pa'i tshig bzang po'i yi ge shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
kathaṃ niruktikuśalo bhavati ji ltar na nges pa'i tshig la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
ātmātmīyeti janapadaniruktimanabhiniviśyānuvyavahārajñatāmupādāya bdag go bdag go zhes yul mi'i nges pa'i tshig la mngon par ma zhen par rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
kathaṃ pūrvāntāparāntānusandhikuśalo bhavati ji ltar na sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mthar 'brel pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
pūrvānte udgrahaṇaṃ tāmaparānte niḥsaraṇaṃ tāmupādāya sngon gyi mthar gzung bas dang phyi ma'i mthar nges par 'byung bar bya ba shes pa nyid kyi phyir /
kathaṃ dharmeṣu dharmavihārī bhavati /
bhāvanāmanāgamya kevalaśrutacintāprayogeṇa na dharmavihārī bhavati 		ji ltar na chos rnams la chos la gnas pa nyid yin zhe na /
bsgom pa la ma brten par thos pa dang sems pa'i sbyor ba 'ba' zhig gis kyang chos la gnas pa ma yin la /
śrutacintāmanagamya kevalabhāvanāprayogeṇa na dharmavihārī bhavati zos pa dang sems pa la ma brten par bsgom pa la sbyor ba 'ba' zhig gis kyang chos la gnas pa ma yin gyi /
ubhayamāgamyobhayavihāreṇa dharmavihārī bhavati gnyi ga la brten te gnyi ga la gnas na /
chos la gnas pa yin no /
udgrahāya svādhyāyadeśanābhiḥ śrutamayaṃ draṣṭavyam 'dzin pa dang kha ton byed pa dang bshad pas thos pa las byung bar blta'o /
samadhiprayogāsantuṣṭibhyāṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ draṣṭavyam ting nge 'dzin la sbyor ba dang chog par mi 'dzin pas bsgoms pa las byung bar blta'o /
prayogaḥ sātatyasatkṛtyaprayogeṇāviparītaprayogeṇa ca draṣṭavyaḥ sbyor ba ni rgyun du chud pa dang gus par sbyor ba dang ma log par sbyor bar blta'o /
asantuṣṭiranāsvāditottaśamayaprayogeṇa draṣṭavyā chog par mi 'dzin pa ni ro mi myang ba dang gong du zhig gnas la sbyor bar blta'o /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ pāramitāpiṭakamucyate /
pāramitānāṃ saṃkhyānirddeśatāmupādāya lakṣaṇanirddeśatāmupādāya kramanirdeśatāmupādāya niruktinirdeśatāmupādāya bhāvanānirdeśatā mupādāya prabhedanirdeśatāmupādāya saṃgrahanirdeśatāmupādāya vipakṣanirdeśatāmupādaya guṇavarṇananirdeśatāmupādāya anyo 'nyaviniścayatāṃ copādāya 		ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sde snod ces bya zhe na /
der pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi grangs bstan pa dang mtshan nyid bstan pa dang go rims bstan pa dang nges pa'i tshig bstan pa dang bsgom pa bstan pa dang rab tu dbye ba bstan pa dang bsdus pa bstan pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs bstan pa dang yon tan gyi bsngags pa bstan pa dang gcig la gcig nges par bstan pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyaṃ audāryaṃ gāmbhīrya ca deśyate ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la rgya che ba dang zab par bstan ce na /
sarvākārajñatāma udāragambhīratāmupādaya rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rgya che ba dang zab pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā audāryagāmbhīryaṃ nādhimucyante uttrasanti /
dharmatāviyuktatāmupādāya anavaropitakuśalamūlatāmupādāya pāpamitraparigrahatāṃ copādāya 		ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa la sems can kha cig rgya che ba dang zab par mi mos shing skrag par 'gyur zhe na /
chos nyid dang bral ba dang dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa dang sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs su zin pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena vaipulye ekatyāḥ sattvā adhimucyante ci'i phyir shun tu rgyas pa la sems can kha cig mos kyang nges par 'byung bar mi 'gyur zhe na /
adhimucyamānā api na niryānti /
svayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśa sthāpitayā 		bdag nyid lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa la gnas pa dang don la sgra ji bzhin du mngon par zhen pa'i phyir ro /
'di la dgongs nas /
idaṃ ca sandhāyoktaṃ bhagavatā mahādharmādarśe dharmaparyāye bodhisattvasya yathāruta mayoniśo dharmānvicinvataḥ aṣṭāviṃśatirasadṛṣṭaya utpadyante bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi me log chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs las gsungs pa /
byang chub sems dpa' sgra ji bzhin du tshul bzhin ma yin par chos rnam par 'byed pa la /
aṣṭāviṃśatirasadṛṣṭayaḥ katamāḥ /
nimittadṛṣṭiḥ prajñaptyapavādadṛṣṭiḥ parikalpāpavādadṛṣṭiḥ tattvāpavādadṛṣṭiḥ parigrahadṛṣṭiḥ pariṇatidṛṣṭiḥ anavadyatādṛṣṭiḥ niḥsaraṇadṛṣṭiḥ avajñādṛṣṭiḥ prakopadṛṣṭiḥ viparītadṛṣṭiḥ prasavadṛṣṭiḥ anabhyupagamadṛṣṭiḥ kusṛtidṛṣṭiḥ satkāradṛṣṭi dṛḍhamūḍhatādṛṣṭiḥ mūladṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭāvadṛṣṭadṛṣṭiḥ prayoganirākaraṇadṛṣṭiḥ anairyāṇikadṛṣṭiḥ āvaraṇopacayadṛṣṭiḥ apuṇyaprasavadṛṣṭiḥ vaiphalyadṛṣṭiḥ nigrāhyadṛṣṭiḥ abhyākhyānadṛṣṭiḥ akathyadṛṣṭiḥ mahādṛṣṭiḥ abhimānadṛṣṭiśca 		lta ba ngan pa nyi shu rtsa brgyad 'byung ste /
lta ba ngan pa nyid shu rtsa brgyad bo dag gang zhe na /
mtshan mar lta ba dang btags pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang kun tu rtog pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang de kho na la skur ba 'debs pa'i lta ba dang yongs su 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang bsgyur ba'i lta ba dang kha na ma tho ba med par lta ba dang nges par 'byung bar lta ba dang dpa' za ba'i lta ba dang rab tu 'khrug pa'i lta ba dang phyin ci log tu lta ba dang 'phel ba'i lta ba dang khas mi len pa'i lta ba dang ngan g yo'i lta ba dang bkur sti'i lta ba dang rmongs pa brten pa'i lta ba dang rtsa ba'i lta ba dang lta ba la lta ba ma yin par lta ba dang sbyor ba sel ba'i lta ba dang nges par 'byin pa ma yin par lta ba dang /
sgrib pa sogs pa'i lta ba dang bsod nams ma yin pa 'phel ba'i lta ba dang 'bras bu med pa'i lta ba dang chad pas bcas pa'i lta ba dang skur ba 'debs pa'i lta ba dang bsnyad pa ma yin pa'i lta ba dang lta ba chen po dang mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyi lta ba'o; /
yaduktaṃ vaipulye niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā iti /

nirvedhabhāgīyeṣu pañcadaśasu darśanamārgacittakṣaṇeṣu yaḥ pudgalaḥ gang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa la mthong ba'i lam gyis sems kyi skad cig bcom ldan la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
strota āpakṣaḥ katamaḥ rgyun tu zhugs pa gang zhe na /
ṣoḍaśe darśanamārgacittakṣaṇe yaḥpudgalaḥ gang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa la gnas pa'i gang zag go /
darśanamārgaḥ satyakatvaniyāmāvakrāntiḥ mthong ba'i lam ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur ba la zhugs pa ste /
dharmābhi[samaye]pi saḥ chos mngon par rtogs pa yang de yin no /
kāmeṣvavītarāgaḥ pudgalaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāman strotaāpanno bhavati 'dod pa rnams las 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i gang zag ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas /
rgyun tu zhugs par 'gyur ro /
yadbhūyo vītarāgaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāman sakṛdāgāmī bhavati phal cher la 'dod chags dang bral ba ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas lan cig phyir 'ong bar 'gyur ro /
kāmebhyo vītarāgaḥ samyaktvaniyāmamavakrāmannanāgāmī bhavati 'dod pa rnams las 'dod chags dang bral ba ni yang dag pa nyid du nges par gyur pa la zhugs nas phyir mi 'ong bar 'gyur ro /
yadā darśana prahātavyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇāt [stota ā]panno bhavati /

ūrddvā parityāgakāraṇatāṃ copādāya 		ci'i phyir gong ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba rnam pa lnga spangs pas dgra bcom pa zhes bya zhe na /
gtso bo bsdu ba'i phyir ro /

gong ma nye bar len pa'i rgyu yin pa dang gong ma yongs su mi gtong ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
saptakṛdbhavaraparamaḥ katamaḥ re ltar thogs na srid pa lan bdun pa gang zhe na /
strotaāpanna eva pudgalaḥ saptakṛtvo 'pi miśromiśra devamanuṣyeṣu bhavāt saṃsṛtya yo duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti rgyun tu zhugs pa'i gang zag nyid lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du lan bdun yan man du srid par 'khor bar byas nas gang sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
kulaṃkulaḥ katamaḥ rigs nas rigs su skye ba gang zhe na /
deveṣu vā kulātkulaṃ gatvā [manuṣye]ṣu vā yo duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti lha dang mi rnams kyi nang du rigs nas rigs su song na gang sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma tho ba pa'o /
ekavīcikaḥ katamaḥ bar chad gcig pa gang zhe na /

antarāparinirvāyī katamaḥ /
upapattisaṃyojane prahīṇe abhinivṛttisaṃyojane aprahīṇe antarābhavamabhinirvarttayanneva yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti abhinivṛtto vā antarābhave upapattibhavagamanāya cetayannevayo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti 		bar mdor yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na /
skye ba'i kun tu sbyor ba ni spangs la mngon par 'grub pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni ma spangs pa ste /
bar ma dor srid pa mngon par 'grub pa na /

abhisaṃcetayitvā vā upapattibhavamabhisaṃprasthitaḥ [bhavānu]papatticchandaṃ yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti /
upapadyaparinirvāyī katamaḥ /
ubhayasaṃyojane aprahīṇe rūpadhātāvupapannamātra eva yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti 		skye ba'i srid pa ni ma thob pa na gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
skyes nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na /
gnyi gar kun tu sbyor ba ma spangs la gzugs kyi khams su skyes pa tsam nyid kyis gang lam mngon du byas nas sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
anabhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī katamaḥ mngon par 'du byed pa med par yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na /

abhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī katamaḥ /
upapanno 'bhisaṃskāreṇa yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti 		mngon par 'du byed pa dang bcas pa'i yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba gang zhe na /
gang skyes nas mngon par 'du byed pas lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
ūrdhvaṃstrotāḥ katamaḥ gong du 'pho ba gang zhe na /
upapanno rūpāvacarāṇāṃ bhūmau bhūmau yāvadakaniṣṭhagān praviśya tannānāsrava mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti gang gzugs kyi khams su sa nas sar skye zhing 'ong min gyi bar du zhugs nas /
der lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
puna kaścid yāvad bhavāgragān mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtya duḥkhasyāntamanuprāpnoti /
api ca vyavakīrṇabhāvitasya caturthasya dhyānasya pañcaprakārā prabhedāḥ /
mṛduparibhāvitaṃ madhyaparibhāvitamadhimātraparibhāvitamadhimātrādhimātrāparibhāvitamadhyādhimātraparibhāvitaṃ ca 		la la ni srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du song nas lam mngon du byas te sdug bsngal gyi mtha' ma thob pa'o /
spel mar bsgoms pa ni bsam gtan bzhi pa la chung ngu yongs su bsgoms pa dang 'bring du yongs su bsgoms pa dang cher yongs su bsgoms pa dang ches char yongs su bsgoms pa dang shin tu ches cher yongs su bsgoms pas gnas gtsang ma rnams su skye'o /
taiḥ vyavakīrṇābhāvitasya caturthadhyānasya pañcaprabhedaiḥ yathākramaṃ paścasu śuddhāvāseṣūpapattiḥ /
parihāṇadharmā arhan katamaḥ 		yongs su nyams pa'i chos can gyi dgra bcom pa gang zhe na /

gsod kyang rung /
mi gsod kyang rung ste /
mṛdvindriyaprakṛtiko vikṣipto vā avikṣipto vā cetayitvā vā acetayitvā vā dṛṣṭadharmasukha vihārāt parihāṇameti gang mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams pa'i skal pa can yin no /
bdag gsod pa'i chos can gang zhe na /
dbang po rtul po nyid myos kyang rung /
cetanādharmā arhan katamaḥ ma myos kyang rung /
mi gsod na /

gsod na skal pa can ma yin pa'o /

ma myos na skal ba can ma yin pa'o /
gnas pa las mi bskyod pa gang zhe na /

ma myos kyang rung /

rab tu rtogs pa'i 'os su 'gyur ba gang zhe na /

kāmāvacaraḥ pṛthagjanaḥ katamaḥ 'dod pa na spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo gang zhe na /

'dod pa na spyod pa'i mi slob pa gang zhe na /

yathā kāmāvacarāstrayaḥ tathā rūpāvacarā ārupyavacarā api 'dod pa na spyod pa'i gang zag gsum ji lta bar gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i gsum la yang de bzhin du blta'o /

gzugs kyi khams su skye ba'i gang zag go /

dvayoḥ phalayo strotāpattiphalārhattvaphalayoḥ prajñāpyate 'di ni rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu dang; 'bras bu gnyis la gdags so /

dharmābhisamayaḥ arthābhisamayaḥ tattvābhisamayaḥ pṛṣṭhābhisamayaḥ ratnābhisamayaḥ asamudācārābhisamayaḥ niṣṭhābhisamayaḥ śrāvakābhisamayaḥ pratyekabuddhābhisamayaḥ bodhisattvābhisamayaśca 		smon lam gyi dbang gis 'dod pa'i khams nyid du skye ste /
